## Page 6

Preface & Introduction

Salutations to Lord Ganesa, the Remover of Obstacles; to Goddess Saraswathi, the all-pervading
Mother of Learning, and to Nava Grahas, the destiny-makers of the Universe. After bringing out
Essentials of Predictive Hindu Astrology last year, I am happy to be amidst my readers with Book 1 of
Deva Keralam with English translation, notes etc.

Some have just heard the name of this work, Deva Keralam. Some have seen the Sanskrit
manuscript. Yet, almost every student of astrology has been keen to possess an English translation of
this work since decades. And, now, here is an occasion for all of us to actually enjoy the instructions
of Achyuta, the author of Deva Keralam.

The name itself suggests that the work belongs to Kerala, in the south of India, which is a
treasure-house of original astrological manuscripts like Jatakadesa Marga, Krishneeyam and Prasna
Marga. Each work from Kerala is a magnum opus, unto itself.

Deva Keralam has over 8200 slokas in all. Its author Achyuta had unfortunately left no clues
about his lineage, place of origin, time period etc. Lack of such information does not affect the
greatness of the work adversely. The name however suggests that it hails from Kerala.

_ The author obviously was a man of letters in astrology and had mastered various Nadi Granthas.
He specialized in use of Nadiamsa apart from employing Parasarian principles. He had consulted, in
compiling the present work, several Nadi Granthas including Surya Nadi, Chandra Nadi, Kuja Nadi,
Budha Nadi, Guru Nadi, Sukra Nadi, Sani Nadi, Lagna Nadi, Lagnadhipathi Nadi, Sarva Nadi and
Yoga Nadi.

He had also quoted Garga, Vasishta, Parasara, Yavana etc. As far as I know, thc. Nadis are not
available in any form nowadays. These Nadis, unlike Saptahrshi Nadi, apparently contained principles
usable in predictive astrology and not full-fledged horoscopes. The readers may be aware, Saptharshi
Nadi contains horoscopes discussing various aspects of natives, but far less instructive principles. The
average reader can hardly know of the basis of such conclusions without the help of an experienced
tutor. However, in case of the Nadi texts consulted by our author, those apparently fulfilled, inter alia,
the sole purpose of laying down rules for exhaustive interpretation of events of numerous kinds mainly
from one starting point - Nadiamsa.

Other stages of instructions contain predicting without the help of Nadiamsa, i.e. with the help
of special planetary combinations, positions, Ashtaka Varga, Dasa periods and the like as is normal
for any standard work we follow.

What is a Nadiamsa is:. :sessary to be explained to the reader. Most of us are us are aware of
Shodasa Vargas, the Parasarian division of a sign or Rasi into sixteen different parts of different lengths
of longitudes. What is less commonly known or employed is Nadiamsa, the 150th part of a Rasi, or one
fifth of a degree. That way, the entire space of 360 deg of the zodiac is divided into 1800 Nadiamsas.

In Table 1, in the immediately ensuing pages, I have enlisted the order and names of Nadiamsas,
as collected from the present work (the relevant original slokas appear much later in our work) and
from late C.G. Rajan of Madras, a known authority on Nadi astrology in particular. Late Rajan’s list
## Page 7

is hence taken with a specific purpose of textual utility on some occasions. And in Table 2, the
commencing and ending spaces of these 150 Nadiamsas are given.

In giving notes, I have followed the Nadiamsa divisions as shown in column 5 of Table 1. The
reader may use alternative spaces according to his choice and experience if he feels he can obtain
better effects of the text. .

As could be observed, the order and names of these Nadiamsas are identical for all the four
movable signs in a specified manner. Immovable signs again have a common pattern for themselves,
but different from those followed by movable and common signs. The same is the case among the four
common signs, i.e. these have an exclusive arrangement for themselves.

For example whatever applies in this classification and identity to Aries applies equally to Cancer,
Libra and Capricorn; whatever applies to Taurus applies to Leo, Scorpio and Aquarius; and lastly
whatever applies to Gemini applies to Virgo, Sagittarius and Pisces.

The Nadiamsa count is different for movable, immovable and common signs as could be witnessed
in Table 1. In movable signs, the count is in regular order from 1 to 150 (as shown in col 1).

For an immovable sign, the count is reverse, ie. from 150 to 1 (i.e. 150, 149, 148, 147, 146, ete...
as shown in col.2).

For common signs the count is firstly from 76 to 150 and then from 1 to 75 (as shown in col.3).

Keeping the list for movable sign as basis. Col. 4 gives the names of these segments as per C.G.
Rajan while col. 5 gives what is at one stage followed by our present work. Table 1 will of course make
the whole thing very clear.

Now if you observe the list, Vasudha Nadiamsa is the Ist of a movable sign, the 150th of an
immovable (or fixed) sign and the 76th of a common (or dual) sign. Vaishnavi Nadiamsa is the 2nd of
a movable sign, the 149th of an immovable sign and the 77th of a common sign. Braahmi is the 3rd of
a movable sign, the 148th of an immovable sign and the 78th of a common sign. The concerned segments
should be selected from Table 2.

Details about all the names and positions of Nadiamsas can be well understood from Table 1.

Table 2 is an easy one and can be used to know the serial number of Nadiamsa when the actual
longitude is selected following which the exact name of Nadiamsa should be referred to in Table 1.

For example there is a planet or the ascendant cusp in one of the movable signs (Aries, Cancer
Libra, Capricorn) at 10 deg 52’ of arc. That is 55th Nadiamsa which is Seethala Nadiamsa (as per col
1, Table 1). The same longitude in an immovable sign (Taurus, Leo, Scorpio, Aquarius) causes
Apavargaa Nadiamsa (as per col. 2 of Table 1). Again in a common sign (Gemini, Virgo, Sagittarius,
Pisces) the relevant Nadiamsa is Raudri (as per col. 3 of Table 1). We should do well to remember that
the first Nadiamsa in a movable sign is Parameswari Nadiamsa, and in a common sign it is Mahamaaya
Nadiamsa.

For ascendant, its cusp should be used to find out its Nadiamsa position, and for the planets the
usual longitudes we obtain from the ephemeris.

In many cases, the text divides the Nadiamsa in four parts called Vipra, Kshatriya, Vaisya and
Soodra Kalas. Vipra denotes a Brahmin, Kshatriya a ruler, Vaisya a trader and Soodra the fourth caste
as per Vedic divisions. Kala means time. Simply these are quarters 1 to 4 (each of 3’ longitude) of a
given Nadiamsa and are superior or inferior in that order for certain purposes. In other words they
‘lo not always indicate the birth in a certain caste as prevailing in olden days. These are actually meant
for attainment of perfection in prediction. Needless to mention, this kind of division makes the whole

Vi
## Page 8

zodiac into 7200 equal minor segments, each of 3’ arc (total 21600’ accounting for 360deg) - 1800 each
of Vipra, Kshatriya, Vaisya and Soodra Kalas, the use of which can hardly allow accuracy to escape
from the hands of a master astrologer.

The reader going through the pages will find the extent of changes in events each quarter (viz.
Vipra etc.) of a Nadiamsa can introduce. In the same Nadiamsa, for example Vipra Kala gives certain
result while another of the 3 parts gives completely different results.

Another division made of this Nadiamsa is first half and second half making the whole zodiac in
3600 parts. That is of 6° longitude. Here again the effects are absolutely in mutual variance.

On quite limited occasions, we find that a Nadiamsa is made into six parts attributing to Garga’s
authority. Meseems, this division is however questionable and must have been wrongly attributed to
the said sage.

True, exact degree of ascendant in terms of degrees and minutes of arc is very essential to use
some of the instructions contained hereof. Then without that, there can be no real astrology. Astrology
of approximation can only be disastrous. To use the principles containing Nadiamsas, the astrologer
must also obtain excellence in standard methods of rectification, prenatal epoch theory and through
Horary methods. Once that is done, with known events the correct Nadiamsa can be located.

For an established astrologer, Ayanamsa or precession is not an unsettled issue. Let me however
state for the benefit of the new reader that Lahiri’s Chaitrapaksha Ayanamsa is the accurate one when
the horoscope is cast using the exact coordinates at every point.

Not just for Nadiamsa, accuracy of Ayanamsa is a must even in other cases, like Navamsa,
Sapthamsa and Shashtiamsa. To wit, ifa planet, say Saturn is in Aries 19deg 59’ as per Lahiri ayanamsa,
another ayanamsa even with a small difference of minus 2’ of arc can place Saturn somewhat ahead
and give it Libra Navamsa instead of Virgo navamsa due to Lahiri. Saturn even in Aries Rasi with
Libra Navamsa protects one from heart ailments, gives him longevity and helps him progress in his
calling. The same Saturn with Aries sign position but in Virgo Navasma makes him wholly unreliable,
and makes him a victim of some sort of diseases of hand and legs. This difference could be easily located
by an experienced astrologer. Same is the case with other divisions including Nadiamsa.

All the rules given in this book do not, as could be seen, always revolve around Nadiamsa. And
each Nadiamsa in each sign is of course not given in the context of delineation. Select Nadiamsas are
given and they can be easily applied to the same kind of sign - movable, immovable or common, thus
multiplying their use four - fold. Sometimes the reader should be careful for they are just for a given
sign only.

Some Nadiamsas appear with synonym though not in that name. Some have not been enlisted in
both the lists of the text in which case, I have to the possible extent supplied suitable alternatives. These
may or may not be acceptable to the reader.

There are umpteen rules given by the text without ever considering Nadiamsa division. Such
rules, which can be rarely found in other sources than the present text, could be of exemplary use. For
an easy understanding several groups of slokas have been given suitable captions and any reader can
understand where a Nadiamsa features, and where it does not.

The beauty of the text lies in the fact that based on one planetary hint, many of the native’s relatives
have been exhaustively discussed.

The original suffers from certain defects. In some cases, the Sanskrit heading denoting a certain
Nadiamsa and ascendant clashes with the actual text thereof. The reader better follow the body text

Vii
## Page 9

for details. In some cases, copying errors, hopeless interpolations etc. are there, particularly in terms
of transit, using meaninglessly words like "Sphuta Yoga" even though only one planet features. In
some cases, the expression "Sukhi" is used denoting happiness although the effects are not always so.
Such misnomers including some corrupt words have been as far as possible, if not invariably but
carefully, omitted in translation to protect to the reader from being misguided. This mention is not
belittle the author, but with an understanding mind of the limitations of the copyist.

The Contents pages given before the commencement of the text, for understandable reasons, is
only brief as it is bound to be. For in each section, a number of items have been discussed and enlisting
them is only enlarging the volume.

I have in fact tried to give due exposure to the original’s true spirit and I believe I have succeeded
to a great extent in this direction.

I have left no stone unturned in fulfilling my task as the reader expects, having provided English
translations for rare standard works like Saravali (2 vols), Parasara Hora (vol 1 only), Suka Nadi, Hora
Sara etc... etc... Yet there ought to be some shortcoming out of my ignorance, what in Sanskrit, and
what in astrology. In such an event, I can only pray the reader’s broad-minded favour of forgiving me
on such count of failures.

I have however the happiness that I am the first person to have undertaken the task of rendering
these slokas in English and the reader is well aware that so far no language translation has been
provided for the present original text. The present issue, Book 1, contains 2718 slokas while Book 2
and Book 3 containing discussions on further Nadiamsas in many ascendants, and a number of general
rules independent of Nadiamsas, will soon follow to complete the work in question.

The text also excels in suggesting suitable remedies for many shortcomings in the lives of the native
and his relatives.

I am specially appreciative of the interest and enthusiasm shown by Mr. Narinder Kumar Sagar
in placing the present title before the readers.

I will feel greatly honoured if the reader finds something useful in my present efforts.

R. Santhanam,

Editor,

The Times Of Astrology,

9/1040 Govindpuri,

Kalkaji,

New Delhi 19 (India)
January 15, 1992 Telephone 6462777

1-2. Effects of Vasudhamsa: One born in
the first half of Maalini Amsa with Jupiter in
Kaala Koota Nadi Amsa with Maatanga Yoga
will have blood-red complexion and un auspi-
cious (i.e. or pleasing) appearance. If Jupiter is
exalted, simultancously occupying Pisces Navam-
Sa (i.e Jupiter in the last Navamsa of Cance1) and
is in the company of Venus, Maatanga Yoga is
formed. The Moon should further be in he: own
Rasi and Navamsa (for completion of Maatanga
Yoga).

Notes: According to the author, Maathanga
yoya is formed when Jupiter is in Cancer between
26 deg. 40’ and 30;. The positions of Venus and
Moon should also be in Cancer. The Moon
should additionally be in Cancer navamsa itself,
ie. be in Vargottama. For this Yoga, only ap-
pearance and comlexion are discussed in these
two slokas, while in slokas 5 etc. other effects for
whole of this Nadiamsa are discussed.

Malini Nadiamsa is not enlisted in the
present work, while the caption hereof inentions
‘Vasudha’. Vasudha Nadiamsa extends from 0
deg. 0’ to 0 deg. 12’ in a movable sign, 29 deg. 48”
to 30 deg. of an immovable sign, and 15 deg. to 15
deg. 12’ of a common sign.

Is the position of Malini identical with
Vasudha? Perhaps the compiler’s source con-
firmed this.

Jupiter’s position is fixed in Kalakoota
Nadiamsa which in Cancer extends from 0 deg.
36’ to 0 deg. 48’ which cannot allow simultancous-
ly last Navamsa of Cancer.

Apparently, the compiler made some er-
rois. It should be Jupiter in Kalakoota Nadiamsa,
or in last Navamsa of Cancer.

4-5, Maatanga Yoga’s effects: One born in
this Yoga with Maalini Amsa will have no full
brothers and sisters but will have step- brothers.
His father will have three spouses. The nutive’s
mother will be long-lived and her sister will be of
questionable character. The native’s mother will
be a chaste and devout wife and meritorious. She
will become emaciated due to family impedi-
ments ("Griha-chidrena”, thus losely transiated to
suit the context) She wil! have her husband
(i.c.the native’s father) long-living. She will come
to grief following her brother’s destruction.

Notes: The 9th lord, Jupiter, as counted
from the Moon sign joining both the Moon and
Venus denotes step-mother/s for the native.
Venus ruling the 4th from the Moon, joining
Jupiter and Moon, gives long life to mother.

6-7. The native’s father will be long-lived and
the mother will be grieved on account of destruc-
tion of her brother if Jupiter in the said Maatanga
Yoga is in Maatanga Nadiamsa. One of her sisters
val be long-lived while others will die premature-
y.

listed in the present work. _

8-131/2 The Matanga Yoga subject will
desire union with his spouse (i.e. he will not join
others). His spouse will become a widow due to
separation and will die. The native’s father will
die in (native’s) childhood or before native’s mar-
riage. If the Moon placed in Srikaara Nadi Amsa,
becomes the lord of the 4th, (or) occupying Scor-
pio/Capricorn Navamsa, and is aspected by the
9th lord (Jupiter), one born in Durbhaga Nadi
Amsa will have no brothers born after him. His
only sister will be long-lived. So also the mother.
If the Moon is in Durbhaga Nadiamsa, there will
be one sister who will be unfortunate. There will
be also destruction of step-brothers while father
will have two marriages. After the native attains
15th year of age, the father will become very
fortunate. He father) will tour many countries
for business in diamonds, grains, clothes etc. He
will live kv commercial activities, be an intellec-
tual and will have brothers and sisters.

Notes: Sloka 9 and others deal with Aries
ascendant in which the birth Nadiamsa should be
Durbhaga (from 7 deg. 12’ to 7 deg. 24’). Then
birth Navamsa falls in Gemini. Another space for
Durbhaga Nadiamsa in Aries is from 11 deg. 48’
to 12 deg. (Cancer Navamsa) The Moon should
be in aspect to 9th lord Jupiter. She should be in
Srikaara Nadiamsa (or) be in Scorpio or
Capricorn Navamsa. Then the native will have no
younger brother, but one younger sister who
along with mother will be long-lived.

Srikaara Nadiamsa is mentioned as
Karikaraa Nadiamsa lor the Moon to be in, (with
other conditions as per out text) by C.G. Rajan.
Karikaara Nadiamsa is from 6 deg. 24’ to 6 deg.
36° of a movable sign, 23 deg. 24 to 23 deg. 36’ of
an immovable Rasi and 21 deg. 24 to 21 deg. to
36’ of acommon sign. Hence Srikaara Nadiamsa
of our text is Karikaara Nadiamsa, as per Table of
Nadiamsas, supra.

Even though the 4th lord Moon is in debility
in Navamsa, or in the 8th in Capricorn in Navam-
sa, she will give a long lease of life to the mother,
because of Jupiter’s aspect. The aspect as a rule
should be seen in Rasi chart only. Not in Navam-
sa and other charts. For aspects emanate only by:
longitudinal distances.

Coborns come in the picture because the
Moon is a death-dealer, being lord of 2nd from
3rd.

The sister will be unfortunate if the said
Moon is in Durbhaga Nadiamsa. Durbhaga
means unfortunate. Instead of acquiring carly
death, she will live an unfortunate life. Durbhaga
Nadiamsa = 7 deg. 00’ to 7 deg. 12’ in a movable
Rasi, 22 deg 48’ to 23 deg. 00’ of an immovable
Rasi, and 2 deg. 00 to2 deg 12’ of a commun
Rasi. This position also causes loss of step-
brothers. This Nadiamsa repeats from 11 deg.
48’-12 deg. 0’ of a movable sign, from 18 dey, 0” -
18 deg. 12’ of an immovable sign and from 20 deg.
48’-27 deg. of a common sign.

14-16. Father’s destruction: Destruction of
father will result if Saturn occupies the degree
cause J by adding the longitudes of the Sun (Sura
= Su ) and the 4th lord. For one born in the first
half of Maalini Nadi Amsa with Mathanga Yoga,
the first sub-period of Janma Dasa (first Dasa)
will prove ominous for father bringing illness or
death.
## Page 28

Deva Keralam 3

Notes: Suramsa also means Sura Nadiamsa.

Seeing the words ‘7attrikonage’ in sloka 14,
‘Suramsage’ ibid is not translated as Sura
Nadiamsa while it could also mean so. Sura
means Sun and hence it denotes degree occupied
by the Sun at birth. This should be added to that
of the 4th lord.

As stressed by me often in my writings the
4th lord denotes father’s death while the Sth lord
denotes mother’s death. This technique is used
widely by many Nadi Granthas. In my own
studies, I did find these clues working quite effec-
tively.

Sloka 14 gives important clue about father’s
death. Saturn should not be in the degree arrived
at by adding the degree of the 4th lord (father’s
death-dealer) and of the Sun (signifying father).
If so, being a dire enemy of the Sun, and a planet
incharge of death, Saturn will cause early destruc-
tion of father.

From this, we can form another rule of our
own. The Sth lord rules mother’s death. The
Moon rules the mother. If Saturn occupics the
degree denoted by the degree arrived at by ad-
ding the longitudes of the Moon and Sth lord,
early loss of mother can be anticipated.

In the absence of Saturn being there, the
transits of malefics like Saturn/Rahu/Ketu/Mars
will cause some physical adversity to the parent
concerned. Not death always.

17-18. Dasa effects: In the first Dasa (Janma
Dasa), there will be some comforts and investi-
ture of sacred thread. In the sub- period of 10th
lord in the Vipat Dasa (third from birth) there will
be marriage or in the 22nd or 25th year? There
will be obstacles in childhood for one born in
Maatanga Yoga.

Notes: Terms like Janma Dasa occur often
in this work. These details could be found in the

following table:

Ist dasa : Janma dasa

2nd dasa : Sampath dasa

3rd dasa : Vipat Dasa

4th dasa : Kshema dasa

Sth-dasa : Prathyak dasa

6th dasa : Sadhaka dasa

7th dasa : Vadha (Nidhana) dasa
8th dasa : Maitra dasa

Oth dasa: : Parama Maitra dasa

A general yardstick is: odd dasas from birth
are inauspicious while even dasas are auspicious.

own/exaltation places. Results: Kingship, fame,
courage, happinesss and leadership. Also see

44, Danger to coborn: The native’s coborns

will be struck by destruction (or danger) when

Saturn reaches the Rasis, or trines of the under-

mentioned planets: (1) Navamsa dispositor of

11th lord.(2) Navamsa dispositor of 6th lord.

Notes: Navamsa dispositor is given high im-
portance in prediction by various Nadi texts.
Navamsa dispositor is the owner of the Navamsa
a planet is in. Example: Mercury is in Libra
Navamsa. Then his Navamsa dispositor is Venus.

The present sloka asks us to note the
Navamsa lords of the 11th lord and 6th lord.
Then we have to find out in which Rasi, such
dispositors are placed. Saturn coming over to
such Rasi/trine thereof will prove dangerous to
one’s brothers/sisters.

The 11th lord is understandable. Why the
6th lord comes in the picture can be understood
by some probe. The 6th is 8th from 11th.

in my view, this rule applies only to elder
coborn as the 11th, and the 8th from 11th feature.
To apply this to younger coborns one should be
somewhat careful. But the 11th lord has been
cited regarding younger coborn also.

47-48. Cancer Ascendant: When the Moon
is the lord of the ascendant, the sub-period of
Jupiter in the dasa of Mars will cause extreme
difficulties, untimely death, evils to one’s own
people, and destruction of female children. In the
absence of these, financial destruction will take
place in the end of the dasa (of Mars).

Notes: These two slokas relate to Cancer
ascendant, as the Moon is required to rule the
## Page 32

Deva Keralam

ascendant. The dasa of Mars (lord of Sth and
10th) and the sub period of Jupiter (ruling 6th and
9th) is quite destructive for the native in the form
of loss of daughters, many difficulties to the native
and his kinsmen. He may also have fear of un-
timely death because the combination of Mars -
Jupiter does not seem to be a good augury in
general.

Also make a note of Jupiter’s period being
evil for one born with Cancer Navamsa, in Aries
ascendant. This need not be straightaway applied
to birth in any of the other eight Navamsas of
Aries ascendant.

49-50. Aries Ascendant: For one born in
Aries ascendant in Cancer Navamsa, the dasa of
Mars will give happiness. Rahu dasa will beget
him favours or kindness (from others), and will
cause busy activities on account of marriage of a
son. Sixty-third year, in Jupiter’s interval (i.e.
dasa) will bring effects of untimely death to a
Maalini Nadiamsa native for which remedies may
be resorted to.

Notes: These effects be attributed to rising
Navamsa being Cancer, for a native of Aries as-
cendant. The dasas of Mars and Rahu will be
then favourable while Jupiter’s dasa, or 63rd year
will cause fear of untimely end of the native. By
conducting suitable remedy like Mrityunjaya
Japa/Homa, the native of Cancer Navamsa as
above shall overcome the fear.

54-55. Abala Nadiamsa - Firsthalf: One
born in this part will be a Brahmin, be happy, be
dark in complexion and lean in composition. He
will be fond of his older brother. He will in his
childhood be gentle and have an emaciated physi-
que. Due to the good offices of his brother-in-law
he will migrate to a foreign place and will beget
prosperity.

Notes: Slokas 54 to 93 deal with an immov-
able ascendant including Taurus. The reader will
suitably according to context understand these.

Abala Nadiamsa is also known as Prabha
Nadiamsa according to late C.G. Rajan.
## Page 33

\ Chandra Kala Nadi

This Nadiamsa in an immovable Rasi ex-
tends from 26 deg. 48’ to 27 deg. 00’ of urc. And
can cover even the 9th Navamsa Virgo according
to a given case. In case of movable sign. this
Nadiamsa extends from 3 deg. to3 deg. 12’ andin
a common sign from 18 deg. to 18 dey. 12’ of
space.

The first half of this Nadiamsa in this case is
26 deg. 48’ to 26 deg. 54 of arc, again with a
possibility of attaining cither Leo Navamsa or
Virgo Navamsa.

The effects given in the current slokas are
for just birth in first half of Abala Nadiamsa,
without reference to positions of any planets.

56. Coborns: Mars in ascendant (which is an
immovable sign) while Jupiter is in the 5th house
will deprive the native of after- borns. Even if
there be such a birth, only death (of alter-born)
will result.

Notes: Immovable signs are Taurus, Leo,
Scorpio and Aquarius. For Taurus and Aquarius
ascendants, this rule can be safely applied as
neither Mars nor Jupiter will be in own sign. In
case of Leo, Jupiter in 5th will be in Sagittarius,
and in case of Scorpio both Mars and Jupiter will
be in own signs (Scorpio and Pisces respectively).
Hence, for Leo ascendant and Scorpio ascen-
dant, this rule should be used after a thorough
scrutiny, more so for Scorpio ascendant.

61-721/2. Taurus Ascendant: One born in
Taurus ascendant, with Aries Navamsa, will beget
prosperity in a pilgrim center. Gradually his
prosperity will increase in Andhra region. The
native born in the 2nd one-third of former half of
Abala Nadiamsa will lose his father in childhood.
For Abala Nadiamsa native, the mother will be
long-lived, Saturn in the | 1th house along with the
Sun, for an Abala Nadiamsa native, will in Sam-
path (2nd) dasa cause evils to father and displace-
ment of the native from his birth-place. Malefic
bhuktis in the dasa of the planet owning the 8th
from the Moon will cause danger to both father
and mother. The Moon (Saturn according to
another text) in this Nadiamsa will give two wives
to the native. Yet some say there will be three
wives. The native with Moon (or Saturn) in Abala
Nadiamsa will be devoid of marital happiness. For
one born in the former half of Abala Nadiamsa,
Salurn aspecting the 12th house will give two
mariages While the first wife will suffer from
penury. The native ol former half of this Nadiam-
sa will have obstacles in getting progeny if the 5th
lord is with Rahu, while the 11th is tenented by
Saturn. One born in the 2nd half of this Nadiamsa
will greatly enjoy pleasures; his wife will give birth
to just one child and will later on become barren.
One will be totally childless if birth be in the
former half of Abala Nadiamsa. According to
some other authorities, such a native will beget a
child in his old age, alter a long interval. This will
be when Jupiter is in the 5th house in aspect to
two malefics. This childlessness for Abala
Nadiamsa native will be due to a curse of a Brah-
min in previous life. To ward off this evil, bathing
in Sethu (in the South) will bless the native with
the mercry of Lord Shiva (Nageswara also means
the Cobra King) and then children will be born.

Donations on Mondays, and worship in the morn-
ings be resorted to.

Notes: Aries Nuvamsa for Taurus ascendant
extends from 10 deg. to 13 deg. 20° (4th Navam-
sa).

That the native of Abala Nadiamsa will have
a long-living mother (irrespective of first/sccond
half) should be applied to only Taurus ascendant
and not the other three immovable ascendants, as
slokas 57 and 58 give a specific account o! parents’
lifespans.

Abala Nadiamsa will incur evils in the end of the
3rd Dasa, while one born in the first half (with
Moon in Vargothama) will have to leave his birth
country (in the end of the 3rd Dasa), and his
parents will die in a place different from birth
place. Relative results are detailed under Pras-
tarashtaka Varga (elsewhere),

88-92. Sixth Lord: For effects of Abala
Nadiamsa, other sources may also be consulted.
If the Moon is in Nirmala Nadiamsa as the 10th
lord is in his own Rasi/Navamsa, the native will
have knowledge of Vedanta (second and most
important part of Mimamsa or third of the three
great divisions of Hindu philosophy) and Tatwas
(24 in number) and will perform actions enjoined
by the Vedas. He will be ever-pious. He will be
pure, virtuous, eloquent in speech and will wor-
ship Lord Vishnu and Lord Siva. He wiil leave his
birth country in a revolution. He will incur danger
after his 10th year or 12th year. He will wander in
many coutries. Due to destruction of parents, he
will incur abundant grief. He will live in a town on
the banks of the Mahanadi. One born in Abala
Nadiamsa will enjoy yoga (i.e. effects due to for-
tunate birth), and will be quite happy. His fortune
will be on the increase in the beginning and end
of 3rd dasa.

Notes: From hereon, the relative slokas deal
with Aquarius ascendant, an immovable sign.
The Moon is the 6th lord who should be in Nir-
mala Nadiamsa. The lord of 10th Mars should be
in Aries or Scorpio, either in Rasi or in Navamsa.
Then the native will be skilful in Vedanta and the
like. Other effects may also be noted.

The beginning and concluding parts of 3rd
dasa causing prosperity suggests that the middle
portion will be adverse.

Maha Nadi can be interpreted to be the river
so named, or a great river like the Ganges or
Cauvery.

94-96. After the age of thirty he will attain
great prosperity, and happiness through royal
patronage. Due to Saturn’s adverse transis, his
enjoyments will be interrupted and he will be in
mental agony; when Saturn comes to the Navamsa
Rasi of the dispositor of 6th lord or its trine, much
grief will descend upon him. Remedies will re-
store happiness to him. In the Dasa of 4th lord, he
will gain much wealth. He will die in the Dasa of
the 8th lord. He will take to ascetic order follow-
ing a calamity in the family.

Notes: The 6th lord for Aquarius is the
Moon. If Saturn in transit comes to the Rasi
occupied by the Moon at birth, or alternatively
the Rasi represented by the Moon-occupied
Navamsa at birth, the subject will incur abundant
grief.

97-98. Jupiter in Scorpio, falling in Virgo
Navamsa as Mercury occupies the Navamsa of
Virgo/Pisces wil make one born in Vipra Kaala
wealthy right from birth. (But) the native if born
in Vaisya Kaala will be engaged in trading, in
Kshatriya Kaala be a king, and in Soodra Kaala
will take to such calling prescribed for his caste.

Note: There is no Agada Nadiamsa enlisted
in our test. Agada is Sukhada as per C.G.Rajan.
Thus it covers 20 deg. 36 to 20 deg. 48’ of a
movable sign, 9 deg. 12’ to9 deg. 24’ of an immov-
## Page 37

12 Chandra Kala Nadi

able sign and 5 deg. 36’ to 5 deg. 48’ of a common
sign. Although Viprakala etc. are mentioned in
these slokas, there is no reference to particular
Nadiamsa hereof. However, in sloka 108 infra, we
find Agada Nadiamsa which reference is carried
on, in the slokas ahead. Hence results from $.97
must belong to Agada Nadiamsa.

Vipra Kaala, Kshatriya Kaala, Vaisya Kaala
and Soodra Kaala in order are for 3’of arc of
ascendant, each in any Nadiamsa.

Nadiamsa extends from 21 deg. 00’ to 21 deg. 12’
of a movable sign, from 8 deg. 48 to 9 deg. 00” of
an immovable sign, or from 6 deg 0’ to 6 deg. 12’
of a common sign.

101-102. Jupiter in Scorpio: Jupiter in Scor-
pio, occupying Virgo Navamsa will make the na-

skilled in the expression or interpretation of in-
ternal sentiments by external gesture i.e. skilful in
understanding others’ minds, and be truthful.

He will excel in writing and studies (will be
a skilful writer endowed with great learning), will
be talkative and be intelligent.

Notes: For a birth in Aquarius ascendant,
Jupiter in the 10th house and attaining the
Navamsa position of Virgo causes excellence in
writing and other related activities. This can also
bless the subject with a high degrce of ancestral
inheritance, as Jupiter connected with 10th and
2nd occupies the 8th Navamsa Rasi.

115-118. The step-brother of the person
born in the former half of Agada Nadiamsa will
have no issues. Or they will be dead as they are
born, due to the (previous birth’s) sins of the said
relative. To overcome this evil, the step-brother
should bathe in the Setu, worhsip Lord Siva and
perform Shashti (the 6th lunar day of cither
fortnight) Vratha (for example fasting on these
days and observing religious rituals). Then he will
beget progeny. Other authorities quote Maharshi
Vyasa suggesting donation of the image of Lord
Krishna (by the’ said relative to overcome such
evils), The idol of Santhana Gopala (Krishna) be
also worshipped. Due to the blessings of
## Page 39

14

astrologers. birth of healthy and long-living
children will then be possible.

119-120. The ascendant of the step-brother
will be the Navamsa Rasi occupied by the 11th
lord, or one of its trines. Alternatively the Rasi
aspected by the 11th lord could also be such
ascendant. From the 9th house and its lord,
father’s ascendant be deduced. So also from the
Navamasa, or its trines, occupied by the Sun (at the
time of the native’s birth).

125-128, Father’s death: If Mars is placed in
the 5th house from the ascendant, as the 9th lord
is in the company of a malefic, the native’s father
will die in a foreign place. If the Sun is in Manjus-
wana Nadiamsa, the father’s death will be in a tiny
village, due to indigestion and loose motions. At
the time of death, the native will be by the side of
his father. For birth in Sun’s hora, if Mars joins
the solar ascendant (i.e. Mars and ihe Sun be
together) without beneficial aspect, father’s,
death will occur en route. If these planets occupy
benefic Navamsas, death will be instant, but if
these are in malefic’s navamsa, father will incur a
tragic end. At the time of father’s death, the
native’s mother will have gone out of the relevant
place.

Notes: These four verses describe place of
death of father. The death should not be inter-
preted to be untimely.

Mars and Sun joining in a hora ruled by the
Sun denotes tragic end for the father of Aquarius
native. Solar hora is the first 15 deg. of any odd
sign, viz. Aries, Gemini, Leo, Libra, Sagittarius
and Aquarius. For this, the two planets should
also be in a Navamsa ruled by a malefic.

130-131. About Mother: When the birth is in
the former half of Agada Nadiamsa, as the Moon
is positioned in Kutila Nadiamsa, following ef-
fects may be noticed. Sins will be galore in the
mother’s family. The mother of the native will be
fond of promoting quarrels. There will be many
troubles to the mother’s sister. The said maternal
aunt will be of questionable character and will
indulge in sinful acts.

Notes: Kutila Nadiamsa is: from 2 deg. 48’
to 3 deg. 0’ of a movable sign, from 27 deg. 0” to
27 deg. 12’ of an immovable sign, and from 17 deg.
48’ to 18 deg. 0’ of acommon sign. The Moon in
one of these threc position, while birth is in first
half of Agada Nadiamsa in Aquarius, the results
described in the slokas above will come to pass.

132-135. According to Chandra Nadi: The
Moon being the lord of the house signifying
maternal relatives (i.e. in 6th house, the ascendant
being Aquarius) if placed in Kutila Nadiamsa, in
aspect to Mercury gives a long lifespan to mater-
nal relatives. According to some authorities,
(early) destruction will take place. The mother of
such a native will be of questionable nature, and
will incur troubles on account of brotheis and be

emaciated. She will incur widowhood and also
enmity of step-children, during the native’s
childhood. She will beget auspicious effects fora
long time. (This part of the text is a corrupt
addition, considering other bad effects, par-
ticularly early widowhood.) The mother will,
however, be endowed with along lease of life. She
will beget happiness through her middle
daughter. These results are declared in Chandra
Nadi. Effects - good and bad - about mother and
maternal relatives have elaborately been dealt
with in Sukra Nadi,

Notes: In slokas 130 and 131, eviletfects are
described for the mother, maternal aunts etc. for
the Moon being in Kutila Nadiamsa. According
to the present slokas, Mercury (the significator of
maternal relatives) getting connected with the
Moon gives a long-life to maternal uncle. There
is another source to specify early end. Long life
to maternal relatives, as per Chandra Nadi is
apparently acceptable. This yoga is however ad-
verse for the mother.

139-142, Half sister: If the Moon be in Kutila
Nadiamsa, there is a possibility of having twin
half-sisters. The half sister will incur much grief
on account of destruction of her progeny. Her
husband will be pained by diseases and will be
bereft of coborn. The half sister will in her mid-
life be deprived of fortunes and will suffer penury.
Her husband will earn fume through royal service.
Their fortunes will recover after some interval.
They will prosper through children, when the
native will be in his 2nd dasa. The brother-in-law
in question will acquire men-borne conveyances,
fame and yoga effects (i.e. prosperity) and be

happy.

151-153 1/2 . Should the 7th lord be in Man-
juswana Nadiamsa (instead of being in the 11th in
Navamsa, as the 11th lord is in Viswambhara
Nadiamsa, vide sloka 159 supra) there will be
relief from obstacles (like brothers being with
impure hearts) and the native’s step-brothers will
enjoy marital happiness etc. By the native’s obser-
vance of vows to the Sun-god, and bathing in the
‘sea on the day of Tula Sankranthi (the Sun’s entry
in sidereal Libra), hundred evils like the step-
brothers being impure-hearted etc. will be cured.
Following this, birth of children and happy family
life will result to step-brothers. If the remedies are
not done, penury will result.

Notes: The remedies suggested, viz. bathing
in the sea on the day of Sun’s entry in Libra and
daily worship of the Sun-God will help in a
general context to get relief from troubles with
step- brothers, father etc.

134-1571/2 . The Sun devoid of beneficial
aspect, in the Sth from 6th house along with Ketu
will be an obstacle for step-brother to beget
progeny. He will lose wealth on account of
Soodras and will later on be happy. When the
native is in his 8th/10th year of age, his father will
incur destruction (losses) on account of Soodras.
Afterwards he will obtain great happiness which
will lead to amiability with step brothers. Prior to
this, the native’s step-brother-in-law will enjoy
effects of good yoga (prosperity).

Note: The sequence of these hints can be
arranged thus to have a clear picture:

The Sun with Ketu in the 10th house without
a benefic’s aspect leads to the following:

1. Step-brother will have difficulties in
begetting progeny. He will initialy lose wealth on
account of Sudras and then will lead a happy life.

2. When the native will be 8 or 10 years of
age, financial losses to father will have to be
feared. After sometime he will have good terms
with children born to his other wife (than the
native’s mother) and be happy.

a few villages. He will excel in writing and studies.

163-1671/2 . The Moon in the 2nd house, in
Kutila Nadiamsa will make one fond of crooked

Chandra Kala Nadi

thoughts. The native will be talkative. He will
serve a king and become famous thereafter. The
Moon in the said position will cause infantile
mortality through small- pox. Once he survives he
will be fortunate. The planet Jupiter in Vis-
wambhara Nadiamsa in Sagittarius while the
Moon is in the 2nd house, makes the native ac-
quire conveyances after 20. After 16 he will be
somewhat famous. He will be highly intelligent
after 21 years of age. He will incur danger of
untimely death during 5th year, or in a junction
period of two Dasas (in childhood), or 12th year,
or 32nd year or the 16th year.

Notes: In Sloka 165, 'Jeeve Kendra Trikonage"
means Jupiter in an angle or trine. But this expres-
sion is out of place as the Moon is in the 2nd for
Aquarius. Hence Jupiter can be only in angle
from the Moon, but not in trine.

Kutila Nadiamsa in Pisces extends from 17
deg. 48’ to 18 deg. and the Moon therein, for an
Aquarius native, will be prone to cause Balarishta
and other effects as stated. Kutila means
crooked, and the Moon therein will cause
crooked thoughts.

when Saturn comes to one of the undermentioned
Rasis: (a) The Navamsa Rasi occupied by the 4th
lord at birth. (b) A trine thereof. (c) The Rasi
occupied by 4th lord at birth. (d)The Rasi
aspected by the 4th lord.

171-1731/2 . In Janma (first) Dasa, the
emperor will be destroyed. The emperor’s son
will become famous in the 10th year, or the 12th.
Later on happiness will come elsewhere. In first
Dasa and 3rd Dasa there will be drought. In the
3rd Dasa, with Saturn’s transit in Lagna, troubles
from enemies will occur, and in royal treasury,
some wealth will be lost.

Note: The above hints make no meaning for
an individual’s horoscope. There is apparently
some avoidable ix-up in transmission.

188-189. Varuna Nadiamsa - Coborn
destroyed: Should Jupiter be placed in Sagittarius
in the company of the Moon, and birth be in the
Nadiamsa entitled Varuna, in aspect to Mars, the
native’s coborn will die as they come in this world.
Such an event will occur during the last three
nights of the end of the first year of (brother’s)
birth.

Notes: Slokas from 188 to 224 deal with
Sagittarius ascendant. The relevant birth
Nadiamsa is entitled Varuna - extending from 7
deg. 48 to 8 deg. 0’ of Sagittarius. The
Nadiamsa’s correct name is Varuni, which ac-
cording to C.G. Rajan and Deva Keralam’s alter-
native Table (Vol. I of original text) is the 115th of
a movable sign, 36th of an immovable sign and
40th of a common sign. That is from 22 deg. 48”
to 23 deg. of a movable sign, from 7 deg. to7 deg.
12’ of an immovable sign and from 7 deg. 48’ to 8
deg. of a common sign.

201-203. A specific horoscope: Mars, the
Sun and Mercury in the 6th house, Saturn in the

dant, Venus with Ketu in the 4th, and Rahu in the
10 house: With this array of planets, the native will
be quite happy, and bea great man. His childhood
will be marked by difficulties. He will have limited
number of issues. His coborn will also similarly

wealth and be so prosperous like a king. After

increasing trends. His father will be happy.
During his 8th year, the native will sce his father

being in the 10th, the position of Ketu should be

Sloka 201-203

Let us study the astrological combinations
with the help of the future events suggested.

1. The native will become great (profes-
sionally, etc.) because of Jupiter being in Lagna
while Venus, the 11th lord aspects the 10th, from
his exaltation sign.

2, Childhood will be marked by difficulties
as the 8th lord is in Lagna.

3, Limited number of issues is because 5th
lord Mars joins Mercury in the 6th house.
Jupiter’s aspect on Sth is a saving grace.

4. Royal kind of wealth and prosperity will
occur to the native because of 2nd lord Saturn in
Moolatrikona Rasi, conjunction of lords of Sth
and 9th, Jupiter aspecting 5th and 9th, Rahu in
the 10th aspected by an exalted planet, Sth lord
Mars aspecting the Lagna-cum-4th lord Jupiter,
dispositor of 5th and 9th lords in exaltation, 2nd
lord aspecting the 5th and the 9th etc. etc.

224-225. Mangala Nadiamsa: One born in
this Nadiamsa, having Mars as the 7th lord will
obtain a spouse who will be blood-red in com-
plexion. Such a native will be happy following
marriage. There will be ever-lasting wealth apart
from acquisition of quadrupeds and grains, fol-
lowing marriage. The wealth and auspiciousness
of this native will be long-lasting.

Notes: Although Mars is required to be 7th
lord, this does not apply to Libra ascendant, as it
is not a fixed sign. The instructions here relate
only to Taurus ascendant.

In Taurus ascendant, Mangala Nadiamsa
should rise, according to the sloka. This Nadiam-
sa in Taurus ranges between 11 deg. 36’ and 11
deg. 48’ the Navamsa of which is Aries, ruled by
Mars. Mars should be in Manjuswana Nadiamsa
(sign not specified). The 7th house being that of
Mars and the Navamsa ascendant also being that
of Mars helps the native to have happy marriage
apart from enjoying firm wealth.

227. (During childhood, the native will, due
to separation from coborns, incur difficulties
galore). In the dasa of the 6th lord.... be in trinal
to the Rasi indicated by the 6th lord’s navamsa
position, or be in Navamsa ascendant, there will
be danger to maternal relatives.

Note: Here we need some clarifications.
Seeing the sequence after sloka 226, this sloka
does not seem to relate to Mars’ position in Man-
gala Nadiamsa. This apparently relates to
Varuna Nadiamsa. Actually Mangala Nadiamsa
slokas are wrongly appended hereof, while the
slokas otherwise deal with Varuna Nadiamsa.

Secondly sloka 227 has three lines, the first
line having been placed in brackets. This is a
misplaced line. In the 2nd line, the reference is to
some planet in trine to 6th lord’s Navamsa posi-
tion, or with reference to Lagna Navamsa (vide
3rd line). To which planet the reference is made,
is not understood. Hence these 3 - line sloka may
be treated as defective. Yet, rendering in English
has been made as above.

239. After 11/2 yoars of birth, the native of
second half of Prabha Nadiamsa will be happy.
His father will acquire great wealth in the con-
cluding portion of the 9th lord’s dasa.

Note: In the first line, the word "Saayaka"
denotes an arrow, which makes no sense for us
here. If the expression is "Saayanaabde", then its
meaning is: Sa + Ayana + Abde which means
“one year and a half". ( Add 6 months denoted by
one Ayana to one year, which is 11/2 years).

The second line refers to 9th lord’s dasa (i.e.
Sun’s dasa) being quite favourable in respect of
father’s prosperity.

240-241, Father: Jupiter in Sagittarius as-
cendant, Venus in the 4th house in the company
of lords of the 9th and 10th (i.e. the Sun and
Mercury), will provide the native’s father
numerous vehicles, and fame via royal service. He
will be endowed with coborns, be diseased and be
subjected to loss of older brother. He will have
three long-living brothers and one long-living
sister.

Sagittarius - Ascendant with Jupiter; Pisces
- Venus, Sun and Mercury. This partial horo-
scope throws up certain clues like father having
numerous conveyances (the Sun being 9th lord,
with exalted Venus), getting fame through as-
sociation with king and long-living coi »rn.

Father being subjected to diseases proves
that the 9th lord joining Mercury in debilitation is
not good for his wellbeing. Loss of father’s older
brother is due to 7th lord in debility with Karaka
for father, the Sun. The native’s 7th house
denotes his father’s older brother, being 11th
from the ninth.

tions are made in the original. The result of these
three conditions is mere fortune, while Chakra
Yoga alone can give the most excellent result of
emperorship for any Lagna.

For the information of the reader, Chakra
Yoga is formed thus: when the six alternative
houses from Lagna are occupied by the 7 planets
from the Sun to Saturn, this Yoga is formed. As a
result, the native will "become the most powerful
emperor at whose feet, the heads of many kings
will lay in honour”. In the face of this effect,
Chakra Yoga in the present sloka, with two other
conditions, giving mere fortunes is of doubtful
origin.

This anamoly is extended to Slokas 250 etc.
infra. In my opinion, without Chakra Yoga, these
verses be taken.

Kumara Nadiamsa is not found anywhere.
It is Kumari that is enlisted in our work which
extends from 21 deg. 12’ to 21 deg. 24’ of a mov-
able sign, from 8 deg. 36’ to 8 deg. 48’ of an
immovable sign and from 6 deg. 12’ to 6 deg. 24’
of a common sign.

245-2461/2. Effects for combinations in
sloka 244 - continued: The native’s father will also
incur a high degree of prosperity. The subject will
be happy after marriage. His childhood will also
give happiness. There will be less happiness in
boyhood while his youth will be fortunate. In his
third dasa, he will acquire wealth. Due to 8th
lord’s blemish, occasionally there will be worries
on account of father. Due to loss of the native’s
paternal grand-father, his father will incur grief.
He will be (generally) happy.

Notes: Blemish for 8th lordship is men-
tioned in the text, without mentioning the position
of the Moon, 8th lord for Sagittarius. Apparently
she should be related to the Sun, 9th lord, by
aspect or by conjunction, or in an angle or in a
trine from the Sun.

Thus we gather that the Moon is harmful to
Sagittarius native by virtue of her ownership of the
8th house, unless she is connected with Mars, the
Sth lord.

247-248. Obstacles: There will be twice
obstacles (of major order, causing significant
decline) in the first Dasa and the 9th lord’s Dasa
(ruled by the Sun), if Jupiter is in Kumara
Nadiamsa while the Sun is with Mercury.

Notes: "Jaddasayam" meaning in that Dasa
is redundant seeing a specific reference to the
Dasa of Janma Nakshatra and 9th lord’s Dasa.

The sloka apparently attributes decline of a
great order in these Dasas, not once, but twice.
Hence for Sagittarius Lagna, Jupiter in Kumara
Nadiamsa seems to be a blemish.

of the Moon could be in Lagna.

257-258 1/2. Dasa results: The Dasa of as-
cendant lord will give balanced results, both good
and bad. The sub period of Mercury (in the said
Dasa) will bring dangers which can be stalled by
remedies. He will face due death in the 8th lord’s
sub period, during Ascendant lord’s Dasa in case
of birth in Varuna Nadiamsa.

Notes: For birth in Varuna Nadiamsa, Sagit-
tarius ascendant, the dasa of Jupiter is said to give
such resuits which will be both good and bad, but
in equal measure. Mercury’s sub period (in
Jupiter’s dasa) being that of 7th lord (death-
dealer) will endanger the native. The Moon’s sub
period, coming much after that of Mercury will
unfailingly endanger the native. This applies only
to the specified Nadiamsa.

285. Loss of fortunes: For birth in Varuna
Nadiamsa, Saturn in transit in the Rasi denoted
by the natal Navamsa of the 2nd lord or its trine

himself transits such a Rasi or a trine thereof, the
native will have decline of fortunes. Similar use
of Saturn’s transit be made with reference to the
Rasi he occupies at birth.

298-299 1/2. Mother: There will be evils to
the mother of Varuna Nadiamsa native when
Saturn transits the Rasi identical with the Navam-
sa position of the 11th lord or its trine. Also when
Saturn comes to the sign that is aspected by the
11th lord. Diseases and physical danger to mother
will have to be feared in the concluding part of
Vipath (3rd) Dasa, or in the first sub-period of
Kshema (4th) Dasa.

Notes: Transit Saturn opposing natal Venus,
or moving in such a Rasi/trine equal to the
Navamsa occupied by Venus at birth endangers
the native’s mother. Apparently for Sagittarius
ascendant, Venus holds some clue about death of
mother. (So also the 5th lord Mars).

The 11th house playing a role in this regard
can be seen in the following slokas.

300-301 1/2. Parents: The 4th lord in Varuna
Nadiamsa while Saturn is placed at birth in Sagit-
tarius Rasi and Virgo Navamsa - in this case
predict mother’s death when Saturn in transit
comes to aspect the 11th house. Instead of Virgo
Navamsa, if Saturn is in Aries Navamsa, his move-
ments in Taurus will bring about father’s end. This
can as well occur in the 4th Dasa (Kshema). The
death of father may alternatively occur when
Saturn transits the Navamsa Rasi of the natal Sun
or its trine.

Notes: The 4th lord Jupiter in Varuna
Nadiamsa, while Saturn is in Sagittarius 16 deg.
40’ to 20 deg. (Virgo Navamsa), the aspect of
Saturn on the 11th (from Capricorn/Aries/Leo)
will endanger the mother. Instead if Saturn is
within 3 deg. 20° of Sagittarius (Aries Navamsa),
his transit in Taurus will endanger father.

303-304 1/2. In the Dasa of the 8th lord, or in

native’s father will face mental agony, and fear of

transit will get effects of great Raja yoga.

These two clues can be profitably used in case of
Sagittarius ascendant according to circumstan-
ces.

dangerous illness.

333-334 1/2. Physical Troubles: See if the
lord of the ascendant aspects and the 8th lord
joins (the said Deha/Jeeva Rasi ) and if so
declare physical troubles to the native on the
week-days indicated by the 6th/8th lords during
the setting periods of Mercury/Jupiter. Further,
difficulties to the native’s co-borns and relatives

Chandra Kala Nadi

be also foretold. These adverse results can occur
in evil months of every year (during the dasa
periods of Deha and Jeeva Rasis).

Notes: The 8th lord Moon should be in
either the Deha Rasi, or Jeeva Rasi, and aspected
by Jupiter, the lord of Sagittarius ascendant. The
setting periods of Jupiter/Mercury should come
in such intervals. (These setting periods because
of combustion in the Sun can be known from
standard ephemeris). The week-days that are
important in this context are Friday and Monday.

An important clue emerges from the present
discussion. The lord of 8th in Deha Rasi or Jeeva
Rasi according to KCD is unwelcome.

Sloka No. 333 should be related to sloka 331
for a clear picture, and that is what we have done
here.

of times which the reader may ignore for practical

344. Astrologers oredict effects of sub
periods dividing a dasa into 12 various segements,
according to odd and even signs.

Notes: In the first line, the expression
‘Becjayugmaanu- saarathah’ should be
‘Ojhayugmaanusaarathah’ to make proper sense.
The author suggests that each Rasi dasa should
be made into sub periods spreading over twelve
zodiacal signs according to odd and even signs.
For odd signs, the counting is in the reverse orders
while for even signs, the counting is in usual as-
cending order. But there is no clear instruction

as to what particular Jaimini dasa is referred to
Apparently, this sloka is a lone occupant of this
part of the text.

ae aH ys vata

345-3451/2 . The native will get auspicious
effects relating to the Rasi aspected by the lords
of ascendant, and 9th and 10th. (That is, these
bhavas will turn auspicious). So also the Rasis
aspected by 9th/10th lords.

Notes: Here are given some general rules.

_ The house aspected by the lord of the ascendant
' will prove favourable. This rule is generally found

in many standard texts. But in this text we find
some additional instructions about 9th and 10th
lords. The house aspected by such a lord, or the
house occupied by such a lord, will prove auspi-
cious. One of these lords for example related to
the 2nd house as above will give wealth, happy
family life and the like. To the 3rd - acquisition of
coborn, good terms with them etc. To the 4th -
education, conveyances etc. To the 5th - progeny,
intelligence etc. To the 6th - freedom from dis-
eases, debts etc. only when the planet in question
is well-placed. To'the 7th - auspicious marriage,
chaste sex life etc. To the 8th - the 9ta lord will

confer fortunes if strong; misfortunes/ profes-
sional adversities if weak. To the 12th - success in
foreign countries by 9th lord if strong and profes-
sional progress if 10th lord is strong. As far as
ascendant is concerned, such relation by lord of
9/10th is a Raja Yoga.

346-3471/2. The 2nd dasa and the Rasi dasas
of the four angles will be auspicious for the native
of Varuna Nadiamsa. When Jupiter in transit
arrives at the end of Gemini, the subject will earn
wealth; his fortunes will increase with Jupiter
moving in Cancer. When Jupiter obtains the
Navamsa of Leo during his transit in Virgo, the
## Page 61

ey

subject’s sister will be married off. The native will
obtain Rajayoga effects, and auspiciousness will
accrue to him through his father.

Notes: The first line of sloka 346 states that
one born in Chakra Yoga, with the rising Nadiam-
sa being Varuna (in Sagittarius) will be ever for-
tunate. There seems to be some erroneous
composition in the line, hence not added in the
translation.

Second dasa refers to Vimsottari. Rasi dasa
referred to in this sloka canfiot be KCD as 4
Kendra Rasi dasas are referred. These refer to
Jaimini dasas. But the clues here are too limited
to make wide use of.

348-350. In the malefic dasa cited earlier
and during malefic sub periods, he will be sub-
jected to great miseries and his prosperity will be
obstructed. During the dasa of Mars, coinciding
with transit Jupiter’s aspect on Leo, the native of
Sagittarius ascendant will attain a high degree of
fortunes. He will be married for the second time.

Notes: The second marriage cited here
shall apply only to Varuna Nadiamsa native but
not to all Sagittarius natives. However, we can
take advantage of the condition that Jupiter’s
aspect on the Leo, during the dasa of Mars will
increase fortunes. So to say, if the 9th house if
favourably aspected by a favourable planet or by
Jupiter during the currency of a Yogakaraka’s
dasa, the native of any ascendant will reap better
fortunes.

For example in case of Libra ascendant,
Saturn is a benefic planet. If he aspects the 9th,
Gemini, while in transit, during the rulership of
Mercury dasa, or Saturn dasa, the native will
become more fortunate.

In case of another ascendant, say Aries,
Jupiter if in transit aspects Sagittarius during the

dasa of Sun/Moon/Mars/Jupiter, the subject will
obtain better results.

351-352 Saturn in Aquarius with Capricorn
Navamsa at birth will cause second marriage
either inthe last one-third part of Vipat Dasa (3rd
from birth) or in the first half of Kshema Dasa
(4th from birth). Results should be declared after
analysing suitably the dasa periods. Also after
analysing the transits (of the relevant planets) on
the degrees concerned.

353. The dasa ruled by 5th lord will greatly
endanger the native’s paternal uncle. Distress to
paternal uncle will come to pass in the dasa of the
Moon’s dispositor.

Notes: The hints given hereof will specifical-
ly apply to Sagittaris ascendant. The dasa of
Mars will endanger paternal uncle. One’s pater-
nal uncles are denoted by 11th house as well as
the 7th.

Distress to paternal uncles during the dasa
of the planet in whose house the Moon at birth is
placed is a significant clue. For Sagittarius ascen-
dant, the Moon’s dispositor has something spe-
cially to do, with paternal uncle.

354, Take a particular bhava. See in which
Navamsa, the 8th lord for that bhava is placed.
When Saturn in transit comes to Navamsa Rasi in
question, the relative indicated by the bhava will
be endangered.

Notes: Given in this sloka are gneral hints,
not for one particular ascendant.

For example the 9th rules father. The lord of
the 8th counted from the 9th house is the 4th lord.
See in which Navamsa the 4th lord is placed. Take
it as a Rasi. When Saturn comes to that Rasi ina
future transit, he will prove ominous to the father

With the help of above table, we can find

easily the Navamsa dispositor of the lord of the

house noted in column 3. Then we can link it to
Saturn’s transit. An inquisitive reader can take a
great advantage of these clues. Also, see slokas
526-527 infra.

Further to an intelligent student, the above
table will clarify, why the 9th house is treated as
house of father instead of 10th which is 7th from
4th.

357-359. Should Rahu and the Sun be in
Aquarius, while the Sun begets a Navamsa ruled
by 7th lord (i.e. ruled by Mercury), the subject will
have union with other women, that is, he will be
adulterous. Further he will suffer from windy and
urinary disorders. After some interval he will
emerge pure-hearted and will give up the habit of
adultery. He will ever take to bad path and be
somewhat troubled by diseases. His wife will be
perennially ill, but will intermittently recover. If
the Sun is in a Navamsa of Venus (while being in
Aquarius Rasi in association with Rahu), the na-
tive will enjoy abundant prosperity. He will be
happy through spouse (i.e. she will be devoid of
health problems).

Notes: In the above yoga, Sun in Mercury’s
Navamsa will be a source of health problems
while in Venusian Navamsa he will give her good
health.

is aspected by Jupiter while the Moon is with
Rahu in the first half of Uraga Nadiamsa in Scor-
pio, the child born will be entangled with umbili-
cal cord. If the birth is in the 2nd half, there will
be no such entanglement. Jupiter aspecting the
birth in former half of this Nadiamsa will at times
give happiness (at the time of delivery, free from
such complications).

half of Uraga Nadiamsa will climinate fear of

381-381 1/2. First Half of Uraga Nadiamsa:
Birth in this half will ensure a (long) living father.
The native’s mother will be (often) troubled by
diseases. His 3rd dasa will cause her death, with
Saturn moving in the end of Libra, or in Scorpio.

Notes: In Cancer, the first half of this
Nadiamsa extends from 29 deg. 24’ to 29 deg. 30’
of arc. The second half extends from 29 deg. 30’
to 29 deg. to 36’. Birth in first half will give a
long-living father while the 2nd half will cause
danger to the father during the native’s 8th/10th
year of age. Also see sloka 396 infra.

The first-half native will not however be
happy about father, nor will he inherit paternal
property (vide slokas 388-390 infra).

388-390. Family, wealth etc: One born in

the second half of this Nadiamsa will indulge in
thieving. He will be addicted to others’ women.

Otherwise he will get a wicked spouse promoting
quarrels. The native of the former half will have a
good family but be bereft of happiness through
father. He will have self- earned wealth and be
fond of parents. Rahu placed in Arudra Nak-
shatra will give wealth, valour and gratefulness. If
Rahu is in Navamsa (or divisions) of a malefic, the
native will be base and be a sinner. He will eat
anything and be ever troubled by diseases.

391-393. Rahu: The native of Uraga
Nadiamsa with Rahu in the 4th quarter of Arudra
(i.e. in Pisces Navamsa) will be fond of friends.
One born in the first half of this Nadiamsa will be

398-399. Maternal relatives: The Moon
placed in Uraga Nadiamsa’s first half with
benefic’s aspect will cause destruction of mater-
nal relatives for one born in Leo Navamsa
(Mitramsa is the navamsa owned by the Sun) in
Scorpio ascendant. If she be in second half of the
said Nadiamsa, there will be manifold growth of
members of maternal relatives’ families. They will
in addition be happy. The native will have three
maternal uncles while one of them will be some-
what fortunate.

Notes: Mitra means the Sun. It also means
a friend. But seeing the reference to Scorpio
ascendant, the Navamsa of the Sun is a befitting

|

rendering instead of friendly Navamsa. Here the
reference is not to Mars, but to Scorpio.

The Moon in first half of Uraga Nadiamsa,
while birth is in Leo Navamsa, Scorpio ascendant
(3 deg. 20’ to 6 deg, 40°) will cause maternal
kinsmen’s destruction. Just by change of the
Moon into the 2nd half of this Nadiamsa, the
other condition being present, the maternal fami-
ly will see growth.

433-437 1/2. Exit: One born with the Mocn
in Uraga Nadiamsa, in first half will have a long
life if the Sun is in debilitation Rasi and such
Navamsa. His life span will be 71 years. At 61
(contrary to 71 just mentioned) he will die in
Dakshinayana (Sun’s southerly course) when the
Sun will be moving in Cancer/Virgo/Scorpio. His
death will be on a Friday. In his next birth, his
natal constellation will be Aswini. One born in
second half of this Nadiamsa will be a great sinner
and will not attain heavens. The general effects
for birth in former half will be mixed, and for

second half both happiness and unhappiness will

result.

438-4441/.2. Durdhara Nadiamsa: If Jupiter
jos Saturn or is aspected by him, one born in an
immovable ascendant with Durdhara Nadiamsa
will incur destruction of elder brothers. He will
be endowed with younger coborns, will be weal-

i ail

|
afrad are — afe1 }~34 1 1 thy and will be emaciated in childhood due to

grief. He will have three wives, be passionate,
given to anger but could be appeased instantly.
He will be endowed with learning and intel-
ligence. He will be fond of sweet and sour juices,
will be lustful, dear to mother, sacrificing in na-
ture and attached to women. He will be wealthy
on account of his fahter’s properties and will be
affectionate to his younger coborn. During his
childhood, loss of a paternal uncle will come to
pass. He will further be troubled by smallpox,
ulcers, dental and windy disorders. He will be
somewhat mixed in disposition with Satwa, Rajas
and Tamas. He will eat even uneatable food. He
will be skillful in gathering wealth. His first child
will be destroyed. He will attain surviving children
through second wife. Three of his daughters will
be longlived. These are the effects concerning
progeny and coborn.

of movable signs, from 6 deg. 48’ to 7 deg. 0’ and
in case of common signs from 21 deg. 48’ to 22
deg. 0’ of arc.)

445-4471/2. Mohana Nadiamsa: The ascen-
dant lord in Mohana Nadiamsa while Jupiter
aspects the 8th house will cause danger in
childhood. Malika Yoga formed from the Rasi
occupied by 6th lord will give a charming ap-
pearance. One born in Mohana Nadiamsa will
deceive others and will gather wealth by ques-
tionable means. He will be dutiful to his father
and will be troubled by digestive disorders. He
will help others, be passionate, be somewhat
religious. (Dharma Sudehavaan is an improper
addition. Apparently the text implies acquisition
of a beautiful physique).

Notes: Here the ascendant refered to is an
immovable one, with Durdhara Nadiamsa on the
horizon. The lord of such ascendant should be in
Mohana Nadiamsa.

Mohana Nadiamsa is not enlisted. But we
have Trailokya Mohanakari Nadiamsa which ex-
tends from 14 deg. 48’ to 15 deg. 0’ of a movable
sign, ftom 15 deg. 0’ to 15 deg. 12’ of animmovable
sign and from 29 deg. 48’ to 30 deg. of a common
sign. Mohana is an abbreviation, for metric pur-
poses.

454-454 1/2. Sudha Nadiamsa: The Moon
placed in Sudha Nadiamsa in Cancer in aspect to
Jupiter will ensure long-living maternal uncles in
case of birth in Aquarius Lagna.

Notes: Discussions for Durdhara Nadiamsa
in Aquarius ascendant continue. Now the posi-
tion of the Moon in the 6th in Cancer in Sudha
Nadiamsa is dealt with. Sudha Nadiamsa in Can-
## Page 71

11 deg. o’ to 11 deg. 12

46 Chandra Kala Nadi

cer extends from 18 deg. 36’ to 18 deg. 48”. (In
Immovable sign it is from 11 deg. 12’-11 deg. 24
and in common signs from 3 deg. 36’ to 3 deg. 48”
of arc.)

For Aquarius Lagna, the Moon is the 6th
lord, denoting maternal uncles. The 11th is the
6th from the 6th and the 11th lord is Jupiter. The
Moon in the said Nadiamsa falls in Sagittarius
Navamsa. Such a yoga assists maternal uncles
with long-lives.

455-4551/2 . Relatives: The number of rela-
tives that will face (early) death will correspond
to the number of Ashtaka Varga Bindus (after
reduction) in the Ashtaka Vargas of the Moon
and the Sun. The Moon denotes maternal uncles
and the Sun paternal uncles. (This applies to
Durdhara Nadiamsa native.)

Notes: This sloka deals with maternal and
paternal uncles. Some condition detailing their
deaths seems to be missing. What all we gather
Moon’s Ashtaka Varga deals with maternal rela-
tives and the Sun’s Ashtaka Varga paternal un-
cles. This deals with Durdhara Nadiamsa in
Aquarius ascendant. Also see sloka 458 1/2 infra.

456-4581/2 . Other texts state that one born
in Durdhara Nadiamsa will not have paternal
uncles, His father will attain prosperity after a
long interval. The native’s childhood will be
marked by troubles. There will be difficulties in
the native’s father’s home and that of maternal
uncles. His father will be happy because of help
from his brother-in-law. With the Moon ruling the
6th if placed in Sudha Nadiamsa in aspect to
Jupiter, the native will have two maternal uncles
and there will be growth of (prosperity for)
maternal relatives.

Notes: These slokas deal with birth in
Durdhara Nadiamsa in Aquarius ascendant
without reference to any planet. The last instruc-
tion hereof however relates to the Moon’s posi-
tion in Sudha Nadiamsa as a continuing link to
sloka 454-4541/2 supra.

459-4611/2 . Jupiter in Durdhara Nadiamsa
in aspect to Saturn for an Aquarius Lagna native
according to some will give one maternal uncle.
After a long interval, the native will acquire a
step- mother. As per Naradeeya Jataka, Jupiter
in this Nadiamsa will give a long-living maternal
grand-father. The native will have two maternal
uncles. His mother will have two fathers-in-law.
(That is, the native’s paternal grand-mother
would have two marriages.) She will have only one
long-living son. She will be somewhat sickly and
will be grief-ridden on account of death of a
brother. She will have progeny after a long inter-
val and will be highly prosperous and happy.

Notes: Jupiter’s position could be in any
sign, u$ no signis mentioned, But he should be in
Durdhara Nadiamsa in aspect to Saturn, while
birth be in Aquarius ascendant, with Durdhara
Nadiamsa. As a result, the native will have one
maternal uncle apart from acquiring a step-
mother after a long interval. That is, the native’s
father will remarry.

Clues from Naradecya Jataka given hercof
relate to Jupiter’s position in Durdhara Nadiamsa
without mention of Saturn.

462-4631/2 . Jupiter placed in Pisces, with

## Page 72

Deva Keralam 47

The said dasa will be greatly prosperous. Second
half of the dasa will give conveyances. The native’s
paternal aunt’s husband will enjoy prosperity and
fame and will acquire conveyances.

generally described as a malefic. He can however
be favourable in given circumstances. One of this
is: Venus should be in Sagittarius in Rasi, while
Jupiter in Pisces should get Aquarius Navamsa
(23 deg. 20° to 26 deg. 40’). Then the dasa of
Jupiter will be prosperous & C. Also see slokas
509-5151/2 infra.

auspicious. If the 5th lord is in the 9th, his dasa

tive. In the first sub period ruled by Mercury, the
native will commence acquiring wealth.

475-4771/2. Maternal relatives: Jupiter
should be in Durdhara Nadiamsa, be the ruler of
the Moon-occcupied Navamsa, and be lastly
aspected by Saturn. Then, the native will have two
maternal uncles and two maternal aunts. Both the
maternal uncles will have adopted sons who will
only be destroyed. After a long interval, maternal
uncles will be grieved on account of peternal
destrucion. The two maternal aunts will be en-
dowed with sons and daughters. One of them will
be troubled by grief, will lose her husband and be
emaciated. The other one will have a long-living
husband and be endowed with many sons and be
happy.

brothers.

occurs to a planet when it isin the last six degrees.

505-506 1/2. Daridra Malika Yoga: If the
seven planets are disposed in the various seven
Rasis continuously counted from the Navamsa
Rasi of the 6th lord, the native will incur penury
and many difficulties in childhood. A malefic in
the 8th house without a benefic aspect will also
cause poverty.

Notes: Only seven planets from the Sun to
Saturn are considered in Malika Yoga. They
should be progressively in continuous seven
houses. Thus 2 planets cannot be in one house.
When the Yoga starts from ascendant, it is called
Lagna Malika. From the 2nd Dhana Malika,

Chandra Kala Nadi

from the 3rd Vikrama Malika, so on and so forth.
To simplify, the Malika yoga goes under the name
of the house from where it commences.

The present work adopts a practice of
counting Malika Yoga from the Navamsa oc-
cupied by a certain planet. Here it takes the 6th
lord Moon. We should note Moon’s navamsa,
and from the Rasi identical with said Navamsa,
we should find seven planets in seven continuous
houses. Then the native instead of getting a Raja
yoga will suffer from poverty etc.

For Aquarius ascendant, a malefic in the 8th
house (Virgo) should be related to a benefic lest
he should cause penury.

520-522. These will be in the sub period of
Saturn in the 4th dasa, or in the sub periods of
Jupiter as well as Mars, in any dasa (ruled by any
planet). The native’s health will decline in Mer-
cury sub period, with Sun’s transit in an evil Rasi,
or at the time of Saturn’s combustion in Gochara,
on Wednesday, Thursday or Saturday.

Notes: The adverse results (not travels)
mentioned in slokas 518 - 519 1/2 will materialise
in Saturn’s sub period in the dasa which is 4th
from birth. Alternatively, the sub period of Mars
and of Jupiter, in any dasa, can also be noteworthy
in this regard.

The period of illness relating to Saturn’s
combustion in transit may specially be noted.
That is, combustion is one of the clues to time
events, like retrogression/direction.

aspected by the 8th lord counted from a certain

531. According to Manu: From Lagna to
12th, the movements of Saturn in the respective
8th Bhava denote death of concerned relatives.
Or when Saturn transits such Rasis as aspected by
him at birth will also give same effect. Good and
bad for them be estimated accordingly.

Notes: This sloka may be linked to sloka 354
and 526-527 supra. According to Manu, the
planet Saturn holds key to deaths of various
kinsmen which can be foretold from one horo-
scope.

532-542. Venus in the 11th, while Jupiter is
in 2nd/10th/4th - this Yoga will give following
effects if birth is in Durdhara Nadiamsa. The
native will be very prosperous. His prosperity will
be in the region of Mahanadi(also a great river)
or in a foreign country. He will enjoy pleasures,
will serve a mean king, will befriend many in the
course of his business activities, will be passionate
and will be sacrificing in nature. In his second
dasa, he will beget happiness'and children. In 4th
dasa he will prosper, will get sickness, and will be
famous. He will reject remnant food, be endowed
with firm riches; his fame will specially increase
after the 25th year. He will enjoy pleasures after
63rd year and gather riches. He will incur abun-
dant grief on account of loss of friends and
employer. In the 4th dasa, in a different kingdom
he will acquire wealth. In the same dasa, he will
get his daughter and son married in that order. In
the Sth dasa he will be grieved on account of
enmity with his friends. In the 2nd dasa, he will be
happy following birth of coborn when Saturn will
be in Libra. Saturn moving in Virgo will increase
prosperity of relatives. At the same time, the hus-
band of father’s sister will also prosper and his
father will acquire happiness. Saturn in transit in
Libra will give wealth; in the middle of Virgo he
will cause auspicious effects. When he moves in
the end of Scorpio or in Sagittarius, he will cause
the death of paternal grand-mother. In trines
thereof he will cause the wellbeing of the inmates
of Chola kingdom(?) The ruler of his country will

die in a war(?) These effects relating to countries

| 1 &3&] | have been stated in Sani Nadi.

Notes: These eleven slokas apart from sloka
462-462 1/2 and 509-510 1/2 supra deal with Jupiter
and Venus for the ascendant Aquarius.

543-547, The said Sani Nadi extensively dis-
cusses (such) effects in a surprising manner. One
born in Vipra Kala of Durdhara Nadiamsa (read
Durdharamse instead of Dasamsc) with the 9th
lord placed in the 11th house would have been a
Brahmin in the previous birth. Inthe next birth he
will be a Vaidic (following codes prescribed by the
Vedas) Brahmana. Following a calamity in the
family he would then take to ascetic order. Birth
as Vaidic Brahmana will be duc to the meritorious
deeds done by him. If the 12th lord is aspected by
Jupiter, he will attain final emancipation follow-
ing the next birth. (That is he will have one more
birth after the current one.) His life’s length will
he 74 years. 49th/52nd year will cause effects of
untimely death. If the 9th lord joins Jupiter, 71st
year Will be fatal. These effects as stated in Guru
Nadt will be unfailing.

548-5491/2. Sachira Nadiamsa: Ascendant
(Capricorn) in Sachira Nadiamsa with Mars
## Page 79

54 Chandra Kala Nadi

therein will cause physical ailments to the native’s
mother, or to his older sister. If the Moon is in
Pisces ia her fateful degree and in the company
of Ketu, the native’s mother’s sister will indulge
illicit contacts. (Vishakyamsa can also be inter-
preted as Visha Nadiamsa instead of fateful de-
gree.)

Notes: In none of the works in my posses-
sion Sachira Nadiamsa is enlisted. Not even in
the present work.

{ do not know if I am right when | feel it is
Chitra Nadiamsa. This extends from 12 deg. to 12
deg. 12’ in a movable sign, from 17 deg. 48” to 18
deg. of an immovable sign, and from 27 deg. to 27
deg. 12’ ina common sign.

Mars rules the 4th (mother) and 11th (older
coborn) and hence relatives are referred to here
when Mars is in Capricorn ascendant.

The second clue given is: the Moon in her
fateful degree in Pisces, and to be with Ketu.

The fateful degrees for the Moon are:

Rasi As per As per

Jaathaka Parijatha Phala Deepika

Aries 8th degre 26th degree
Taurus Sth degree 12th degree
Gemini 22nd degree 13th degree
Cancer 22nd degree 25th degree
Leo 21st degree 24th degree
Virgo Ist degree 11th degree
Libra 4th degree 26th degree
Scorpio 23rd degree 14th degree
Sagittarius 18th degree 13th degree
Capricorn 20th degree 25th degree
Aquarius = 20th degree Sth degree

Pisces 10th degree 12th degree

The degrees given by Vaidyanatha in his
Jaathaka Parijata appears to be more or less ac-
ceptable to a majority of astrologers. The views

followed by Mantreswara agree with the work
entitled ‘Brihat Prajapatyam’.

For Visha Nadiamsa, see notes under sloka
554-559 infra.

§50-5531/2. One born in Capricorn ascen-
dant, Sachira Nadiamsa, having Saturn in
Aquarius with Mars will marry a girl hailing from
mother’s side. The 9th lord in Gemini Navamsa
while the 9th contains Rahu in aspect to the Moon
denotes a sister (i.e. the native’s coborn) being
interested in other men. Birthin Capricorn ascen-
dant with Leo Navamsa while Saturn is in con-
junction with Jupiter denotes an unfortunate and
wicked mother, who will not care to honour her
husband’s words. The 4th lord in Chaaravas-
tha(?) in the company of Saturn will give a long
living mother, who will have secret relations with
others and be auspicious (?)

Notes: In these slokas four important events
are prescribed which are independent:

(1) Ascendant Capricorn, Sachira Nadiam-
sa, containing Saturn-Mars in it - bride from
mother’s side.

(2) The lord of 9th Mercury in Gemini
Navamsa, while Rahu is in the 9th house (Virgo)
in aspect to Moon - sister with illicit connections.

(3) Capricorn ascendant with Leo Navam-
sa (i.e. 23 deg. 20’ to 26 deg. 40’ of Capricorn
rising) while Jupiter and Saturn are together in
Rasi - unfortunate and wicked mother who does
not care for her husband, i.e. the native’s father.

(4) 4th lord Mars (in Charavastha?) with
Saturn - long-living mother but with illicit ties.
