§54-5591/2. Relatives: Saturn in Sachira
Nadiamsa with the lord of the 4th denotes an
abundantly prosperous maternal family. The
native’s father will have a (good) living. The 4th
lord in Sagittarius along with Jupiter, as Saturn is
placed in Aquarius denotes a fortunate maternal
grand-father. The said grand-father will have
numerous children, much wealth, brothers and
sisters, will acquire fame in royal service and will
have men-borne conveyances. The Moon in the
ascendant for a birth in Visha Nadiamsa will
cause happiness to mother who will be pure-
minded and will be endowed with brothers and
sisters. Elsewhere it is stated that the ascendant
lord (Saturn) in the company of a planet that is in
Rajavastha denotes a mother bereft of a sister but
endowed with brothers. The number of living
coborns will correspond to the net Bindus in
Chandrashtaka Varga.

Notes: In sloka 557, Visha Nadiamsa is
cited. This Nadiamsa in a movable sign extends
from 10 deg. 12’ to 10 deg. 24’; in an immovable
Rasi from 19 deg. 36’ to 19 deg. 48’; and in a
common sign from 25 deg. 12’ to 25 deg. 24 of
space.

In Capricorn, this Nadiamsa rises from 10
deg. 12’ to 10 deg. 24’. In such a case, the Moon
should be in Ascendant. Then the mother will be
happy & C.

587-5901/2. Saturn in Capricorn while the
Moon is in Pisces Rasi with Aquarius Navamsa -
this yoga will give virtuous children to maternal
uncles, but troubles on account of tuberculosis
and emaciation. The native’s maternal relatives
will prosper while his father will sometimes be
happy. With Saturn in Pisces in transit coinciding
with the native’s first dasa, his sister will get mar-
ricd and he will have his Upanayana (Sacred
thread ceremony as per Vedic prescriptions). His
marriage will occur in his second dasa. His third
dasa will cause acquisition of wealth. When
Saturn comes to the Rasi indicated by the navam-
sa position of Ketu at birth, or its trine, the
country’s army-chief will be destroyed(?)

Notes: The Moon in Pisces will begct
Aquarius Navamsa when placed between 23 deg.
20°’ and 26 deg. 40’. The Moon rules maternal
uncles only when she is the 6th lord. But here the
text takes the Moon into account although she is
the lord of the 7th. The Navamsa ascendant being
Aquarius and the Moon being ruler of mother,
the text gives importance to the planet. The
Moon is 6th lord from Navamsa ascendant.

Saturn’s transit in 3rd in Pisces features in
respect of sister’s marriage. This is because of the
Moon’s position therein.

§93-5931/2. Second dasa: For one born in
Sachira Nadiamsa, his second dasa will give abun-

594-5971/2. Evils: Saturn in the 2nd, Raku in
the 9th, and the lord of the week-day of birth with
a malefic - this yoga kills the native’s wife in the
(very) second dasa, and immediately re- marriage
will occur to the native. Saturn coming in transit
to the Rasi represented by the natal Navamsa
position of the 2nd lord, or to a trine thereof, or
to the Rasi that is aspected by the 12th lord, will
cause danger to the native’s children. Maternal
uncles will be destroyed with Saturn’s transit in
the Rasi identical with the natal Navamsa position
of the ascendant lord, or its trine, or the Rasi
identical with 8th lord’s Navamsa position or trine
thereof. In the absence of this, there will be severe
destrucion of some other maternal relatives. The
Sun’s transit in evil Rasis will in this connection
be revealing. The entire clan of relatives will be
grief-struck (on account of such death/deaths).

Notes: The lord of the week-day of birth is
brought into the picture in this 3-planet yoga.
Saturn in 2nd in Aquarius, Rahu in 9th in Virgo,
and lord of week-day of birth in association with

a malefic. This will cause wife’s death in the
native’s 2nd dasa, paving way for an immediate
remarriage. From this we understand that the
lord of the week-day of birth is not less important
than the lord of ascendant.

The seven week-days are named after the
seven planets from the Sun to Saturn. Ketu
denotes Tuesday and Rahu Saturday.

Exclude this 3-planet yoga in respect of
danger to children. The requirements then are:
Saturn should come to the Rasi in transit which is
identical with his own natal Navamsa position.
Alternatively he can transit the Rasi which at birth
is aspected by the lord of the 12th (i.e. Jupiter),
Such a transit of Saturn will endanger the native’s
offspring.

The Rasi aspected by 12th lord assumes
additional importance as the 12th house for
Capricorn ascendant is ruled by Jupiter, the sig-
nificator of progeny.

603-6041/2. Father’s death: Saturn in
Sachira Nadiamsa while the Sun is in Mukunda
Nadiamsa will prove fatal to the native’s father or
a rclative equal to father during third Dasa when
Jupiter in transit comes to the last degrees of
Scorpio, or when he moves in the sign Capricorn,
in adverse months. The mother will live for a long
time as a widow.

Notes: Mukunda Nadiamsa extends from
26 deg. 36’ to 26 deg. 48’ in movable signs; from 3
deg. 12’ to 3 deg. 24 in immovable signs; and from
11 deg. 36’ to 11 deg. 48’ in common signs.

Mukunda is a synonym of Lord Vishnu who
is known so for He is the authority to bestow final
emancipation or Moksha. Thus this Nadiamsa

deals with one’s exit from this world. The Sun is
the indicator of father.

As per the present slokas, the Sun should be
in Mukunda Nadiamsa which denotes short life
to father.

610-611. Children: Saturn in Sachira
Nadiamsa will give a number of children. Many
children will be born dead. Ultimately the native
## Page 85

6l)

will be left with two or three surviving children.
The number of long-living children will depend
on the rays obtained, or on the Navamsa past, by
the Sth lord.

Notes: For Capricorn ascendant, Saturn in
Sachira Nadiamsa carries with him the blemish of
instant deaths of "many’ children. In the end, two
or three will survive. However, the number of
surviving children can increase if the Sth lord
Venus obtains more Navamsas. That is, the Sth
lord Venus covering increased Navamsas in the
Rasi he is in at birth will have chance of giving
more surviving children. This clue is clear.

Another clue is to depend on the rays ob-
tained by the 5th lord Venus. Rays are known as
Kiranas in Sanskrit. Calculating Kiranas is rather
an elaborate process all of which cannot be ex-
plained in the notes here. The reader is referred
to Saravali, English translation by R. Santhanam,
(Ch 36).

638-6421/2. Kunda Nadiamsa: For a native
of Pisces ascendant, if Mercury is placed in his
own sign in Kunda Nadiamsa, in the company of
the Sun and in aspect to 10th lord Jupiter, good
fortunes will accrue. Mercury becoming the lord
of the Moon sign and being in aspect to Jupiter,
will give paternal wealth to a Pisces native of the
Kunda Nadiamsa, in Vipra Kala. One born in
Kshatriya Kala will worship Lord Vishnu and will
serve an emperor. If the birth be in Vaisya Kala,
the subject will acquire livelihood by various busi-
ness activities. He will gain wealth and grains, will
serve Brahmanas and be happy. One born in
Soodra Kala will serve a king, will own lands and
villages, will be an agriculturist and will have plen-
ty of quadrupeds and corns.

Notes: From here through sloka 855, rules
from Budha Nadi are quoted.

To start with, Pisces ascendant, Kunda
Nadiamsa is dealt with.

Kunda Nadiamsa rules thus: From 26 deg.
24 to 26 deg. 36’ in movable signs; from 3 deg. 24”
to 3 deg. 36’ in immovable signs; from 11 deg. 24
to 11 deg. 36’ of common signs.

In the first yoga, Mercury should be in
Gemini/Virgo in unity with the Sun and be

aspected by Jupiter. As a result the native will be
fortunate. The Sun is 6th lord.

In the second yoga, Vipra Kala should rise.
That is to say, birth ascendant should be 11 deg.
36’ to 11 deg. 39’ of Pisces. Further, the Moon,
being Sth lord, should be in the 4th/7th
whereupon Mercury begets Moon Rasi owner-
ship. Jupiter should additionally aspect Mercury,
Result - paternal wealth.

The clues for births in other 3 parts of this
Nadiamsa are independent of second yoga men-
tioned above.

Kshatriya Kala of Kunda Nadiamsa in Pisces
extends from 11 deg. 3%” to 11 deg. 42’ of arc. One
born in this part will be a devotee of Lord Vishnu
and will be associated with an emperor.

Vaisya Kala of this Nadiamsa is from 11 deg.
42’ to 11 deg. 45’ when it rises in Pisces. The
native will be a trader true to the nathe of the part
of the Nadiamsa.

Soodra Kala is the last one fourth part, i.e.
11 deg. 45’ to 11 deg. 48’ in Pisces. Such a native
will be a rich person with agricultural lands, quad-
rupeds and the like.

643-6441/2. For birth in Pisces ascendant in
Vipra Kala of Kunda Nadiamsa, if Mercury is in
aspect to Jupiter, the younger coborns are
destroyed. The native will have older coborns, be
honourable and will have abundant paternal
wealth. He will have full brothers and step-
brothers as well.

Notes: Here Mercury’s position is not
prescribed unlike in the previous slokas. His con-
nection in general with Jupiter is adverse for the
native’s younger coborn. But the birth should be
in the portion 11 deg. 36’ to 11 deg. 39” in Pisces.
However, the native will have full preborns,
paternal wealth and step- brothers. He will be an
honourable person as well.

645-6501/2. If the 7th lord is in aspect to
Jupiter, one born in Kunda Nadiamsa will wor-
ship Lord Vishnu and Lord Siva. He will honour
gods and Brahmins and will have (long-living)
parents. He will be happy, will gain fame in royal
service and will have three conveyances. During
the native’s middle age, his father will acquire
palanquins (i.e. some conveyance) and fortunes.
The native will indulge in self-praising and will
help others. His father will have five brothers and
two sisters and be happy. Due to loss of older
brother, his father will incur grief. Following this
the father will migrate to the southern part of the
country. He will serve an emperor and will
befriend Brahmins. He will live in a town amidst
forests and will also serve a mean ruler. Hating
Vaishnavites, he will incur many difficultics.

Notes: We have to delink here the four parts
of Kunda Nadiamsa, and just apply the present
rules in general to Kunda Nadiamsa in Pisces
ascendant.

Mercury aspected by Jupiter will make the
native worship Lord Vishnu and Lord Siva. Mer-
cury rules Vishnu. Devotion to Lord Siva is be-
cause of Jupiter-Mercury association. Other
effects given upto sloka 6501/2 are clear.

651-6541/2. Mercury in Kunda Nadiamsa for
a Pisces native will at the time of native’s birth
cause grief to father. If Navamsa Lagna be
Capricorn, the native’s fourth year —_ will cause
distress to father, and after some interval father
will have increased fortunes. The native’s second
dasa will cause happiness to father. The native’s
prosperity will be in progress. He will lose his
protectors. His step-brothers will acquire
progeny. His (full) brothers will be abundantly
happy. In the native’s first dasa, birth of children
to maternal uncle will come to pass. And his
step-brother will get married. Possibly children of
step- brothers will also be destroyed. Evils to
maternal grand-mother will also be experienced:
she will meet with near death and will survive.

is fixed in Kunda Nadiamsa. The ascendant
should be Pisces, but need not necessarily be in a
particular degree. Then the father will be

655-6551/2. Kesari Yoga: One born with this
Yoga while the Moon is in the 7th house from the
ascendant will have long-living parents. His
maternal grand-mother will also be long-lived.

Notes: The author refers to Kesari yoga
where the Moon should be in Virgo in the 7th. We
should know the difference between Gaja Kesari
Yoga and merely Kesari Yoga.

Very few texts exactly describe Gaja Kesari.
Perhaps many compilers for want of brevity did
resort to brief mention of the conditions of Gaja
Kesari.

In Gaja Kesari the main constituent is

Jupiter. The Moon may or may not be in the
picture. I have given some relevant information
## Page 89

64

on this in Essentials of Predictive Hindu Astrology,
as well as Brihat Parasara Hora, Part 1.

Coming to Kesari yoga, the constitutents are
two planets - the Moon and Jupiter by being
mutually angular.

Long life, renown, high intelligence,
destroying enemies and valour are the main ef-
fects of this Yoga. There is a view that one with
this yoga will highly prosper in the dasa ruled by
Venus.

Coming to our text, the Moon forming
Kesari Yoga should be in Virgo in the 7th. Jupiter
can be in any of the four common signs. As a
result, the native’s parents and maternal grand-
mother will enjoy long leases of life.

659-(421/2. When Saturn in transit arrives at

Chandra Kala Nadi

while ascendant lord Jupiter is in the end of
Gemini, or in Cancer. In the dasa of Sth lord, the
native in question will be very happy. His father
in this dasa will acquire royal honours, and be
happy after destroying his enemies. The native
will acquire palanquins, jewels etc. and will be

meaning the dasa of 4th lord. As the text so far
deals with Mercury from the beginning of this
portion of Kunda Nadiamsa, sloka 660 etc. should
be dealing with Mercury’s dasa and not Moon’s
dasa. Hence it should be Sukhadipa dasa kaale.
This terms continues in the following slokas also.

685-686. For a Kunda Nadiamsa native, the
Sun in Harina Nadiamsa will give Raja yoga ef-
fects according to Surya Nadi. Similarly, when the
Sun is in Ambuja Nadiamsa as Jupiter is is Harina
Nadiamsa. So declare the learned about these
three Nadiamsas.

Chandra Kala Nadi

Notes: Two different Raja Yogas are men-
tioned for a native of Kunda Nadiamsa native in
Pisces:

(1) The Sun in Harina Nadiamsa. This
Nadiamsa is ensisted as Harini (meaning deer)
Nadiamsa in all the three sources consulted.

This Nadiamsa extends from 23 deg. 48’ to
24 deg. in a movable sign; from 6 deg. 0’ to 6 deg.
12’ of an immovable sign; and from 8 deg. 48’ to 9
deg. 0’ of a common sign.

The Sun in respective space of Harini
Nadiamsa in any Rasi for Pisces native with
Kunda Nadiamsa will give a Raja Yoga. The Sun
is the lord of the 6th, and being just in such a
position he can elevate the native to a worthy
position.

(2) In the second yoga the Sun and Jupiter
are required to be in certain spaces. The Sun in
Ambuja Nadiamsa while Jupiter is in Harini
Nadiamsa.

Harini Nadiamsa is explained above.

Pankaja (lotus) Nadiamsa extends from 29
deg. 36’ to 29 deg. 48’ of a movable sign; from 0
deg. 12’ to 0 deg. 24 of an immovable sign; and
from 14 deg. 36’ to 14 deg. 48’ in a common sign.
Jupiter should be anywhere in this manner.

These two yogas are from Surya Nadi.

Birth in Dhanada Nadiamsa in Virgo is
referred to. This Nadiamsa extends thus:

From 24 deg. 48’ to 25 deg of a movable sign;
from 5 deg. to 5 deg. 12’ of an immovable sign, and
from 9 deg. 48’ to 10 deg. of a common sign.

The first half of this Nadiamsa in Virgo is
from 9 deg. 48’ to 9 deg. 54’ of arc.

Nadiamsa. For Sura Nadiamsa, the various

of an immovable sign; and from 16 deg. 24’ to 16
deg. 36’ in common signs.

Nadiamsa, the Virgo native will be 2nd/3rd issue

719-7211/2. For a Virgo native, Venus should

grand-father. In addition, the paternal grand-

will incur troubles on account of Brahmins. He

Venus and Mercury exchange Navamsas owned
by them. The natal ascendant should be Virgo.

724-7271/2. One born in the first half of
Dhanada Nadiamsa while the ascendant lord is in
Sura Nadiamsa will have long-living parents. He
will have increased wealth and corns. If Mercury
is inthe 2nd house in Sura Nadiamsa, Chitra Yoga
is caused as a result of which the native will be
extremely rich. His father will be in royal service
and will enjoy a high degree of prosperity. The
native will be honourable, happy and will have two
brothers and two sisters. He will have 8 sisters in
all (out of whom only two will survive). Birth in
Dhanada Nadiamsa as Mercury is Sura Nadiamsa
will cause five sisters. Out of them the first one
will be famous and fortunate.

Notes: We find a new Dhana Yoga in this
part. This yoga is entitled Chitra Yoga which is,
for a Virgo native, caused by Mercury being in
Libra in the space from 1 deg. 24 to 1 deg. 36’ and
will cause abundant riches. Also note other ef-
fects in the text above.

Whether this Chitra Yoga applies to all as-
cendants by the ascendant lord being in 2nd in
Sura Nadimasa, may be examined.

Begetting five sisters etc. as mentioned in
the text are independent of Mercury in the 2nd &
C.

730-7321/2. If the 9th house is occupied by
Saturn in the company of Mars, the native will be
bereft of after-born and be short-lived. If the
ascendant lord isin Libra Navamsa, the native will
have four brothers and sisters (in all). He will be
endowed with longevity. His older brother will
enjoy wide fame. Mars becoming the lord of the
9th Aroodha and being in the company of 10th
lord (i.e. Mercury) will cause Bhagya Yoga lead-
ing to prosperity. Further the native will perform
virtuous deeds.

Notes: Saturn and Mars in the 9th house will
affect adversely the life-span of a Virgo native.

If Mercury begets Libra Navamsa, one will
be long-lived, and will have four coborns.

The above two rules are general.

The 3rd rule, viz. Mars becoming lord of 9th
Aroodha Pada, and be in association with Mer-
cury, the 10th lord, leading to prosperity is quite
suggestive. Mars, otherwise is an evil lord for
Virgo, ruling 3rd and 8th. But if he lords over
Bhagyaroodha (9th Aroodha) he becomes
capable of conferring riches, being in the com-
pany of 10th lord. In a way it implies association
of lords of 9 and 10.
## Page 95

Deva Keralam 71

How to count Aroodha Pada is explained in
many standard texts. A brief narration is given
here for immediate use by the reader. Count
from a house the number of signs its lord is away.
Again count equal number of signs from the sign
occupied by that lord. The resultant sign is
Aroodha Pada for the first mentioned sign. For
example, for Taurus ascendant, 5th lord Sun is
placed in Capricorn. We get six signs from Leo
to Capricorn. Again from Capricorn when we
count six signs we reach Gemini. So Gemini is
Aroodha for the 5th house, in this case. And is
called Putra Aroodha.

There are certain exceptions. The reader
may consult Part 1 of Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra,
English translation, by R. Santhanam.

775-777, Dhanada Nadiamsa: One born in
the first half of this Nadiamsa, with Mercury
placed in Sura Nadiamsa will live upto 65 years.
The dasa of 5th Rasi will be fatal for him. Should
Venus be in the 12th, he will attain the world of
Brahma (Sathya Loka, or Brahma Loka). In the
end of 11th Rasi dasa, the native will attain fame
and happiness. These effects as stated in Budha
Nadi will bear truth,

778-7781/2. Pisces Lagna - Kamala Nadiam-
sa: One born in this part of Zodiac while Saturn
occupies Aries Rasi and Leo Navamsa, will have
blood-red complexion. He will be learned. He
will disregard his religion and join another
religion. He will incur grief on account of
enemies.

Notes: From now on, the text deals with
birth in Pisces ascendant as told in Budha Nadi.

Kamala Nadiamsa obtains thus: From 5 deg.
48? to 6 deg. of a movable sign; from 24 deg. to 24
deg 12’ of an immovable sign; and from 20 deg.
48° to 21 deg. of a common sign.

Birth should be in the space between 20 deg.
48? to 21 deg. of Pisces. Saturn should be in the
2nd in Aries from 13 deg. 20’ to 16 deg. 40’,
begetting Leo Navamsa (6th from Pisces). This
gives many troubles from enemies.

The native changing into another religion is
rarely discussed in the texts known to us. This is
one such useful yoga.

should be in Aries in Kamala Nadiamsa in the
company of Mercury. In that case, one born in
Pisces ascendant will be devoted to Lord Vishnu.

He will have no after-born.

Deva Keraiam

780-7821/2, Saturn-Sun: If these two com-
bine in Aries, the native will be righteous,
valorous, be a knower of all, given to anger, vir-
tuous and be capable of breaking secrets. He will
be malignant (at times). The Kamala Nadiamsa
native having Saturn in a malefic Shashtiamsa will
be intelligent but inwardly cunning. He will be
libidinous and will have eyes resembling lotus-pe-
tals. He will be valorous, independent, addicted
to vices, given to instant anger, be pleased and
thin-bodied.

Notes: In the first place, exalted Sun and
debilitated Saturn joining together is discussed,
which is clear.

The second yoga dealing with Saturn in
malefic Shashtiamsa does not mention a specific
sign position to him. Nor the Sunis in the picture.
For details of Shashtiamsa - malefic and benefic -
please refer to Vol 1, Brihat Parasara Hora,
English translation by R. Santhanam.

783. Lakshmi yoga: Rahu in the 10th house
as Saturn is in Aries Rasi, Leo Navamsa: the yoga
called Lakshmi yoga is produced.

Notes: Results for this yoga are not specifi-
cally mentioned here. The name suggests wealth.
Also see sloka 808 which states that this yoga gives
wealth after the age of forty.

788-7941/2. Instead of being Leo Navamsa as
above, if the Navamsa occupied by Saturn (with
Mercury in Aries, for a Pisces native of Kamala
Nadiamsa), is Scorpio/Aries, following (dif-
ferent) effects will come to pass. The native will
be devoid of maternal happiness. Sisters born
after him will be destroyed. He wili be given to
anger and be lustful. He will live in his grand-
father’s home. During his childhood he will be
initiated into Vaishnava order by proper vedic
rituals.(Chakraankita denotes the Vedic
ceremony due toa Vaishnava Brahmin and during
such initiation, the boy’s shoulders are engrossed
by the sacred symbols of Lord Vishnu’s Sudar-
sana Chakra, and Sankhu - conch - by the Guru.
At the time of engrossing, these symbols, made of
copper, are heated. In Vaishnava circles, this is

ky Al 183i
## Page 100

76 Chandra Kala Nadi

called Samashanam.) Later on he will shift to his
paternal relative’s home. After his marriage and
following his 20th year of age he will be happy. As
aresult of his mother’s (early) death, he will live
in father’s (relative’s) home. His mother’s sister
will be fortunate. His father’s brother will have
two wives. The maternal aunt in question will have
a happy marriage. One born in Kamala Nadiamsa
will have troubles in his first dasa for himself and
to his maternal aunt as well. The native will
migrate to a distant country due to destroyed
fortunes.

Note: Chakraankita also means a symbol of
wheel, featuring in phvsiognomy relating to marks
noted at birth.

801-803. If two planets are in exaltation at
the time of birth as Saturn is in debilitation, the
native of Pisces Lagna in Kamala Nadiamsa will
experience the following effects: His paternal
uncle’s daughter will be an adulteress, will have
limited issues; in her middle age she will be in the
grip of poverty. Her coborns will be destroyed.
Further, the native’s paternal uncle (father’s
brother) will be subdued by his wife and incur
infamy due to his daughter’s adulterous charac-
ter.

Notes: Any two planets can be in exaltation,
while Saturn is in Aries, for a Pisces native with
Kamala Nadiamsa. Then the effects cited will
apply.

808-8121/2. Evils: The Moon in ascendant’s
Aroodha will cause distress in the Dasa of Lagna.
The native’s mother will also be troubled while his
father will be bereft of happiness. The 8th lord in
the ascendant in the company of, or in aspect to
Rahu, will cause (premature) danger to wife, if
this yoga is unaspected by Jupiter. One will nearly
escape death in Lagna dasa if Jupiter is in a trine

while the 8th lord is in an angle - both counted
from Lagna. In addition, it denotes utter poverty
and difficulties to father. Marriage to father’s
brother and troubles among kinsfolk will also
result in Lagna dasa, referred to above. In the
dasa of 2nd Rasi, the native will incur financial
destruction.

813-815. Ketu with Mars: If birth be in
Vipra Kala of Kamala Nadiamsa in Pisces ascen-
dant, as Ketu is conjunct the 2nd lord, the native
in the 2nd Rasi dasa will have his sacred thread
ceremony. His education will also commence in
this Dasa. Yet as a result of this yoga, his life will
be miserable. His maternal uncle’s children will
be displaced as a result of a Revolution. In the
native’s birth country, change of ruler will occur
due to agitation(?)

Notes: Vipra Kala in Kamala Nadiamsa in
Pisces extends from 20 deg. 48’ to 20 deg. 51’ of
space.

When such space ascends, Ketu should be
in association with Mars. Then the results for
Aries Dasa (KCD) as mentioned in the text will
apply.

Budha Nadi mostly uses Kala Chakra Dasa
for this Nadiamsa in Pisces ascendant.

829-8311/2. In the dasa of the 6th Rasi, the
native will be grieved on account of the death of
his daughter. If the Sun is exalted, then in the end
of the said dasa, the marriage of the native’s
daughter will take place. The last one-third part
will prove quite auspicious. His son will get mar-
ried; his friends will be greatly happy. The Sun’s
exaltation effects will be specially felt in the last
one third part of the dasa. In the initial part of the
dasa, good effects will go in vain, while in the
beginning and end of the middle part and in the
third part, enemies of the native will be destroyed.
Inthe middle of the last one-third part of the dasa,
the native will earn fame and prosperity.

838-8411/2. In the dasa of the 8th Rasi, one
born in Lakshmi Yoga will obtain prosperity for
his children, but in the last one third part there
will be great danger. The 8th lord in exaltation
Rasi and debilitation Navamsa will give medium
life span, provided he is in aspect to 8th lord. A
death will takeplace among his kinsmen and his
children will be troubled. In adverse months, his
wife will experience problems to her health, but

will instantly recover. His children will become

842-843. The Lakshmi Yoga caused by
Rahu’s position ia the 10th will greatly endanger
Pisces Lagna native in the dasa of Sagittarius
Rasi. [n the dasa ruled by a trine from Sagittarius,
he will nearly die.

Notes: One kind of Lakshmi Yoga is
produced by Rahu for a Pisces native by his cing
in the 10th in Sagittarius. Simultaneously Saturn
should be in Aries, with Leo Navamsa. (See sloka
783 supra).

The said Lakshmi Yoga apart from giving
wealth serves to greatly endanger, the native. The
Kala Chakra Dasa suggested is of Sagittarius
which contains Rahu.

It is also further suggested that the dasas of
Aries and Leo (Saturn’s Rasi and Navamsa posi-
tions) could also nearly kill the subject.

847-849. Nirmala Nadiamsa: One born in
the first half of this Nadiamsa in Libra ascendant,
will be a Soodra, be ever happy and will be the
ninth issue of the family. If Venus joins Saturn
while the latter is in Capricorn Navamsa, and the
Moon joins Rahu, birth will be in a place sur-
rounded by forests. The same effect will occur if
the ascendant being Libra is in Nirmala Nadiamsa
and is aspected by the Sun. Further such a subject
will live in a town.

Notes: From now on, Libra Lagna with Nir-
mala Nadiamsa commences. The Nadi’s name is
left blank. Apparently it relates to Sukra Nadi.

Nirmala Nadiamsa extends thus: from 13
deg. 24’ to 13 deg. 36’ in a movable sign; from 16
deg. 24’ to 16 deg, 36’ in an immovable sign, and
from 28 deg. 24’ to 28 deg. 36’ of a common sign.

Its first half in Libra extends 13 deg. 24’ to
13 deg. 30’. The first half covers both Vipra &
Kshatriya Kaalas.

The second half is from 13 deg. 30’ to 13 deg.
36° in Libra.

850-8501/2. Street of birth: For Nirmala
Nadiamsa, former half, birth will be in north-
south street. The house concerned will be north-
facing. In case of the second half of this nadiamsa,
the street concerned will be east-west, in
Mahanadi region, in a city. The native of second
half will be the fifth issue, or the third, and will be
exceedingly fat. The former half will give an auspi-
cious (pleasing) appearance.

861-866. If Mars is in the 9th house for a
native of Libra in Nirmalamsa, there will be in-
crease of good furtunes. The native will be lustful
and be learned in religious codes, meritorious
acts and ancient sacred texts. He will be inter-
ested in wicked people, be given to anger and will
hate his co-born. For some part of his life he will
indulge in thieving. In his youth, he will suffer
from disorders of blood vessels. He will worship
Lord Siva’s idol.

For one born in the first half of Nirmalamsa,
there will be happiness from father in the middle
age of life. He will be ever intent upon doing
charitable acts. He will have enmity with his
kiasmen and in his old age he will obtain huge
fortunes through his son, and be happy.

The father of the native (born in first half of
Nirmalamsa) will have ten or twelve brothers. He
will be happy with one brother. Two of the native’s
paternal uncles will have sons while one will have
_ ho sons born to him, be emaciated and troubled
by great (serious) diseases due to the sins of his
previous birth

874-877. The native will have two wives, be
prosperous but will do sinful acts. if Saturn is in
the 5th house, or Sagittarius or its trines, the
native’s grand-father will be troubled by
planetary evils, and by a weapon like dagger, will
indulge in thieving, and will swallow the wealth of
his kinsmen. Because of these evils, he will incur
grief on account of danger to his children. Wor-
ship and prayers offered to the Sun-God will
grant good health to the said relative, and one
(long) living son and happiness thereof. This ap-
plies to the native born in Nirmala Nadiamsa of
Libra ascendant, having Saturn in the 11th, falling
in exalted or own Navamsa, being in the company
of Venus. (That is Saturn and Venus in Leo, while
Saturn is in Libra, Capricorn or Aquarius
Navamsa.)

878-880. His grandfather will enter royal
service, be valorous, will have two wives, be lustful
and incur grief on account of his children. His
children will be destroyed due to his sins. How-
ever, after a long interval he will have birth of a
(long) living son and be happy. He will be rich
from birth. In the middle age, he will be grieved,
and will incur windy disorders, Due to his sins to
his kinsmen he will incur royal displeasure.

Nirmalamsa of Libra Lagna, father’s younger

his Janma Dasa, there will be destrucion of his
kinsmen. Alternatively such destruction can

884-887, One born in Nirmalamsa will have
destruction of his paternal uncles. His father will
in his middle age acquire wisdom of agreat order.
In spite of having grains (i.e. eating comforts) and
wealth, he (the father) will be sickly. He will be
famous and happy. With the blemish of Mars in
the 9th house (birth in Nirmalamsa in Libra
Lagna), there will be troubles and fear in his home
(of birth). Right from the days of his being in his
mother’s womb, his father would be troubled by
diseases. If birth be in the 2nd half of Nirmala
Nadiamsa, with Mars in the 9th house, his father
will have an untimely death, while additional
results are: evils to paternal uncle’s son and great
destruction of kinsmen, For birth in the first half
of Nirmala Nadiamsa (with Mars in the 9th
house) of Libra or Lagna, there will be illness to
father which will however be speedily cured.

888-891. Libra Lagna - Grand father:
Saturn, who is the lord of the house of paternal
grand-father, for Libra Lagna, joining Mercury
and occupying Libra Navamsa will give comforts
(health, happiness etc.) to the native’s grand-
father. He will also prove auspicious to the
native’s elder brother. The native’s grand- father
will be famous and will have many brothers if
Rahu is in the 2nd house (in Scorpio) and the Sun
in the 10th house. Further his childhood would be
grief-ridden and marked by penury. He will be
emaciated. He will travel in the southern and
northern parts of the country. After marriage he
will become prosperous and celebrate birth of
children. He will be a wise man. These results are
applicable to the grand father of a person born in
Nirmala Nadi Amsa of Libra Ascendant.

892-893. The said grand-father would attain
good fortunes in the end of his youth and would
go to areas surrounded by forests and be happy.
He will have two preceptors, be respectable, or-
thodox as prescribed by Sastras and be religiously
disposed. However for some part of his life he
would take to unorthodox means and then would
tread virtous path. These are when Saturn, the
significator of paternal grandfather for Libra as-
cendant is with two benefics.

Notes: In sloka 892, ‘Kuladwaye’ appears
which denotes that the native will adopt two
religions. In another version ‘Gurudwaye’ ap-
pears which indicates that the native will have two
preceptors.

Seeing the results of the native of being or-
thodox as prescribed by Sastras, I have adopted
‘Gurudwaye’ in translation.

"For some part of life...he will take to unor-

fed Afait 222 1) thodox means” may also mean adopting another

inferior religion, for some.

898-902. Elder brother: For one born in the
first half of Nirmala Nadiamsa in Libra ascen-
dant, with Mercury, Saturn and Venus in the 11th
house, elder brother will enjoy great prosperity
## Page 108

S4 Chandra Kala Nadi

and will be skillful in two languages. His com-
plexion will be blood-red and appearance auspi-
cious (pleasing). He will have two wives and will
enjoy mundane pleasures. He will have many
sisters. The elder brother (of the Nirmalamsa
native) will have various business activities. He
will always honour his father’s words, will worship
God and protect (honour) Brahmins. He will be
happy with limited number of children and
limited wealth. He will live in three cities. He will
deal with gold and other articles imported from
different islands (ic. foreign countries). When
the native will be in his Sampath Dasa (second
dasa) the elder brother will amass wealth, and will
in addition become widely famous. There will be
mercy of Goddess Lakshmi showering on the
family.

909-910. The number of coborns (for the
first half of Nirmala Nadiamsa, Libra Lagna) will
correspond to the dots contributed by Mars in his
Ashtaka Varga. Two of the sisters will be endowed
with long-lives and will be fortunate and be
devout housewives. Rest will be destroyed ac-
cording to wise men. The native (of the said
Nadiamsa) will gain wealth through his elder
brother. There will be increased prosperity in the
family. Birth in Nirmala Nadiamsa will give com-
forts and happiness.

Note: The word "Sumangali" is a specific
word in Sanskrit denoting a woman who is a
fortunate and devout housewife, with a long living
husband, the stress however being on husband’s
longevity.

The last line of sloka 909/10 only reters to
Nirmala Nadiamsa but not as to in which half the
birth should be. However this belongs to first half
of the Nadiamsa.

911-914. For birth in first half of Nirmala
Nadiamsa, Libra Lagna, the lord of the 3rd, ie.
Jupiter, in Vargothama as the 7th house is bereft
of a malefic, denotes that the native’s elder
brother will be long-lived and be endowed with
abundant fortunes and happiness. The native’s
sister will be somewhat troubled. She will lose
children and will have many daughters. The said
native’s two sisters will be blessed with children,
be fortunate and happy. Another sister will be
grief-stricken and will suffer poverty. There will
be in all four sisters.

dant (not necessarily Libra), the Sun in Pisces,

917-919, The mother of the native of second
half Nirmala Nadiamsa of Libra Lagna will be
endowed with virtues and coborns. The native will
not derive happiness both from his mother and
father. He will have long-living coborns and be
blessed with children. Before evils (death) occur-
ring to his father, his mother will pass away.

ee oe Se eae er

920. Death of mother a take place if
Saturn is in Scorpio occupying Libra Navamsa. In
the third round of his transit when Saturn reaches
Libra Navamsa, destruction (death) of mother
will take place.

Notes: The sloka is not very clear. The first
line seems to suggest early death of mother of a
Libra lagna native who has Saturn in Scorpio
Rasi and Libra Navamsa. The second line seems
to suggest that third round of Saturn, after cross-
ing his natal position twice, will bring danger to
mother, when he reaches Libra Navamsa. In the
third round he can reach Libra Navamsa more
than once. Hence the meaning is not very clear. It
is left to the ingenuity of the reader.

921-924. At the junction of Vipat Tara
(third) dasa mother will die when Saturn in the
first round is in Gemini. The native’s father will
die in the middle of the native’s Vipat Tara dasa.
Father’s death will be untimely (Apamrithyu).
Propitiations may prove helpful. If birth be in the
first half of Nirmala Nadiamsa, then the father
will be long-lived. He may live upto the 18/20th
year of age of the native. The native’s father will
fall sick immediately after the birth (of the native
in first half of Nirmala Nadiamsa) while evils to
kinsmen are also possible.

Notes: "Junction of Vipat Tara Dasa (3rd
dasa)" in this case may mean the period between
2nd and 3rd dasa, as mother is said to predecease
father. Also please note death of father is denoted
in the middle of Vipat Tara dasa. So there is no
question of mother passing away at the end of
Vipat Tara Dasa, i.e. junction of 3rd and 4th dasas.
## Page 110

$6 Chandra Kala Nadi

In sloka 922, the words "trines thereof
should relate to "Saturn in Gemini vide sloka 921".

In sloka 923, long life to father is predicted.
In the same breathsthg native is said to be 18/20
years of age at the time of father’s death. We do
not know as to what will be age of the father at the
time of the native’s birth. Hence these may not
mutually contradict.

927-930. Jupiter in the 7th house for birth
in first half of Nirmala Nadiamsa, Libra Lagna:
Should Jupiter be in the 7th house (in Aries) for
native of first half of Nirmala Nadi Amsa in Libra
Lagna, he will be fond of mythological accounts
(Satkatha), and be learned in ancient Sastras and
Puranas. He will perform sacrifices, dig wells and
will do other acts of charity. He will be charitable
in general and will be of sacrificial nature. He will
attain fortunes through grandfather, be a great
donor and be happy. His education will com-
mence in his fifth year. In the third year he will

have fear of fever (of some consequence). In his
childhood, he will be troubled by weak digestion
and will incur danger from chicken-pox. To ward
off these evils, the Moon god be propitiated and
donation of cobra’s image be made. Then sound
health and great happiness will prevail.

931-932, Nirmala Nadiamsa - Libra Lagna
- Lifespan: For one born in the first half of Nir-
mala Nadiamsa, long life will come to pass if
Jupiter in the 7th house (Aries) is in Vargothama
Navamsa. Infantile evils to lifespan, if any, will be
countered in respect of such a native just as
thunderbolt is resisted by the hill. One born in the
second half will face infantile evils to lifespan. If
however he survives (due to other combinations)
he will have a long life. One born in first half of
this Nadiamsa will have eyes resembling a lotus
petal.

933-937. Nirmala Nadiamsa - Other
results: (Birth in first half - continued) - He will
wed a woman who is gentle in nature. He will be
virtuous (or saintly). He will be fond of sweet and
sour juices. He will incur windy and phlegmatic
imbalances. He will also have bilious excesses. He
will have two names. He will be truthful in disposi-
## Page 111

Deva Keralam 87

tion. Being libertine, he will sometimes commit
adultery.

He will enjoy material pleasures and be dear
to king, if Venus joins Saturn. In addition, he will
sexually unite with prostitutes, will regret later
on and will win over his senses. He will be pleased
with his elders. His friends will be limited in
number. He will be thin and will have a long body.
He will be pure, highly intelligent and somewhat
timid. He will follow religious codes and be
charitable. He will dabble in Dharma Sastras.

Should Venus join (the ascendant having
Nirmala Nadiamsa, first half), the native will be
proficient and learned (in ancient Sastras) and
will be a true philosopher (knowing the nature of
Brahman). He will be endowed with pure con-
science. He will be a skilful speaker, be somewhat
troubled by diseases, be given to anger, will have
a good residence and be rich.

938-9491/2. If the Moon is debilitated, oc-
cupying Kamala Nadiamsa and be in the company
of Rahu, the native will not be stable in disposi-
tion. Moreover, he will be somewhat a dunce. The
Moon conjunct Rahu brings to the said Libra
native fear from king and thieves. For one born in
Nirmala Nadiamsa of Libra, there will be grief on
account of coborn in middle age. If the Sun oc-
cupies the 10th house,the native will bathe in
Sethu (or sacred rivers), will attain abundant
meritorious fruits by bathing in the Ganges, and
will undertake a pilgrimage to Sethu (in the
South). In the middle of his life he will perform
good deeds and construct tanks and gardens.
During his pilgrimage he will donate a tawny cow
and will attain Punya (religious merits) and will
do cahritable acts on the banks of the Ganges. He
will help others to visit Ganges etc. and will be
happy. He will be endowed with a long life with
the Sun in the 10th house with Libra Navamsa.
Thus the results be understood to be materializ-
ing in the dasa of the 10th lord.

Lagna Lord’s dasa in its second half will
bring prosperity. In the dasa of Lagna lord, he will
attain a great deal of religious merits and wide
fame thereof. In Sampth Dasa (2nd dasa in se-
quence), coinciding with twelfth or twenty-third
year, in the month of Chaitra (one of the months
in Spring), he will get married to a girl coming
from the eastern part of his country. If the 7th lord
isin Aries Navamsa, for a person born in Nirmala
Nadiamsa of Libra Lagna. The learned say that in
this context, the natal Moon of the spouse will be
in Aries or one of its trines. He will firmly support
his marriage (but) will have a remarriage after
some interval, in his twenty-fourth year, in the
dasa of the Lagna lord. There will be destruction
of wife in his 30th year and immediately thereafter
(?) remarriage will occur.

Notes: Kamala Nadiamsa in Scoprpio ex-
tends from 24 deg. 0’ to 24 deg. 12’ in which space
the Moon is required to be. She should also
conjoin Rahu. Then the Libra native will be un-
## Page 112

88 Chandra Kala Nadi

stable in disposition and will have fear from kings
(or government) and thieves.

950-9521/2. Indra Yoga: ‘For a Libra Lagna
native, Venus placed in the 11th house, joining the
lord of the 9th/4th and begetting Cancer Navamsa
causes Indra Yoga. As a result the native will
enjoy material pleasures and be dear to the king.
He will follow the path prescribed by his religion
(or Sastras) and be endowed with much wealth.
He will attain religious merits (by constructing)
temple boundaries and towers and be happy. In
Phaladhyaya of Yoga Nadi, results have been told
in detail (in this regard).

Notes: Indra yoga forms thus for a Libra
native. Venus should be in the sign Leo. He
should join Saturn and Mercury in Cancer
Navamsa. Result mentioned here apart from
those under Slokas 960 and 963-9651/2 will
materialize in this regard. This combination is
taken from Yoga Nadi by the author.

953-959. Saturn placed in the 11th house will
give two Wives and virtuous children to a Libra
native. Three daughters will be long-lived while
there will also be four sons. In his old age, he will

Sh SEE RA

incur woes due to loss of progeny. He will get
happiness from father in Janma dasa (first dasa)
and wealth in the third year. There will be happi-
ness in the first year of his birth following the
marriage of an older brother. When Saturn
reaches the sign identical with 8th lord’s Navamsa
Rasi, or its trines, there will be evils (to the native)
and his mother in his birth country. There will also
be mental agony to kinsmen, particularly on ac-
count of royal wrath. When Saturn reaches the
birth sign (Libra) there will be great danger to
father in the dasa indicated by the lord of Navam-
sa holding the 9th lord. In the first dasa, the
native’s and his father’s prosperity will increase.
These results for birth in first part of Nirmala
Nadi Amsa of Libra Lagna have been elaborately
narrated in Dasa results chapter of Yoga Nadi.

963. Second Lord’s Dasa - Nirmalamsa:
One born in this Nadaimsa’a first half will con-
front danger of (timely) death in the end of 2nd
lord’s Dasa. The probable months will coincide
with the Sun in transit in Scorpio, Sagittarius or
Capricorn.

964-9651/2. Indra yoga (continued): One
born in Nirmala Nadiamsa with this yoga will face
death in his 60th year. In his 54th year, his elder
brother will pass away. In the native’s 27th year,
the said elder brother may contract fatality but
remedies will help. The native in his 9th year (one
sixth of 54) will incur many troubles and physical
ailments. After death he will attain good heavens.
These are for birth in Nirmalamsa.

Notes: For Indra Yoga see sloka 950-9501/2
as well as sloka 960 supra.

971-972, Emaciated Body: A movable as-
cendant rising at birth, with Scorpio Navamsa, as
Mars is in debilitation and the Moon is in the 3rd
house will cause an emaciated body, tuberculosis
and emission of blood in cough (Haemoptysis).

973-97712. Vishnu yoga: The Sun in Aries
with Leo Navamsa while Jupiter joins Ketu (else-
where) will cause Vishnu yoga. Such a native will
prosper and will follow the codes prescribed for
a Vaishnative. Mars in ascendant while Saturn is
in the 12th house will also produce the said yoga.
The native’s childhood will be marked by grief.
There will be penury upto the age of 27. He will
have an emaciated body, be dark in complexion
and be endowed with an auspicious appearance.
He will realize the Supreme Spirit (theologian
etc.), will be wealthy, heroic, intelligent and fond
of promoting quarrels. He will be dear to king. He
will have two sisters and will also have younger
brothers. Venus causing Raja yoga, placed in the
11th house and occupying Aquarius Navamsa will
give younger and elder co-borns and make the
native libertine.

Notes: Vishnu Yoga described here applies
toa movable ascendant (Aries, Cancer, Libra and
Capricorn). In any case the Sun should be in
Aries, between 13 deg. 20’ and 16 deg. 40’ while
Jupiter is with Ketu elsewhere. Results are
prosperity etc.

Another kind of Vishnu Yoga for a movable
ascendant is formed by Mars being in ascendant
While Saturn isin 12th, The results of such Vishnu
Yoga are grief etc. as discussed in the text. Also
see sloka 980.

978-983. Avastha yoga: Upto the age of 27
the native will have a troubled life. Afterwards
there will be Rajayoga; particularly after the age
of 30 more favourable results will occur.

For one born with Kutila Nadiamsa of Libra
Lagna, with Vishnu yoga, there will be a troubled
(or unfortunate) sister while one will predecease
her husband. In the Kshema Dasa (4th Dasa) the
native’s will become widely famous. Vishnu yoga
is also caused by Bright half Moon placed in
Virgo. Such a native will be ever fond of listening
to accounts filled with jokes. He will be poor in
childhood and will incur grief. He will be skilful
in reading.others’ thoughts, will cheat his friends,
be skilful in his work, be wealthy, will cause
obstacles to the doings of his enemies, and will be
a tale-bearer. He will be a hindrance to others if
in the said Raja yoga, malefics are in the ascen-
dant.

Notes: The sub-heading given in the text as
"Avastha Yoga" is not appropriate.

Hasyavastha of Moon is often referred.
This seems to be a confused term.

986-9941/2. One born in Cancer ascendant
with Scorpio Navamsa will have a warm body. He
will heve phlegmatic imbalances and will be
somewhat troubled by diseases. Due to excessive
observance of (religious) vows and fasting, he will
be troubled by bilious disorders and cough. As a
remedy (to overcome these ills) he should wor-
ship an image of the zodiac, to be drawn on
husk-filled ground. The names of Nakshatras in-
cluding Abhijit be written on the said space and
the Grahas (planet) be worshipped as prescribed
in the Vedas. The astrologer should be honoured
with gifts. Then the patient will get rid of the
disease. The said illness will occur in kshema
Dasa (4th Dasa) on account of dishonouring
Lord Siva (in the previous birth). The zodiacal
image (as above) be worshipped for two or three
weeks, with Prayers and donations. In the
presence of God (or in temples), worship of
Lakshmi and recitation of Mrityunjaya Japa be
performed. Nava Grahas be worshipped in one’s
residence as prescribed. Then comforts and
sound health will prevail. In the absence of these,
recitation of Mrityunjaya in a shrine of Lord Siva
be done and the image of Lord Siva (Siva Linga)
be installed to overcome the cough with emission
of blood (ic. Haemoptysis). Some health and
prosperity can be acquired by donation of pots of
honey.

997-1002. Exessive Limbs & other effects:
One born in Vishnu yoga will have a virtuous
child, which is the 4th or 5th in order, when the
4th lord is in debilitation and the significator
(i.e.Jupiter) is aspected by Rahu, (for birth in
Kutila Nadiamsa of Libra Lagna). One of his
children may have excessive limbs, or be born
with teeth. The native’s elder brother will face
destructiun, be sickly, will marry a barren lady
and will face obstacles in obtaining progeny. The
native’s younger co-born will get a virtuous wife
and will be prosperous. The native will be widely
famous on account of his brothers and will have
many children and much wealth. In his 16th year,
there will be danger to father coinciding with
Vipat Dasa (3rd Dasa), when Saturn is in the Rasi
denoted by the Navamsa occupied by Lagna
Lord, or its trines’ Destruction of his friends and
masters will also follow. Later on, in the sub-
period of Mercury in the Kshema Dasa (4th
Dasa), ascendancy will dawn on the native.

be aspected by Rahu is the lord of the 5th, vide
sloka 997 above.

1003-1009. Kutila Nadiamsa - Libra Lagna:
There will be Raja yoga effects in the eigth year
with Venus in the 11th house. When Saturn in
transit reaches Leo, or Gemini (i.e. Gemini/Leo),
the native will be troubled by a dangerous disease.
There will be great fear in the bhukti of the Sun.
To overcome these evils, gifting be resorted to. In
the (sub) periods of the Sun and Moon in Kshema
Dasa (4th Dasa), great danger will visit the native.
If he survives, he will be subjected to troubles like
destruction of prosperity. Death will result if
Rahu, playing a malefic role (as death-dealing
planet), reaches the Riksha Sandhi (in transit). In
the (sub) periods of the Sun and the Moon, when
Saturn retrogrades in the end of Leo, the native
will die on account of lung tuberculosis. The years
41, 38 or 36 of the native’s life may prove fatal.
32nd or 36th year may bring untimely end. If he
survives, the years after 41 will give Raja yoga
effects.

Notes: For Kutila Nadiamsa, see notes
under slpka 130-131 supra.
Riksha Sandhi is the junction of any of the

following pairs of Rasis in the Zodiac: Cancer-
Leo; Scorpio-Sagittarius and Pisces- Aries.

1010. Naraka Yoga: The first line does not
convey any clear meaning. It states: One born in
Vishnu yoga will for five nights perform Anush-
tana (religious ceremonies). Viththa is money
which makes no sense. The second line means:
After death he will go to hell or will be fallen and
will attain mean worlds/birth.

1020-1025. One born in Indra yoga with the
Moon in Swathi Nakshatra (Indra Daivarksha)
and in Capricorn Navamsa will be dear to king,
libertine, eloquent in speech and highly intel-
ligent. He will have an older co-born and many
friends. He will increase his fame through his
coborns. If the 9th house has a malefic, in the said
yoga, the native’s father will have professional
misunderstandings with his kinsmen. Evils to the
parents of the native be also predicted. Both these
would occur when the native was in his mother’s
womb, i.e. before his birth. In the native’s first
year during Janma Dasa (first Dasa), agony to
father will occur. Good will occur to the native’s
paternal uncle and kinsmen. There will be happi-
ness on account of birth of children amd the like
in the house of paternal uncle. In the native’s
family the third son will do acts of bravery. The
native will be somewhat ill-disposed to his
kinsmen and will steal their wealth.

Notes: "Indra Daivarksha" denote Swathi
and Anuradha. These Nakshatras have Lord
Indra as Adhidevatha, ruling deity. Swathi 2nd
quarter falls in Capricorn Navamsa while
Anuradha has no such Navamsa. Hence in the
present context, Swati is relevant.

native’s father will indulge in foolish deeds, and
will in his middle age incur agony. He will also
suffer from complaints of weak digestion. To ward
off such blemish, remedies (as prescribed by
Sastras) and donation of an image of the Zodiac
be done.

1043-1046. Eye Disorders: In the sub
periods of the 6th lord in Janma Dasa, one will
incur eye-troubles which will (however) be imme-
diately curable. This may coincide with the first
year of birth. The Sun joining Venus in Sth will
give eye troubles to the native in childhood in case
of Indra Nadiamsa. If the ascendant lord is in the
company of Rahu, ulcers on head or shank, or in
the heart, or facial diseases will occur, in
childhood. These can be countered by donation
of a cobra’s image. As a result, disorders of eyes
can also be avoided, acquiring healthy eyes.

1047-10491/2. Fortunate etc: One born with

to enjoy pleasures. He belongs to a fortunate
family. If Venus is in Indra Nadiamsa, the native
of Libra will have two wives. So also his elder
brother. The native will have only one sister who
will incur difficulties in her middle age. If Venus
in Indra Nadiamsa joins Saturn, the native will
have two sisters, with a long and happy marital life
and daughters. Onc of the sisters will have an
adopted son.

Rae Heda Sears FH 12048

1052-1056. Dasa results: Following are the
effects of the 2nd half of the Dasa (of 12th lord)
for the Indra yoga native. In the sub period of
Jupiter, in the Dasa of the 12th lord (from Indra
Lagna?), there will occur evils to father, but ex-
tension of prosperity to the native’s co-born.
(Evils to father will occur) when Venus/Mars is
combust and relief will follow when Taurus comes
to be occupied by a benefic. If Jupiter and Venus
conjoin or mutually be in aspect, in transit, the
good effects due to transit will be nullified. In the
months of the Sun’s transit in malefic Rasis, and
when Venus/Mars is combust, there will be dif-
ficulties (to the Libra native, with Indra yoga and
Indra Nadiamsa), physical illness, mental wor-
ries, financial loss and head-ache.

Notes: These 5 slokas have certain effects
to be linked with certain transits etc. But we find
that the text needs a careful assortment in some
respects while dealing with these five slokas.

(a) Indra Lagna is used in sloka No. 1052.

There is no such term. Perhaps the text hints at
Libra Lagna and Indra Nadiamsa. Then the 12th
## Page 120

lord (i.e. Vyavadheesa) is Mercury whose Dasa is
referred to by the author.

(b) The combustion of Venus/Mars should
refer only to danger to father, not to prosperity of
co-born.

(c) The first line of sloka No. 1054 refers to
improvement possible to troubled father.

(d) Venus/Mars combustion etc. referred to
in sloka No. 1055 relates to the bad effects due to
occur to the native.

(e) Insloka 1054, Venus - Jupiter connection
is brought in to nullify the other good effects due
to other beneficial transits. This may be because
they are lords of 6th and 8th for Libra Lagna and
their association is not productive of good effects
in given cases.

1074-10751/2. Sub-period of 6th lord: In the
2nd dasa, the sub- period ruled by the sixth lord
will cause bewilderment and physical troubles.
This applies to the Indra yoga native. These ef-
fects will come to pass when the Sun transits
malefic Rasis in the zodiac. The sub periods of
Ketu and Venus (in 2nd dasa) will also give effects
as above (i.e. like the 6th lord’s sub period). The
junctions of 2nd and 3rd dasas will cause troubles
according to learned men.

1076-1079. Great danger, Great -fortunes
etc, - In case of Indra yoga, note the dispositor of
the planet that is in aspect to the Moon. If the said
dispositor is in Leo Navamsa or Leo Rasi, the
effects are great fortunes and Raja Yoga (giving
## Page 122

Y8 Chandra Kala Nadi

position, wealth etc.). If Venus becomes a malefic
(by conjunction, aspect etc.), the Indra Yoga na-
tive in Rahu bhukti (of 2nd dasa) will face great
dangers. In Moon’s bhukti he will have fear of
dangerous fevers. To overcome the evils, the
Moon God should be worshipped and donation
of silver be made. When the 8th lord’s sub period
is in operation, malefic transiting the Ascendant
will cause difficulties to one’s kinsfolk.

1080-1082. Rahu in Vargothama: One born
in Indra Yoga with Rahu in the 2nd house in
Vargothamamsa, will be devoted to enjoyments.
He will suffer from illness during his childhood.
Fame and wealth will come to him in his middle
age. During his old age, he will be in the grip by
debts and will steal others’ wealth. In general he
will be proud of his lineage and will be famous
among his men, will be troubled by diseases, and
will be disposed charitably. He will have a notable
position with the king, and be highly honourable.
He will be famous and respectable among
physicians.

1084-10891/2. Effects for other dasa periods:
One born in Indra Nadiamsa with Indra Yoga, will
be happy in the dasa of Lagna lord. In the end of
the 8th lord’s sub period under the 9th lord’s
major period, danger and evils to mother be
forecast. So also in the sub period and sub-sub
period ruled by the Moon, in the dasa, second in
sequence. Danger from thieves and poison apart
from physical diseases will come to pass in the sub
period of Mars coinciding with Sun’s transits in
adverse, or weak Rasis. In the sub period of the
10th lord under the major rulership of the
eleventh lord, the native’s father will be initially
troubled by diseases and will be later on cured. In
the dasa and also sub period of the eleventh lord,
there will be obstructions to one’s income and
acquisition of a disposition marked by repug-
nance and hatred - all these due to blemishes
caused by Rahu. Troubles to coborn, and great
fear to self will strike in the sub period of the 11th
lord in eleventh lord’s dasa, or the initial phase of
it, will be somewhat distressful. In the dasa of the
10th lord, one born in Indra yoga will be ever
happy due to children (either birth of children, or
fame brought by children depending upon the
age in which this dasa occurs).

1092-10951/2. During the dasa of the second
lord, diseases will strike the native’s spouse and
progeny. The children of the Indra Yoga native
will have widespread business activities (in
general). In the beginning or end of the dasa of
the 2nd lord, or in the intervals of the planets
occupying the 2nd house, there will be fear of
death while great danger will strike in the dasa
that is the sixth in sequence. These apply to birth
in Indra Yoga and when Venus is placed in Indra
Nadiamsa. The native will die in the month of
Chaitra (with the Sun’s movement in Aries) and
will attain an excellent rebirth. These effects are
as per Yoga Nadi for one born in Indra Nadiamsa.
Such a native will attain prosperity after 20th year
of age. The length of his life will be 62 years.

1096-10971/2. Saturn - Yenus conjunction
for Seetala Nadiamsa: One born in Seethala
Nadiamsa will be endowed with a fair complexion
and auspicious (pleasing) appearance, if Saturn
is placed in the Shashtiamsa entitled Sudha and
be in a movable Rasi. One born in this Nadiamsa
(Seethala) in Pisces ascendant while Saturn is
with Venus in the 5th house will have auspicious
appearance but be dark in complexion.

Notes: From now on Seethala Nadiamsa in
Pisces ascendant is discussed. This Nadiamsa
rules thus: from 10 deg. 48’ to 11 deg. ina movable
sign; from 19 deg. to 19 deg 12’ of an immovable
sing and from 25 deg. 48’ to 26 deg. of a common
sign.

(There is also Seethala Shashtiamsa, and
Susitala Nadiamsa. These three terms should be
understood according to circumstances.)

According to the first condition, Saturn
should be in one of the movable signs in Sudha
Shashtiamsa. This particular Shashtiamsa ex-
tends from 18 deg. to 18 deg. 30’ of an odd sign,
and from 11 deg. 30’ to 12 deg. of an even sign.
(Sudha is a benefic Shashtiamsa. Sudha means
nectar, ambrosia, name of the Ganges.)

In addition to Saturn being so, Pisces should
rise with Seethala Nadiamsa. As a result, the
native will be fair in complexion with charming
appearance.

In the second instance, Saturn-Venus should
be in Cancer tomake the native dark-bodied, with
auspicious looks.

1101-1104. Saturn - Ketu: In the above
mentioned position, if Saturn joins Ketu, during
the native’s childhood the father will be troubled
and will be quite emaciated. The native will not
have any after-born. His older brother will be
destroyed. The native will have his fortunes in a
foreign place. His father will have two sisters and
three wives, will be passionate, will have windy
imbalances (causing rheumatism, paralysis, ar-
theritis and the like), will make his fortunes
through his own efforts, will have conveyances
carried by men (i.e. palanquins etc.), will incur
many difficulties due to sins committed against
Vaishnavites apart from incurring royal wrath.

1105-11071/2. Venus - Ketu: With these two
planets placed in Indra Nadiamsa in the company
of Saturn, while Saturn himself is in Seethala
Nadiamsa, the native’s father will hate Vaish-
navites. As a result, he will incur difficulties, and
will lose "villages", lands and wealth. Mental
agony to father will occur during the native’s
Janma (first) dasa as well as in the period prior to
native’s birth. Upto the native’s age of 3 yrs and 6
months, the father will face difficulties. Saturn in

eethala Nadiamsa (independent of Venus-Ketu)
will give difficulties to father till the native attains
fourth year of age. Later on, i.e. after the 4th year
till the end of Janma (first) dasa, the father will
enjoyprosperity.

Notes: Indra Nadiamsa rules from 21 deg.
48’ to 22 deg. of a movable sign; from 8 deg. to 8
deg. 12’ of an immovable sign; and from 6 deg. 48”
to 7 deg. of a common sign.

Both Venus and Ketu should be so close that
they are placed in one Nadiamsa (12’ of arc)
entitled Indra, as above. Additionally Saturn
should be in Seethala Nadiamsa.

1108-11161/2. Saturn in 5th: Saturn placed
in the Sth house in Seethala Nadiamsa will cause
distress to father, who will suffer from affections
of gums, fever, dysentery and be fear-struck.
During the native’s Janma (first) dasa, the native’s
father would be subjected to a great deal of men-
tal agony and perplexion. The native’s cobora will
die as they are born. He will sufffer from smallpox
and incur danger. The native’s father will be
troubled by (dangerous) fever if the Moon is in
blemished Nakshatras. Necessary propitiations
be done to ward off this evil. This is when Saturn
is in the Sth in Seethala Nadiamsa. By donation of
gingilee and an image of Lord Vishnu, the native’s
father will regain health. He will further earn
royal favours and will have destroyed enemies.
Some texts prescribe donation of clarified butter
(distinct from ghee or Ghrita) (in place of gin-
gilee), image of Lord Vishnu, and gold, following
which the prosperity of father will increase, and
he will regain sound health. By giving in donation
to a Daivagna (astrologer) four vessels made of
lead, filled with ghee, and just a Nishka of gold (a
golden coin of ancient evaluation), father’s health
will become normal, his poverty will instantly
vanish and he will be blessed by Goddess
Lakshmi.

1117- 11201/2. Venus in the 5th: If Venus is
in the 5th house along with two malefics, gold and

clarified butter be given away in charity when
Goddess Lakshmi will bless the native’s family.
There will be prosperity to the native’s father
after the native’s 5th year (i.e. from 6th year on-
wards) and ever-lasting happiness. In the 4th year
there will be some happiness while the Sth year
will give mixed results, both auspicious and in-
auspicious, to the native’s father. Due to sins
committed against Vaishnavites, the father will be
in difficulties on account of kings and ministers in
his birth place, during the time of the native’s
being in Janma (first) dasa. More specifically in
the middle of such dasa. During the native’s third
year of age, there will be fear of untimely death to
the father; later on till the end of the dasa in
question, happiness, and destruction of enemies
will accrue to father.

1124-11301/2. More about father and other
relatives: Saturn in the Sth house joining Venus
will give prosperity to father in the beginning and
concluding parts of the native’s first dasa. In the
birth country, prosperity to father will be limited,
while it will be abundant in foreign places. Saturn
in movement in Virgo during the native’s Janma
(first) dasa will give wealth (to father). While
Saturn reaches Virgo as Jupiter is moving in tran-
sit in Gemini, the native will have sacred thread
ceremony (Upanayana due to a Brahmin, called
Dwija, which gives him second birth). Marriage
to elder brother will occur during the native’s
Janma (first) dasa when Saturn is in Virgo, while
Jupiter moves in the end of Aries, or in Taurus.
During Janma dasa if Jupiter transits the sign
Aries, the native’s father will gain happiness. His
half brothers will acquire progeny. If Jupiter is
found moving in Pisces, the native will acquire
younger coborns. If Jupiter transits the end of
Pisces, or be in Aries, there will be evils to the
native’s elder sister. Saturn in Seethala Nadiamsa
will cause loss of coborn at a later date. The
husband of the native’s half sisiter will enter in
royal service.

1133-11352. Saturn in Seethala or
Mahamaari Nadiamsa: Saturn placed in
Seethala Nadiamsa or in Mahamaari Nadiamsa
[instead of Sthithau, the word Sanau appears in
another version] will give the native two sisters,
who will be long lived, and also two brothers. The
native will be worshippable. His step brothers will
(also) be long-lived. The native’s sister will obtain
dead children or be barren, but be happy (i.e. will
get progeny) after a long interval. In the native’s
second dasa, the husband of the native’s elder
sister will become wealthy. During the third part
of Sampath (2nd) dasa (i.e. in the last one third
part of the dasa in question), the brother-in-law
of the native will obtain happiness.

Notes: Mahamaari Nadiamsa is also known
as Mahamaaya Nadiamsa. Mahamaari in the
Southern part of India is noted as deity incharge
of small-pox, chicken-pox, cholera etc. Mahad-
hoothi is another name for this part.

Mahamaari Nadiamsa extends from 15 deg.
to 15 deg. 12’ of arc in a movable sign; from 14
deg. 48’ to 15 dég. in an immovable sign; and from
0 deg. 0” to 0 deg. 12’ of a common sign.

1136-11401/2. Saturn - Mars: If Saturn is in
the 7th house while Mars is in Mahaamaari
Nadiamsa, following effects will occur. During his
childhood, the native will be plagued by cholera
and will incur destruction of coborn. His maternal
grand- father will be long-lived. The native will
have two maternal uncles. One of them will be
destroyed (i.e. will die early) while one will be
long-lived. Evils to maternal uncle will come to
pass when Saturn in transit reaches the Rasiiden-
tical with the Navamsa position of ascendant lord,
or its trine. This will also bring grief to maternal
grand mother. In the 2nd dasa, for birth in
Seethalamsa when Saturn comes to the end of
Libra, or when he moves in Sagittarius, evils to
matenal grandfather will occur. During Saturn’s
transit of Virgo, the first dasa of the native will see
birth of children to maternal uncle. And also the
native’s step-sister will acquire progeny.

Notes: Cholera indicated in this part of the
text can also additionally mean small-pox, chick-
en pox etc. true to the name of the Nadiamsa Mars
is expected to be in.

1143-11461/2. Other Effects: When Saturn
reaches the Rasi identical with the Navamsa oc-
cupied by the 6th lord at birth, or its trine, the
native’s father will incur abundant grief on ac-
count of his friends. Father’s enemies will be

or when Saturn reaches the Rasi identical with the
Navamsa occupied by 6th lord or its trine. There

mental agitation. Lack of rains and occurrance of
drought will tear his country(?) Due to change of

prosperous.

1151-1155. Evil Rasis: According to the
learned in astrology, when Saturn is in Seethala
Nadiamsa, the evil Rasis (Kroora Rasis) and evil
months (Kroora Masas - based on the Sun’s tran-
sit) are: Cancer, Leo, Scorpio, Pisces, Aquarius
and Cancer. When Rahu, Ketu or Saturn come to
occupy such a Rasi, the native’s kinsfolk will be in
trouble. Grief to father, and mental agony to
mother etc. will come to pass when Saturn moves
in one of the above Rasis. Thus be understood the
effects of sub peiods of the malefic planets in the
major rulership of the dasa that is 2nd in se-
quence.

1156-1160. Other Effects: The said malefic
bhuktis will in addition cause physical ailments to
father and such other relatives and evils to one’s
kinsfolk. These are due to birth in Seethala
Nadiamsa with Saturn in the 5th house. In the sub
period of benefic planets (in the 2nd dasa), hap-
piness to father, and prosperity will come to pass.
In the 4th dasa, there will be specially effects of
Raja Yoga (to the native). After 24th year of age,
he will attain prosperity and widespread fame.
One born in Seecthala Shashtiamsa will have
Rajayoga effects if Jupiter (at birth) is in the 9th
house, or when in transit he comes to an
angle/trine. Acquisition of conveyances (like
palanquins etc) will also come to pass. After the
27th year, prosperity, acquisition of quadrupeds
and wealth will also take place. The native will
become widely famous through royal service, and
wil gain supreme positions.

and great danger. Cough and breathing disorders

1163-1166. 4th Dasa & Rahu Dasa: In the
sub period of Saturn, in Kshema (4th) dasa, there
will be destruction to friends and employers.
There will also be some fear out of fevers, but
happiness due to royal patronage will also occur.
For one born in Seethala Nadiamsa, with Moon
placed in Virgo, the middle portion of Rahu dasa
will give effects of Raja Yoga. He will gain aname
due to construction of colonies [in charity, not as
a professional builder] and will be intent upon
serving the king. During Rahu dasa, he will suffer
from diseases due to sins of causing evils to his
friends. Later on he will regain health. In the end
of Rahu dasa, he will incur some difficulties and
(yet) be happy. (That is, end of Rahu dasa will give
mixed results.)

1168. Raja yoga: For one born in Seethala

1194-11941/2. Kokila Nadiamsa (upto sloka
1206): For one born in Sagittarius ascendant, in
Kokila Nadiamsa, as Saturn is in the Sth house,
there will be no after-borns. His elder brother will
be destroyed. For birth in Kokila Nadiamsa, if
Saturn is placed in Aries, (in Sth) the native will
be lonely (i.e. he will be the only issue in the
family). He will be endowed with progeny and
friends.

Notes: Slokas 1194 to 1206 deal with birth
in Sagittarius. Kokila Nadiamsa also features in
this part of the text.

Kokila Nadiamsa extends from 21 deg. 24
to 21 deg. 36’ of a movable sign; from 8 deg. 24’ to
8 deg. 36’ of an immovable sign; and from 6 deg.
24 to 6 deg. 36’ of a common sign.

For birth in Kokila Nadiamsa in Sagittarius,
Saturn in 5th in Aries gives such effects as men-
tioned upto sloka 1197 infra.

1207-1211. Sagittarius Lagna, birth in
Dhaatha Nadiamsa, Saturn placed in Scorpio
(upto sloka No. 1218): One born in Sagittarius
Lagna’s Dhaatha Nadiamsa, having Saturn in
Scorpio will lose his father in childhood, will later
on lose his coborn. During his mid-life, there will
be destruction of his elder brother and his
prosperity will commence. He will have two
sisters one of whom will be long-lived, blessed
with progeny and happpiness. He will attain hap-
piness in childhood in one of the Andhra provin-
ces. Later on he will migrate to a different
province in service of a mean ruler. He will have
two wives, will have progeny and will have Amalaa
Yoga (i.e. a benefic in the 10th house, in Virgo).
He will attain palanquins due to his livelihood in
fields of Vedic lore. In the 4th dasa, he will get a
great deal of happiness, but in the middle portion,
there will be (heavy) expenditure. Happiness will
accrue to him in the 2nd half (of Kshema, or 4th
dasa). He will gain villages.

Notes: The heading ‘Vrischikarka Phalam’
should be ‘Vrischikarki Phalany which means ‘ef-
fects of Saturn in Scorpio’ conforming to the text
hereof,

Dhaatha Nadiamsa in Sagittarius ascendant
features. This Nadiamsa is not enlisted. The
relative slokas are 12 in number.

1212. Saturn in Davagni Shashtiamsa for
birth in Sagittarius Lagna, Nadiamisa as above:
The native will have windy imbalances if Saturn is

have two wives, be honourable, and will become
famous through royal service.

Notes: Davagni shashtamsa is a malefic one
extending from 16 deg. to 16 deg. 30’ of an odd
sign, and from 13 deg. to 13 deg. 30’ of an even
sign. Davagni means forest conflagration.

1214-1218. Dhaata Nadiamsa: Birth in
Dhaata Nadiamsa of Sagittarius, with Saturn in
Scorpio makes the native stout- bodied, highly
intelligent, (sometimes) foolish, and enjoy
pleasures. He will be given to anger but will in-
stantly cool off. In his 38th year he will get
prosperity, vehicles in 40th year or 42nd year, and
will enjoy Yoga (good position, wealth etc.) and
become famous. In his 5th dasa, there will be
danger to his wife. Many of his children will die
(untimely) while his eldest daughter will be long-
lived. He will incur abdominal disorders in
childhood. He will have two sisters and also step-
brothers. He will be honourable and devoted to
his father. Doubtlessly the Dhaathamsa native
will meet with obstacles in education. Rest of the
results be understooc from other sources.

1219. Aquarius Lagna - Guha Nadiamsa:
One born in the second half of Guha Nadiamsa
in Aquarius Lagna will be a Soodra (4th caste as
per Vedic prescriptions), be ever happy and be
second of the children born in the family.

in the text. Maybe that one line relates to Dhata
Nadiamsa in Sagittarius dealing with Saturn.

From now on the text deals with Aquarius,
an immovable sign. Guha Nadiamsa is the sub-
ject-matter in this ascendant.

Guha Nadiamsa is not enlisted in the three
sources available with us. From the discussions
in Sloka No. 1313, this is actually Dhruva Nadiam-
sa and may have been wrongly copied as "Guha".

1252-1253. Balarishta combinations (if any)
could be warded off by prayers in the Dasa of
Rahu, Sun, Moon etc. Reciting Mrityunjaya Japa
and giving away clothes etc. in charity will also

oe ame wes gq aes

meas FIGS cea A pce

| 1 eRe TI

1254-1255. One born i: the first one-third
part of first half of Guha Nadiamsa will have a
short life, and the one in second one- third (mid-
dle of the 3 parts) will be long-lived. And the one
born in the first one-third of second half of this
Nadiamsa will have a long life.

Notes. These two slokas need some
reconstruction for proper understanding.

Vasishta and Garga seem to have made each
half of Nadiamsa as 3 sub divisions, i.e. one
Nadiamsa has 6 parts. (This is only my assumption
as otherwise there is no authentic teaching about
a Nadiamsa being made into six sub divisions). In
which case the above rendering conveys some-
thing. Yet the words "Poorva Bhaga" in the first
line of Sloka 1255 are out of place.

Alternatively avoiding a debate whether a
Nadiamsa has six parts, we can simply form two
specific clues from-the above two slokas:

1. Guha Nadiamsa - first half: the native will
be short-lived.

2. Guha Nadi Amsa - Second half: the na-
tive will be long-lived.
## Page 138

"14

The second half of this Nadiamsa seems to
be better for life span, devoid of Balarishta, as
could bé seen in S. 1246 - 1247 above (Yavanas).
Similarly first half of this Nadiamsa gives poverty
and second half of riches (sloka 1261 infra).

1290. Third Dasa: In the native’s third dasa,
the step-brother’s son will beget prosperity and
become wealthy. During the last one third part of
Sampath (2nd) dasa, his brothers will acquire
children.

1291. Relative: The brother of the native’s
step-mother will be happy during his childhood.
Later on he will be troubled by poverty. He will
be endowed with progeny

1292-12921/2. "Her husband" (?) will be
gentle, endowed with calmness and will have
brothers and sisters. After a long interval he will
beget great happiness and will attain wealth
through coborn. She will be happy on account of
her children. He will be endowed with wealth and
grains.

female relative? Not the father of the native at
least. In the end dealing with old age, masculine
gender verb is used. Again to which relatives this
reference is being made is unclear.

lack even normal sleep. His body will be hot in
nature. He will (also) suffer from diseases caused
by worms and from itches. He will have two wives,
or even three. He will acquire progeny.

1313-13141/2. Dhruva Nadiamsa: In the
Nadiamsa entitled Dhruva, following resuits for
Aquarius Lagna be declared. The native’s elder
sister will be dear to her husband and will be
endowed with progeny. She will have grief on
account of coborn. The native of this Nadiamsa
with Saturn and Mars in the 3rd/6th will have such
an elder sister who will be ever troubled by dis-
eases and grief.

Notes: Dhruva Nadiamsa extends from 4
deg. 12’ to 4 deg. 24’ of a movable sign; from 25
deg. 36° to 25 deg 48’ of an immovable sign; and
from 19 deg. 12’ to 19 deg. 24’ of a common sign.

charitable (i.e. he will do good acts relating to old
temples etc).

1333-1335. Balarishta: One born in an im-
movable ascendant with Saturn in the 6th and the
Moor in the Znd will incur infantile mortality. If
he escapes, destruction of his father will follow. If
the Moon be simultaneously in Mrithavastha (in
extremis) death will strike in the sixth month
(from the time of birth). (In the absence of such
an end) death will be certain in the 3rd/6th year.
The Moon in the 6th (or Saturn in the 6th) while
Saturn (or the Moon) is in the 8th will bring
effects of infantile mortality. Alternatively evils
will strike the native’s parents and coborn.

1343-13451/2. Coborn: The 3rd lord Jupiter
in own sign, or in exaltation or in an angle from
Capricorn ascendant, will cause destruction of
older coborn, although the native may be en-
dowed with after-borns. He will have a sister who
will reside in a respectable abode and who will
contact infantile mortality, due to blemishes in
birth family. Evils to older and younger coborn
will (thus) be evident, according to sages. His
older coborn will have progeny.

only once it is meaningful.
