1359-1365. Dasa effects: In the sub period
of an afflicted planet during the main period of
the 8th lord, the native’s kinsmen will face danger
and the native will himself be diseased ina foreign
place. He will gain wealth in the concluding part
of the 2nd dasa and will have professional gains.
His third dasa will generally inflict troubles to his
wife and children, while the sub period of Saturn
thereof will give beneficial results. In the sub
period of Rahu in 3rd dasa, travels and financial
improvements will come to pass. Malefic periods
will cause troubles to coborn. In the 24th year the
native will face difficulties in dealing with others.
The middle one-third portion of Vipath (3rd)
dasa will cause difficulties due ot indigestion (i.e.
stomachial disorders). He will ever be blessed
with the mercy of Goddess Lakshmi (in general).
He will be the fifth issue, or the third or the fourth
(i.e. he will not be among the first two). When the
4th lord Mars is with Saturn, birth and dwelling
of the Kanthaa Nadiamsa native will be in north-
south spread street in the region of Maharnava.

1372-1376. Parents: If Mercury is in the
3rd/6th/8th house while Saturn is in the company
of or in aspect to the Sun, the native’s mother will
pass away in childhood, and a step-mother will
step in his life. His father will be long-lived and
will have secret sexual urges. There will be fifteen
or sixteen coborns to him (father). Eight of them
will be sisters two of whom will live in respectable
abodes. His paternal uncle will also be lorg-lived,
be endowed with progeny. One of them will have
many children, even out of whom female children
will exceed male children. The native’s first pater-
nal aunt will become a widow, but be long- lived.
Because of step-mother, the said aunt will worry
about children. Due to her own good fortunes, a
female child will be born to her after a long
interval.

1377-1378. Second Half - Kanthaa
Nadiamsa: Two of the native’s paternal uncles
will be long-lived. He will be troubled by a great

along with him. Details for first half of this

1379-1380. Mudgara Nadiamsa - Sagit-
tarius ascendant: One born in the second half of
Mudgara Nadiamsa in Sagittarius ascendant will
be in poverty right from birth and will be a
Purohit of the town (family priest performing
ceremonies prescribed by scriptures). He will be’
restless to have progeny as he will beget children
who will only pass away as they are born. Danger
will oecur to his spouse in his fourth Dasa. He will
in the same Dasa live in foreign lands.

Notes: Mudgara Nadiamsa appears in some
places as Mudgala.

This Nadiamsa extends from 4 deg, 36’ to 4
deg. 48’ of a movable sign; from 25 deg. 12’ to 25
deg. 24’ of an immovable sign and from 19 deg.
36’ to 19 deg. 48’ of a common sign.

These two slokas give effects for birth in
Mudgara Nadiamsa in Sagittarius (19 deg. 36’ to
19 deg. 48’) without reference to any planet as
such. Tersely, the native will never be happy in
terms of financial acquisition, will have children
with short life- spans and his wife will pass away
early.

Since a great deal of prosperity is indicated
for birth in 2nd half of this Nadiamsa vide slokas
1384-1386, we may conclude that the above ef-
fects are for birth in first half of the said Mudgara
Nadiamsa, i.e. 19 deg. 36’ to 19 deg. 42’ in Sagit-
tarius.

1384-1386. First half of Mudgara Nadiam-
sa: Explained now are effects for this part in
Sagittarius ascendant. Some prosperity will be
acquired by the subject in his second Dasa while
abundance of the same will appear in the 3rd
Dasa. In the said Dasa, either the native’s wife or
his paternal grandfather will be endangered.
When Saturn in transit passes through the second
half of Libra or through the sign Scorpio, disputes
with and danger to the native’s near and dear will
strike on the scene. The native will be happy only
after a great deal of agitation.

deals with birth in 2nd half of Mudgara Nadiamsa
in Sagittarius, i.e. the ascendant therein should be
between 19 deg. 42’ and 19 deg. 48’ of arc.

is in a comfortable division one born in former
half of Mudgara Nadiamsa will (initially) be wor-

issues.

fortable division" viz. Navamsa etc. suitable to
Mars. I could not locate a Nadiamsa with the
name Toshana. The meaning of the word Toshana
is anything that gives satisfaction.

There seem to be generally obstacles for
Mudgara Nadiamsa native of former half, in
Sagittarius. Such difficulties will well apply to
second half of this Nadiamsa vide sloka 1380
supra.

1398. Paternal wealth: One of former half of
Mudgara Nadiamsa will be wealthy by paternal

127

sources. His 4th and 2nd dasas will give self-

Notes: For first half of Mudgara Nadiamsa

whereas the current sloka, 1398, indicates the
subject being wealthy through paternal sources.

when the Sun is in the 10th house in aspect to
Saturn. Thus the condition laid down in sloka
1397 applies upto sloka 1404 infra.

1412-14131/2. Cancer ascendant - Cham-
paka Nadiamsa: The native of first half of Cham-
paka Nadiamsa, in Cancer ascendant, will be
aBrahmin, be ever happy and will be the first issue
of the family. He is born near a temple of Lord
Siva, in the Mahanadi region, in a big city, in his
relatives’ house. The street of birth is spread from
north to the south. The house is located in the
eastern corner.

Notes: Champaka Nadiamsa is spelt out as
Chambaka Nadiamsa (in Sanskrit text also).

Champaka Nadiamsa rules from 5 deg. to 5
deg 12’ of a movable sign; from 24 deg. 48’ to 25
deg. of an immovable sign; and from 20 deg. to 20
deg. 12’ of a common sign.

The first half of this Nadiamsa in Cancer
extgends from 5 deg. to 5 deg. 6’ of space.

1414-1415. Other effects: He will be good-

charming eyes, be fortunate, charitable, blood-

## Page 152

red in complexion and will have an auspicious
appearance.

Notes: In the 2nd line of sloka 1414, the
following expression is found which is not added
to the English rendering to avoid confusion.

"Lagnaanthye Chaapaseethage" which does
not clearly convey the condition laid down to give
the said effects. Lagnaanthye means end of
(Cancer) ascendant. Chaapaseethagau means
the Moon in Sagittarius. Dhanurasige replaces
the latter expression in some texts, which means
(some planet) in Sagittarius.

Apparently, the description of the native as
above shall exist if the Moon is in Sagittarius while
birth is in Cancer Lagna’s Champaka Nadiamsa,
in first half.

1441. Father’s prosperity : | During
childhood rrosperity will occur to the father, if

43? to 2 deg. in an immovable sign; anc from 13
deg. to 13 deg. 12’ of space of a common sign.

The Sun is required to be either in Kanthaa
Nadiamsa or in Kamini Nadiamsa of any sign.

1442. Other results: The subject of Cham-

stipulated.

amenable to proper translation. Divi is heaven,
Bhuvi is earth, Asthana is assembly and Kolahala
is uproar.

1455-1464, The Sun-Mars: The subject of
first half of Champaka Nadiamsa having the Sun-
Mars conjunction will be absent on the first day
of the obsequies of his father. During the native’s

lord’s major period (or) in the 7th year, in a city
on sea-shore, in a great, fierce battle, the army of
foe will be destroyed(?). He will wander in many
foreign places, and will cause worry to his father.
His Sacred thread ceremony will take place in
Moon/Jupiter periods. 12th year will cause mar-

nal grand father will be happy (comfortable). His
abode will be endowed with quadrupeds and
grains. He will have travels and be powerful. God-
dess Lakshmi will be ever merciful to him. He will
be endowed with golden ornaments and superior
“obes. In the end of (Moon’s) dasa, he will incur

paternal uncle will have tobe feared. His 21st year
will be fatal to mother. This will cause big difficul-
ties to his father, and expenses on travels. When
Saturn reaches the 8th in transit, the subject will
earn the wrath of the king and his ministers, and
will regret thereby- all these in Mars Dasa, Mer-

1480. Rahu bhukti: The second half of
Rahu’s sub period will cause physical illness and
expenditure. When Jupiter in movement comes
to the 11th house, physical conforts will prevail.
(This should be related to slokas 1476-78 supra.)

Notes: The sub period of Rahu relates tothe
dasa of Rahu as could be seen from the following
slokas.

eet aes eT BYR I

1481. Venus Sub-period: The sub-period of
Venus (in the dasa of Rahu, in case of birth in
Cancer ascendant, Champaka Nadiamsa) will
cause to the native a great deal of fortunes. How-
ever, the native’s youngest co-born (last of the
family) will develop evil thoughts. The native’s
friends and relatives will be destroyed. If Venus is
in "Sathamsa", auspicious effects will follow.

Notes: In this sloka, Rahu dasa, Venus sub-
period, for a Cancer native is discussed. This
sub-period is said to give auspicious effects about
native’s fortunes, but adverse effects concerning
friends and relatives. The last line of the sloka
suggests good results in this respect also,
provided Venus is placed in a certain position.
‘Sathamsa’ is not a meaningful astrological term.
At best it could mean 100th degree or 100th part,
which makes no sense. Maybe it should read
‘Ucchamsa’ - exaltation Navamsa. However, ob-
taining a new meaning using Katapayadi numeri-
cal is not advisable at this point.

1483-1491. Further the dasa of Jupiter will

squabbles. During Jupiter dasa, Saturn bhukti,
three of his sisters will be subjected to troubles.
In the dasa of Jupiter, in his middle age, he will
befriend Brahmins and kings. He will also make
friendship with a Soodra (4th caste) minister and
will gain wealth through royal favours. Through
his younger coborn he will gain gold etc. He will
learn foreign languages, befriend the king and will
gain conveyances. The first half of Saturn bhukti
will only give troubles, but no happiness. Its later
half will confer great happiness. He will gather

1493-1496. Further he will sell things that are

he will perform malignant acts and will also be

wife and will experience infamy on account of his

1497-1499, Kalakoota Nadiamsa: One born
in Kalakoota Nadiamsa, and having the Sun in the
7th Navamsa, will have injuries on privities and
other parts. He will lose his (first) wife in 23rd
year in his (very) youth, and will marry for the
second time in the beginning/end of the 24th year.
After marriage he will follow the path of Wisdom.
Jupiter in Brahmagnanamsa (?) being in an
angle/trine from ascendant Sagittarius will make
one a great yogi meditating on the Supreme Being
who will take to ascetic order due to a family
calamity.

Notes: This Nadiamsa, Kalakoota, should
rise in Sagittarius itself. The Sun should be in 7th
place in Navamsa chart.

Kalakoota Navamsa extends from 0 deg. 36”
to 0 deg. 48’ of a movable sign; from 29 deg. 12’ to
29 deg. 24 of animmovable sign; and from 15 deg.
36’ to 15 deg. 48’ of a common sign.

Jupiter is required to be in the Nadiamsa
entitled in Brahmagnana. We have no such
Nadiamsa enlisted. We have ‘Braahmi’ which
means the personified energy of Brahma
regarded as one of the eight mothers of created
beings, said to attend Skanda. Seeing similarity
in names, the text apparently uses a near-
synonym.

Braahmi Nadiamsa extends from 0 deg, 24
to0 deg. 36’ of a movable sign; from 29 deg. 24’ to
29 deg. 36’ of animmovable sign; and from 15 deg.
24 to 15 deg 36’ of a common sign.

_ Jupiter should be in trine from Sagittarius
ascendant, which needs him to be either in Aries
(0 deg. 24’ to 0 deg. 36’) or in Leo (29 deg. 24 to
29 deg. 36’).

1501-1502. Sivada Nadiamsa: One born in
this Nadiamsa in Sagittarius asceadant will be a
Brahmin, be happy for ever, and will have loss of
elder coborns. Later, he wiil have no after- borns.
He will incur poverty in childhood. His mother
will die soon after the native’s birth due to faults
in delivery-chambers.

Notes: Now Sivada Nadiamsa in Sagittarius
ascendant is discussed. This Nadiamsa extends
from 16 deg. 12’ to 16 deg. 24’ of a movable sign;
from 13 deg. 36’ to 13 deg. 48” of an immovable
sign; and from 1 deg. 12’ to 1 deg. 24 ofa common
sign.

Siva Nadiamsa is another division which
should not be confused with Sivada Nadiamsa.

Vaisya native belonging to the first half of Sama

erotics (one of the eight or ten Rasas, sentiments

is Vishnu) and poetry. He will be skilful in writing
be learned, ingenious, sweet in speech, be
devoted to Gods and brahmins, be capable of
understanding others’ thoughts, be inwardly cun-
ning in disposition, be given to anger, be a pleased
soul, and be endowed with brothers and sisters.

1561-66. Long-living Mother etc.: Should
the 4th lord Moon join Ketu, in aspect to Jupiter
and at the same time beget Gemini Navamsa, the
native’s mother will be endowed will longevity.
Further, he will be honourable while his older
sister will be long-lived and will be auspicious
(will have a long-living husband). One of the
native’s brothers will also have a long life, while
other brothers will destroyed (early) in their
respective Maraka periods. The native will be
troubled by small- pox in the sub-period of
Jupiter in the second dasa. He will also suffer
from indigestion, fever etc. and will incur
Balarishta effects to some extent. During the said
dasa, when transit Saturn is found in Gemini (or)
in the 11th year, there will be some troubles.
Twelfth year will cause loss of father. The 6th lord
Mercury, denoting maternal kinsfolk, being in his
exaltation Rasi with Aries navamsa, should at
birth be aspected by Saturn. In that event, Saturn
in transit in Gemini will cause danger to maternal
kinsmen in the 3rd dasa of the native.

narrating Sundara Nadiamsa of Capricorn ascen-
dant suffer incoherence and lack of meaningful
sequence. Partly these relate to the king of the
country and partly to a native. The following
slokas from 1589 onwards give suitable account
of the same Nadiamsa. Hence the present five
slokas (nine lines in all) are to be ignored

Sundara Nadiamsa is not enlisted which
deals with Capricorn ascendant in this part of the
text. I have however a feeling that Surasundari
was wrongly copied as Sundara. Surasundari
Nadiamsa extends from 8 deg. 48’ to 9 deg. of a
movable sign; from 21 deg. to 21 deg. 12’ of an
immovable sign; and from 23 deg. 48’ to 24 deg.
of a common sign.

Jupiter in exaltation, or in the 5th/9th will earn
fortunes in the middle of his life.

1590-1592. Rahu’s period: If the Moon
rules the 7th house and is placed in the 10th
house, the native will gain wealth through a base
king in the dasa periods of Rahu. He will further

periods (either way) cause danger. In the end of
the dasa of the Moon/Sun, (as the case may be),
the subject will face fear of untimely death and
may even die. If he survives, he will (with this
exchange) not cross 61 years of age, but will ac-
quire pleasures and fortunes.

the three Navamsas, viz. Pisces, Libra and Virga,
the subject in Rahu dasa will visit pilgrim centezs
and temples on festive occasions. In the end of
this sub-period, he will incur physical illnesses
and enmity with friends and close relatives.
Suitable propitiations be done (to surmount the
evils concerned).

1599-16021/2. Trailokya Nadiamsa: The

native of first half of Trailokya Nadiamsa belong-
ing to a movable ascendant will be a Soodra, ever
happy and be the fourth child of his parents. If
the 4th lord is conjoined with Rahu (in the above
case) birth will be in a north-south street, in the
eastern part in a house facing the north. See in
which Navamsa the 4th lord is placed. The house
## Page 165

Deva Keralam ifs

of delivery will correspond to such Rasi, Navamsa
or decanate. Should the ascendant lord be in the
company of a benefic as the 4th lord is with a
malefic, the native will either be born in a town
surrounded by forests, or will dwell in such a
town.

Notes: Trailokya Nadiamsa is
Trailokyamohanakari which extends from 14 deg.
48’ to 15-deg. of a movable sign; from 15 deg. to
15 deg 12’ of an immovable sign; and from 29 deg.
48’ to 30 deg. of a common sign. Some texts
simply call it Mohana Nadiamsa, or Mohita
Nadiamsa.

This part of the text deals with a movable
ascendant.

1623-1626. Second half - Trailokya Nadiam-
sa: Mercury ruling the 9th house, (in case of birth
in a movable ascendant) should be placed in
Aries, with Scorpio Navamsa. Then the father of
the natie of this part of Trailokya Nadiamsa will
have five brothers. The subject will be a devotee
of Lord Vishnu and will look after his parents,
Out of the five paternal uncles, two will be en-
dowed with long lives. In case of birth in first half,
both the paternal uncles (ref. S. 1619 etc.) will be
endowed with comfortable living. If birth be in
first half, the native’s father will have ten coborns
five of whom will be destroyed.

Notes: Second half of Trailokya Nadiamsa
in a movable sign rules from 14 deg. 54’ to 15 deg.
of space. Mercury being in 23 deg. 20° to 26 deg
40° of Aries begets Scorpio Navamsa.

1642-16431/2. Father: If the Navamsa ascen-
dant is Gemini the native’s father will be virtuous
and will have predominant qualities of Mercury.
Further he will be of doubting nature, and will be
adulterous. He will have ten co-borns out of
whom two elders will be long-lived. His sister will
have a diseased daughter. Another daughter (of
the native’s aunt) will be miserable and indigent.

Notes: Trailokya Nadiamsa in Capricorn
does not give Gemini Navamsa. Hence the
Nadiamsa should not be linked here. This only
means birth in Capricorn ascendant with Gemini
as Navamsa. That is the ascendant should be
between 16 deg. 40° and.20 deg. of Capricorn.

Trailokya Nadiamsa will be the third issue in the

veyances. If birth be in the 2nd half of the said

Lord Vishnu’s worship and will be the head of a
colony of Brahmins. He will be fond of Brahmins
following orthodox laws, and will serve a Vaish-

fortunes and will honour Gods and Brahmins. He
would be happy through his progeny, but would
be emaciated (worried) on account of his grand-
children. He would have passed away before the
birth of the subject native.

The father of the subject would indulge in thieving

blame on account of his spouse (ie. native’s

(but) be pleased (soon). He would ever be foolish,
would worship Lord Siva and would prefer offer-

grass (Peethaarchana Parah). He would be
happy. During his advanced age, he would get a
lot of satisfaction through his progeny.

1694-1696. Third Dasa: For a native of
former half of Trailokya Nadiamsa, auspicious
events will be pronounced in the dasa which is
third in sequence. He will further acquire
progeny and abundant wealth and grains. Hap-
piness to younger coborns will come to pass.
Family marriages etc. will occur. In this dasa the
native will have widespread fame (prosperity etc.)
but his father will incur a mix of good and bad
events. During the concluding part of second
dasa (Sampath dasa), the native in question will
be distressed, and a series of deaths of relatives
will take place.

1718-1721. Death - First Half: Birth being
in the first half of Trailokya Nadiamsa will cause
timely death in Saturn’s sub period (Sani Bhuk-
fishu is another, right reading which denotes
Saturn’s sub period.) during the major period of
8th lord Sun. But the same Saturn’s sub period
during the dasa which is the third in order will
cause fear of untimely death for which the wise
should seek (suitable) remedies. Saturn’s sub
period in Rahu dasa will also bring (such) danger.
By donating gingilee, this fear can be overcome.
The subject of former half of this Nadiamsa will
live for sixty-two years. His end will strike when
the Sun is in Aries, or its trine.

1745-1747. Troubles from flies etc: If the
3rd lord (or even the second lord) is in the com-

association, the native will have troubles on ac-
count of flies bees entering in his ears. Mars in
the 2nd house in aspect to or in association with
Rahu causes ulcer in the roots of the ears and
growth of worms. If Jupiter occupies the 3rd
house there will be no disorders of the ear. The
Sun present in the said house will cause ear dis-
orders but will give wealth.

1748-17491/2. Jupiter with the 3rd lord and

testicles, apart from windy disorders. Aquarius
in such a case will give fear from thieves, while
Leo will bring danger through royal decree. A
benefic’s sign as 3rd house having Jupiter-Saturn
will cause great happiness and acquisition of or-
naments of the ear.

Navamsa ruled by Saturn, and malefics in 2nd and

of the ears. This is because in the previous birth
during childhood the native committed theft of

to Lord Vishnu should be resorted to. Mantras
and Japas to please Lord Krishna be performed
through Brahmins, installing the image of the
Lord. Donation of ear ornaments be also done.

1764-17661/2. Should Ketu be in Aquarius in
aspect Saturn and Mars, and be in a Navamsa
owned by Mars, without possessing the aspect of
a benefic, the subject will be deaf. (Alternatively)
he may become deaf in his old age due to windy
blemishes. If Ketu described above is in Pisces
Navamsa (instead of Martian Navamsa), the sub-
ject will be childless but will enjoy Rajayoga and
be happy. Should Jupiter aspect Ketu (who is
placed in Pisces Navamsa), the native will beget
dead children (instead of altogether being child-
less). The same effect of begetting dead progeny
will follow if Ketu placed in Pisces Rasi, aspected
by Saturn, occupies a Navamsa of Jupiter (i.e.
Sagittarius/Pisces). These yogas about progeny
apply to a movable sign assurging.

1768-1770. Ketu in the ascendant, which is
either a movable sign or a dual sign will cause
diseases of the eyes to the native’s daughter. Ifin

diseases of the eyes will be cured early. The ear
disorders referred to above are due to the native’s
using harsh words to a Brahimin, according to
Budha Nadi. To get rid of this sin, dips for three
days in Brahma Teertha (a place of pilgrimage on
the Reva or Narmada River) be taken.

. 1773-17761/2. Assessment of native’s son
(i.e. ‘ progeny) be done through the following: The
lords of Sth, ascendant and the 7th apart from
Jupiter. One born in Pankaja Nadiamsa will have
obstacles in obtaining progeny if the lords of the

Nadi

Sth and 7th are in debilitation. If Venus becomes
the lord of the Putra Aroodha Pada (i.e. Aroodha
pada for the Sth house) and is placed in the 10th
or its trine, counted from rising sign, the same
result will materialise. This will apply only when
the rising sign’s Navamsa falls in Pisces.

Notes: For Pankaja Nadiamsa, please see
notes under sloka 685- 686. From sloka 1775 to
1778, Pankaja Nadiamsa, Capricorn ascendant is
dwelt with.

(a) If Venus and Moon are in simultaneous
debility, the native in question will have obstacles
in begetting progeny.

(b) Venus is lord of 5th. He should also
become lord of Sth Aroodha or Putraroodha.
Being so he must occupy Libra, or Aquarius, or
Gemini to give same effects as at "a" above.

As for condition ‘b’, the Navamsa ascendant
should be in Pisces. This is not possible as
Pankaja Nadiamsa in Capricorn ascendant comes
to Vrigo Navamsa.

This should be interepreted as Venus fulfill-
ing the conditions stated above should also be in
Pisces Navamsa - his exaltation Navamsa, to cre-
ate obstacles in respect of progeny.

This view is supported by Venus being in 5th
house and being in Pisces Navamsa & C bringing
in the picture a great delay in birth of children or
through second marriage, vide sloka 1779-1780
infra,

Apparently this strength of Venus is a dis-
count for progeny in case of Capricorn ascendant.

1813-1815. Kahala Yoga: For a Cancer
Lagna native, Mars in Vargothama Navamsa in
Capricorn, being in the company of Saturn will
produce Kahala Yoga. Asa result, the native will
possess abundant grains, much wealth, scented
articles, garlands and ornaments, and be happy.
He will be blessed with the splendour of the sun.
He will be highly intelligent and radiant.
Valorous, given to anger, firm in disposition, ad-
venturous etc. are additonal effects. He will be
enthusiastic among the four kinds of armies
(using men, horses, elephants and chariots) and
will exhibit ilimitable valour in times of war.

Notes: For Kahala Yoga, see notes under
slokas 1430-14301/2 dealing with Cancer ascen-
dant.

Kahala Yoga is discussed involving thé lords of

1824-1825. Sudha Nadiamsa: One born in
Sudha Nadiamsa of an immovable ascendant,
having its Aroodha in Virgo, will be aSoodra (4th
caste in Vedic terms), be ever happy and will be
the 5th issue of his parents. Or he may be the 6th
inorder. These effects are for birth in the former
half of the Nadiamsa in question. If birth be in
.ae second half, he will be the eldest issue.

Notes: Sudha Nadiamsa ranges thus: From
18 deg. 36’ to 18 deg. 48’ of a movable sign; from
{1deg. 12’ tolldeg. 24 of an immovable sign; and
from 3 deg. 36’ to 3 deg. 48’ of a common sign.

This part of the text discusses Sudha
Nadiamsa. Sudha means nectar, lime. Here the
ascendant should be an immovable one. Oc-
casionally Taurus features in particular.

Vide sloka 1824, the ascendant’s Aroodha
should fall in Virgo. For Leo/Aquarius, the

Aroodha ascendant cannot be Virgo. For Taurus,
Venus in Cancer yields Virgo as Aroodha Lagna.
Similarly for Scorpio, Mars in Aries takes Arood-
ha Lagna to Virgo. Thus by implication, this
particular rule relates only to Taurus and Scorpio
ascendants, and not to the other two immovable
ascendants,

1828-1830. First Half - Seethala Nadiamsa:
If birth be in the first half of Seethala Nadiamsa,
in Taurus ascendant, with Jupiter therein, the
native will be endowed with longevity. He will
possess a symmetric body. For a native of first
half (of the said Nadiamsa), results due for
Jupiter (occupying the ascendant) will material-
ize in full measure. At the time of his birth, the
mother would incur much labour pains. But his
coming into this world will be instant (without any
anxiety). Because of Jupiter being seated in the
rising sign, the child (and the mother) will be
happy and be devoid of infantile evils. In case of
second half, infantile mortality will certainly come
to pass.

Notes: Jupiter in Taurus ascendant which
has Seethala Nadiamsa’s firsthalf will undoubted-
ly endow the native with full life-span which will
not be discounted by any other adverse yogas.
## Page 182

164

For the native of second hlaf, the life-span can be
somewhat affected even though Jupiter resides in
the ascendant. The text clearly states that
childhood will see danger to life-span which can
however be overcome.

Other effects relating to mother etc. apply
equally to both the halves of the Nadiamsa.

1855-1858. Obstacles: For birth in an im-
movable ascendant, see if 5th lord Mercury, being
in the company of Venus, is placed in the ending
part of Libra. In that case, the spouse of the
native will have obstacles in giving birth to a child.
She will have some abortions as well, and conse-
quent health troubles (as the term "Aathuraa"
explains). Saturn in the 5th house, being in the
company of Mars, if found in Gemini Navamsa
(or one of the other three dual Navamsas) the
native will find it difficult to beget progeny. How-
ever, Mercury in addition should be in a degree
on which he is stationary (before/after retrogres-
sion/direction). To overcome this blemish, child-
sacrifice be done. (For obvious reasons, this
remedy should be flatly ignored.) Then the native
will be blessed with two long-living sons and long-
living daughter.

1866-1870. Dasa Periods: The Dasa results
being explained now apply to birth in first half of
## Page 185

Deva Keralam

Seethala Nadiamsa. His third dasa will bring
much prosperity. The fourth dasa will cause af-
flux of wealth. With a prosperous calling, the
native will receive unobstructed inflow of wealth.
During the sub period/s of adverse planet/s, in the
5th dasa, the subject will incur physical ill-health
for which remedies will be helpful. The first half
of the sixth dasa will again give wealth while the
later half will create obstacles to financial pursuits
and will (even) thrust untimely death upon the
native. If the native overcomes this untimely
death due to the merits of his past birth, then the
dasa of 8th lord shall inescapably entangle him in
the jaws of death.

1871-1872. The Luminaries: For a Seethala
Nadiamsa native, the Sun in Karala Shashtiamsa
and the Moon in Nirmala Nadiamsa will ensure a
balance between merits and sins (good and bad
effects). During his mortal journey, he will live a
virtuous life, while in the end, he will attain the
Heavens. Throughout his life, he will live with
prosperity and fortunes.

Notes: The Sun should be in Karala Shash-
tiamsa which extends from 23 deg. 30’ to 24 deg.
of an odd sign and from 6 deg. to 6 deg. 30’ of an
even sign. This is also known as Karaladamshtra,
meaning ‘frightful-teethed’. The planet Moon
should be in Nirmala Nadiamsa, for which please
refer to notes under sloka 847 supra.

1901-19041/2. Nirmala Nadiamsa - First
Half: The father of the native will be sickly. The
subject will be wicked in case of wicked people,
and will reply the cruel by cruel acts. He will be
devoid of paternal happiness. His wealth will be
self-earned. Ifthe 4th lord is in the 9th Navamsa,
he will be skilful in the meanings of Religion and
Philosophy. He will be helpful to all, be endowed
with courage, adventures and fame, be fond of
listening to mythological accounts, be rich and
well-disposed to the poor. He will be endowed

1939, Scorpio Ascendant: The native of
Vipra Kaala of Gada Nadiamsa in Scorpio ascen-
dant, in the Trimsamsa of Jupiter will be blood-
red in complexion. He will have a charming
appearance.

Notes: From here on, Gada Nadiamsa of an
immovable ascendant,including Scorpio is dealt
with.

For Gada Nadiamsa, please vide notes
under sloka 518 supra.

This Nadiamsa in Scorpio falls within the
range of Jupiter’s Trimsamsa. From 10 deg. to 18
deg. Scorpio, the Trimsamsa degrees are of
Jupiter.

1943. Elder coborn: The subject of an im-
movable ascendant having Taurus in Navamsa,
will not have any elder coborn. Due to blemishes
in delivery chambers (carelessness, insufficient
medical care and the like), his sister will die (right
at the time of delivery).

required to be Taurus. Such Navamsa can rise in
case of the other three immovable ascendants, viz.
Taurus, Leo and Aquarius.

With such Navamsa ascendant, one born
among one of the three immovable ascendants in
question will not have any pre-born.

also be noted.

1949-19521/2. Lords of 6th & 12th: Now
about the effects of the lords of the 6th and 12th.
The subject will be troubled by a great disease if
the 6th Aroodha Pada is aspected by ascendant
lord or by Saturn, asthe 10th lordis endowed with
strength. With other major transits being evil and
with the Sun in adverse Rasis, during the currency
## Page 192

174 Chandra Kala Nadi

of the dasa of the 12th lord, the subject will be
inflicted by a serious illness. If he survives, his
wealth will be destroyed. In the sub periods ruled
by favourable planets, the 12th lord’s dasa will
bestow wealth. Depending on favourabie planets
in transit, progress of the native will be on the
increase. Gains through progeny will be more,
and fortunes(?) less. He will be greatly grieved
due to loss of progeny.

Notes: Lords of 6th and 12th respectively
are Mars and Venus. For Scorpio ascendant, if
the Aroodha for the 6th is aspected by Saturn or
by Mars, the native will invite dangerous diseases.
10th lord Sun’s strength (not weakness) is a pre-
condition here.

With such a yoga, the dasa of 12th lord Venus
is said to cause either a serious illness, or destruc-
tion of wealth.

Wealth will however be earned in the
favourable sub periods c: Venus dasa. For Scor-
pio ascendant, favourable planets in general are
Jupiter, the Sun, the Moon and Mars. These four
sub periods in the dasa of Venus will give wealth.

Venus dasa is also said to be a minus point
in respect of progeny.

1954-19551/2. Dasa of 9th Lord: Should the
significator for fortunes be placed in the 11th
house; the dasa of 9th lord (Moon) will enable a
Gada Nadiamsa native to have Agraharas (colony
of Brahmins in olden days) constructed. He will
also earn wealth, grains etc. If the 9th lord is in

Vargothama Navamsa, the dasa of the ascendant
lord will grant excellent religious attainments on
the said native. The sub period ruled by the
planet aspecting the ascendant will be sig-
nificiant (in respect of religious attainments) (in
the dasa ruled by Mars).

Notes: Jupiter is the general ruler of for-
tunes. 9th lord Moon is an additional ruler of
fortunes for Scorpio ascendant. Either the Moon
or Jupiter being in the 11th house will enable the
Moon’s dasa give results specified in the text.

1959-19611/2. Mars dasa: In the dasa of the
6th lord Mars and in the sub period/s of malefic
planct/s, the native will have destruction of
enemics, apart from seeing evils to step-
brothers/cousins. The 6th lord (Mars) is capable
of giving Yoga (i.e. Raja Yoga) if he is in the
company of Sth lord (Jupiter). IfMars is conjunct
Jupiter, then the dasa of Mars will confer great
fortunes, wealth, quadrupeds, birth of children,
sound health and other auspicious effects. Par-
ticularly the sub periods of favourable planets in
the dasa of Mars will give much comforts.

Notes: ° Malefic plancts for Scorpio ascen-
dant arc Saturn, Mercury and Venus. These sub
periods in the dasa of Mars will help the native
succeed over his enemics. These malefic sub
periods will causc harm to cousins and step-
brothers.

However, the time of Saturn’s moving on the
Sth lord's Navamsa position or a trine thereof will
give troubles from enemies (vide sloka 1962-63
1/2 infra).

1964-1965. Sub-periods of Mars and of
Mercury: Inthe dasa ruled by the 6th lord (Mars)
and in the sub-periods of 6th lord (Mars) and of
8th lord (Mercury), the native’s health will
decline due to his kinsfolk being in adversities.
These will occur on the week days which are not
ruled by the lords of the various ascendants
caused by the Shadvargas (six divisions) of the
natal ascendant.

Notes: Shadvargas are Rasi, Hora, Navam-
sa, Drekkana, Dvadasamsa and Trimsamsa. The
week-days denoted by the lords of these 6 ascen-
dants will not prove harmful in the present con-
text. The weekdays other than these will cause
illness to the native during the rulership of Mer-
cury sub period and Mars sub period - both in the
dasa ruled by 6th lord Mars.

1966-1969. The junctions of the dasa periods
of the Moon and Mars will cause distress. Except
## Page 194

the months denoted by transit Sun in the signs

1978. Death of Son: Should Saturn be in the
9th in the company of Mars, while the significator
for progeny, Jupiter, is with Rahu, the native will
incur loss of a son. To overcome this grief,
remedies as prescribed by Sastras be resorted to.
## Page 195

Deva Keralam [77

Notes: Saturn-Mars in the 9th while Jupiter
is with Rahu will cause death of a son. However,
if Saturn in the process obtains Leo Navamsa (i.e.
Saturn in Cancer between 3 deg. 20° and 6 deg.
40’) will not cause such a loss, but the child will be
long-lived (vide sloka 1983 infra).

In case Saturn is not in Leo Navamsa,
remedies as prescribed in slokas 1979-1982 infra
be resorted to.

1979-1982. To overcome such an evil (and to
beget a long-living son), given below are the
details of remedies. Lord Vishnu (or Lord Siva)
should be worshipped with a desire for obtaining
of a son, and a six-day vow be maintained. Im-
mersion (or donation) of an image of Lord San-
thana Gopala be done. Prayer to Naga (Cobra
incarnate) be offered. Dips in sacred waters like
Sethu be done. Siva Linga bejewelled with orna-
ments etc. be given in donation. Then a worthy
son will be born (whol will not incur early death).
A golden image of Lord Surya (i.e. Sun) be given
to a Brahmin on a Monday (Timmamsu = Moon,
who has rays that are not fierce). Worship of such
an image of the Sun will eliminate all diseases
(obstructing birth of a son) and instant results will
prevail. A son so born will be intelligent,
valorous, modest, and skilful in arts. Alternatively
a heavy image of a child be donated following
which wealth and acquisition of a child will occur.

1988. Notwithstanding debility of a planet,
if its dispositor is in an angle, the debility in
question remains nullified. The debilitated planet
turns happy (i.e. becomes auspicious) if its dis-
positor unites with it. Lastly, the planet in debility
proves favourable if it obtains extremely
favourable divisions (in Shodasa Varga).

1994, The conjunction of an exalted planet
with a debilitated planet, devoid of the company
of its dispositor, will be the cause of a Rajayoga.
An emperor is born if (two) planets exchange
their Rasis.

Notes: Mars and Jupiter can join in
Capricorn without Saturn’s position therein, or
they can join in Cancer without the Moon therein.
Similarly the Sun-Saturn conjunction in Aries
should not be shared by Mars in Aries. Nor
should the Sun-Saturn in Libra acquire Venusian
association.

Thus four Raja Yogas are produced by the
company of an exalted planet and a debilitated
planet.

The second yoga given here is wellknown
Parivarthana Yoga.

1997-1998. Ashtaka Varga: Firstly, commit
trinal reduction, then Ekadhipatya Sodhana
(reduction on account of a planet owning two
signs). Multiply the net dots by seven and divide
by eight. If three dots be the remainder, the
native will be wealthy and skilful in speech but will
have limited number of issues. Should Jupiter be
in a fatal degree, the subject’s children will die as
they are born.

Notes: The text does not specify as to which
Ashtaka Varga is dealt with. It relates to Jupiter’s
individual Ashtaka Varga.

After the two reductions, the bindus be mul-
tiplied by seven and multiples of eight be cast
away. The remainder 3 will give skill in speech
apart from a number of children.

Jupiter’s fatal degrees are:

Aries 19 deg,
Taurus 29 deg.
Gemini 21 deg.
Cancer 27 deg.
Leo 6 deg.
Virgo 4 deg.

179
Libra 13 deg.
Scorpio 4 deg.
Sagit 27 deg.
Capri 12 deg.
Aqua 29 deg.
Pisces 19 deg.

These degrees applicable only to Jupiter
should be used in this particular context when the
Sth house is badly afflicted with other combina-
tions required being in existence.

Particularly, the ‘fatal degree’ for Jupiter in
Cancer Sagittarius and Pisces should be handled
with care.

1999-2001. The sub period and sub-sub
period of Rahu will cause physical ailment and
loss of wealth. The dasa which is 4th in sequence
will cause acquisition of abundant wealth. One
will receive uninterrupted wealth and will enjoy
professional progress. In the malefic sub periods
of (Rahu) dasa, the native of Champaka Nadiam-
sa will face timely death. One born in an immov-

have an excellent rebirth. The effects described
in Devakeralam about the 11th lord will bear

2002. Now results for birth in the first half
of Suprabha Nadiamsa in Scorpio ascendant.

Notes: Suprabha Nadiamsa extends thus:
from 15 deg. 36 to 15 deg. 48’ of a movable sign,
from 14 deg. 12’ to 14 deg. 24 of an immovable
sign; and from 0 deg. 36’ to 0 deg. 48’ of acommon
sign.

The first half of this Nadiamsa in Scorpio is
from 14 deg. 12’ to 14 deg. 18’ of arc. Slokas from
2002 to 2012 deal with Scorpio ascendant.

2003-2006. He will be a Soodra (4th caste in
olden days) by birth, be ever happy, born in an
emperor’s family(?), be engaged in deriving fruits
of his work, be strong and be fond of charity and
juices. (Daana Rasa Priyah is not a proper com-
bination meaning: fond of charity and juices.) In
his childhood, he will be miserly. But in his youth,
he will be charitably disposed. He will feed the
poor. He will ever protect many a people. He will
also take care of his friends and kinsfolk. Some-
times he will be given to anger, sometimes forgiv-
ing in disposition. He will be instrumental in
constructing temples, tanks and rest- houses. He
will engage the services of Brahmins in
meritorious acts.

Notes: Birth in an emperor’s family is a
misfit in the present context.

2007-2012. Lord of 9th: If the 9th lord Moon
joins the 4th lord and is angular, counted from the
natal ascendant (Scorpio), the native will worship
Lord Vishnu and Lord Siva. He will be fond of
divine recitations and will have literary achieve-
ments. He will marry a beautiful woman, will join
others’ women, be valorous and be skilful in
poetry, drama etc. He will be learned in
philosophy and be a philosophical teacher as well.
He will be fond of sexual enjoyments and will join
the spouses of other men. He will join women
who are in their monthly periods. In his
childhood, he will be troubled by ulcers, and in
youth he will contract some physical ailments. He
will have falls from vehicles. Through Mlechchas
he will have some worries. He will incur dangers
through sexual contacts in youth, and through
weapons in a battle. In the absence of these
adversities, his prosperity will be obstructed and
the wealth saved by him be destroyed. He will be
a fortunate person, charitably disposed and will
have blood-red complexion with a pleasing ap-
pearance.

Note: Vide sloka No.2007, Bhagyese Lagna
Rasige meaning the lord of 9th in ascendant, is
redundant as "9th lord with 4th lord in an angle"
already appears.

2026-2029. Nirmala Nadiamsa: During the
Sun’s northerly course, coinciding with his transit
in the three signs commencing Aries, the mother
of the subject of Nirmala Nadiamsa will be in
danger. In the dasa that is sixth in sequence, the
native of Nirmala Nadiamsa will incur physical
illness. This will occur in the end of the 4th dasa,
or in‘adverse years/months. One born in this
Nadiamsa in an immovable ascendant will ex-
perience royal wrath in the sub-period denoted
by fifth Nakshatra from the natal Moon, during
the rulership of 6th major period. To overcome
this, suitable propitiations be done. For a native
of Nirmala Nadiamsa, former half, the 6th dasa
will bring danger. If at all he survives, the dasa
ruled by the 8th lord will endanger him.

Notes: Slokas 2026 -2032 are wrongly ap-
pended here. These deal with Nirmala Nadiamsa
of an immovable ascendant. For details of Nir-
mala Nadiamsa, please see notes under sloka
79-80 1/2 supra. In this portion of the text, Nir-
mala and Champaka Nadiamsas are clubbed
together. The reader may carefully assort such
rules without confusion.

ruled by Jupiter. During his journey in this world,
he will perform meritorious acts and in the end he
will go to the Heavens. Throughout life, he will
enjoy prosperity. The effects for Gada Nadiamsa
explained in Deva Keralam will bear truth and
come to pass in actual experience.

2088-2089. Gemini ascendant, being in a

Jupiter will give the following effects: The subject
will be devoted to Lords Vishnu and Siva. He will

Notes: In case of Gemini ascendant, one of
the three dual signs, viz. Sagittarius, Pisces and
Gemini can be Navamsa ascendant in which case
Sura Nadiamsa becomes irrelevant as it takes
Aquarius Navamsa position.

in aspect to Jupiter, while the Navamsa ascendant
is also Gemini.

2109-2110. Mercury in Jarjhara Nadiamsa:
(According to Budha Nadi) Mercury in Jarjhara
Nadiamsa for a birth in Vargothama ascendant
with the first quarter of Gada Nadiama will give
following effects. The subject will be the second
issue of the family, born in a colony of Brahmins,
in the Mahanadi region. The house of birth,
facing the east, will be located in a north- south
spread street.

Notes: The present part deals with
Mercury’s position in Jarjhara Nadiamsa (also
known as Jarjhari) which spaces itself as under:

From 4 deg. to 4 deg. 12’ of a movable sign;
from 25 deg. 48’ to 26 deg. of an immovable sign;
and from 19 deg. to 19 deg. 12’ of acommon sign.

The present yogas are from Budha Nadi.

In view of Vargothama in a common sign,
Gada Nadiamsa should be excluded. They can-
not go together. Hence from slokas 2109-2111,
Gada Nadiamsa to ascend doés not apply.

2143-2146. Progeny: If the Moon, aspected
by Mars, is in extremis, and at the same time
aspects the Aroodha Lagna, the subject will face
hurdles in begetting progeny. One born in
## Page 210

Deva Keralam 193

Jagathi Nadiamsa will only obtain dead children.
After a long interval, through his second wife, he
will obtain progeny. He should recite
Mahamantra installing a deity’s image and read
Vishnu Sahsranama for a myriad times. Worship
as prescribed be conducted regularly. These
remedies will ward off numerous blemishes. And
after a great deal of efforts, he will obtain a female
issue. She will live long.

Notes: The Moon will be in extremis if she
is in the last six degrees of an odd sign, or in the
first six degrees of an even sign.

The Moon so placed should be aspected by
Mars. The Moon should aspect the Arroodha
ascendant. The result is hurdle in acquiring
progeny.

The word "Ayutha" in sloka 2145 means a
myriad or even ten thousand. Vishnu Sahasra
Nama should be recited for ten thousand times,
as a remedy to overcome obstacles in acquiring
progeny.

Another remedy suggested is recitation of
Mahamantra installing the image of a deity. The
deity concerned is not specified. Mahamanitra is:
any very sacred or efficacious text of the Vedas,
particularly a great spell against a snake’s venom.

2151-21541/2. For a Jagathi Nadiamsa birth
in Capricorn ascendant, see if the 7th lord Moon
is in Pisces. If so, the dasa of Cancer (7th Rasi)
will cause troubles. In the dasa of the 6th Rasi
(or) in 24th year, the subject will be much dis-
tressed. The dasa junctions in all cases will be
troublesome. Predict danger to mother when
Saturn traverses the sign represented by the
Navamsa occupied by the ascendant lord at birth,
or a trine thereof; during the currency of the 6th
Rasi dasa, thus, the mother will be endangered.
See if the 5th lord is in an angle to ascendant at
birth. In that case, marriage of a son/daughter
will occur in the dasa of the Sth Rasi.

some important clues from the present slokas.

7th Rasi dasa - troubles.

6th Rasi dasa - distress to native and danger
to his mother.

5th Rasi dasa - marriage of son/daughter.
4th Rasi dasa - happiness.

2159-2161. Gada Nadimsa: If birth is in
Gada Nadiamsa, first one fourth part (Vipra
Kaala), with the 9th lord in the ascendant, know
that the native was a Brahmin in his last birth and
that he will be reborn (after the present birth) in
a Vaidic family. During the concluding part of his
birth as a Brahmana (i.e. in the last birth), he took
to ascetic order following a calamity. As a result,
the next birth will be in a Vaidic family. Saturn in
the company of the 12th lord denotes that the
current native will attain final emancipation, after
the next birth.

2166. Vaishnavite: The 5th lord in Kunda
Nadiamsa related to Saturn by aspect/company,
will be devoted to the Wheel of Lord Vishnu and
be interested in following the codes prescribed
for a Vaishnavite. He will be quite intelligent.

Notes: In ardent Vaishnava circles, a true
and enlightened devotee worships the Sudarsana
(the Wheel held by Lord Vishnu to destroy evils
in the Universe) and Sankha (the Conch called
Panchajanya, with which the God raises His voice
against evils). These two Symbols are held in
great reverence by the Vaishnavites.

In a nutshell, the sloka refers to the native
being a great devotee of Lord Vishnu. This apart,
the position of 5th lord, Mercury, with a connec-
tion with ascendant lord Saturn marks a piercing
intelligence on the part of the native.

2171-21731/2. Effects for father (contd.):
When Saturn in transit comes to the Rasi repre-
sented by the Navamsa tenanted by the ascendant
lord, during the rulership of the 3rd dasa, the
native’s paternal uncle (father’s younger coborn)
will be in danger. After this, the father of the
native will migrate to a country situated in the
south of the place where he will make much ad-
vancement. He will either serve an emperor or
will progress by associating with Brahmins. He
will obtain royal honours and be happy after
eliminating his enemies. Men-borne conveyan-
ces and ornaments will accrue to him keeping him
ever happy.

2174-21751/2. Thread Ceremony & Wealth:
During the 2nd dasa, when Saturn traverses the
sign represented by the 8th lord’s Navamsa at
birth or its trine, the native’s Thread Ceremony
will take place. When Jupiter mov.ng in transit
attains Aries Navamsa, during the rulership of the
2nd dasa, the subject will beget wealth. Jupiter
traversing in Gemini will also increase one’s for-
tunes. The native’s coborns will also be happy
and prosperous. (These apply to birth in Kunda
Nadiamsa, of an immovable ascendant, par-
ticularly Aquarius.)
## Page 213

196

Notes: The 8th lord’s Navamsa, normally
used for death and such other tragic events is used
by the text in the context of Thread Ceremony (or
Upanayana). For immovable ascendants, Jupiter
and Mercury rule the 8th as the case may be.
These two planets are in charge of such Vedic
functions. Venus (another benefic) holds sway
over material functions like marriage.

2176-21771/2. About Father: For a Kunda

Nadiamsa, except in malefic bhuktis, the other

native, and he will be happy as well.

2178-2181. Marriage etc.: According to
other authorities, for a movable ascendant, the
ascendant lord in a benefic’s sign (or in a Rasi of
Mercury) will give marriage in the native’s early
years. In second dasa, this position will enable
him earn wealth. His marriage will be from within
his family circles (or from a family whose head will
be a true pater familias). He will be prone to
second marriage. In the 3rd dasa he will beget
progeny whose education will also commence (in
the said Dasa). The native will be skilful in three
languages and famous for his high degree of
learning. He will be versed in Sanskrit and

Chandra Kala Nadi

Telugu. He will be widely famous in fourth dasa.
In the various sub periods of the fourth dasa, the
native’s prosperity will increase.

Notes: The present three slokas deal with
movable ascendant and not an immovable one.
The lord of a movable ascendant should be in a
benefic’s Rasi, while Venus is in Kunda Nadiam-
sa. This will give the native an early marriage &
C.

2187-21881/2. The native will acquire three

2189-2192. Saturn’s Navamsa Positions: If
Saturn at birth is in a fixed Rasi and fixed Navam-
sa, his transit in a trine thereof will give the fol-
lowing effects to a native belonging to Kunda
Nadiamsa. He will visit a king and will gain a
great progress in work. He will uninterruptedly
enjoy sweet food (or quality food). With the

Fi

pleasure of royal ministers, he will enjoy great
prosperity. Further, he will derive happiness
from coborn. During his transit in Libra, with
Aries Navamsa, or in Aries with Libra Navamsa,
Saturn denotes prosperity to the native’s coborn.
The native will in addition become great, will earn
royal favours, wealth and robes. His brothers will
greatly prosper. This native of Kunda Nadiamsa
will also gain through a foreign king.

2205-2207. One born in the former half of
Mangala Nadiamsa in Aries ascendant, will be a
Soodra (4th caste as per traditional classifica-
tion). He will be ever happy. He will be either
the 7th or the 9th issue of the family. In spite of
this, his elder coborns will be destroyed. One
born in the second half of Mangala Nadiamsa
(Viprakala is a contradictory term in the text and
hence to be disregarded) will be a Brahmin and
be the second issue of the family. There are small
differences in the events mentioned for the
second half of this Nadiamsa.

Notes: Please see notes under sloka 226 for
Mangala Nadiamsa. This part of the text deals
with Aries Navamsa.

2210-2211. Acquisition of Twins: The as-
cendant being in the second half of Mangala
Nadiamsa (in Aries) in aspect to or in association
with Mercury denotes that the native will acquire
twins. The same is the case with the native of first

2213-22151/2. Saturn in Direct Motion:
Saturn in Sudha Nadiamsa placed in the 10th
counted from the Sun, being in direct motion, and
occupying a dual navamsa, denotes a wealthy
father. The native will be black in complexion
and be thin-bodied. He would be poor in

childhood and prosper in youth. He will be en-
dowed with after-borns, be honourabie, bereft of
preborns, will have cwo sisters and be passionate.
Only one of the said sisters will have a long mar-
ried life (while the other would soon become a
widow). If the native’s birth be in second half of
Mangala Nadiamsa, both the sisters will be en-
dowed with long married lives (not becoming
early widows). In case of birth in former half, one
sister will be endowed with longevity (while
another will not be).

Notes: For Sudha Nadiamsa, please consult
notes under sloka 1824 supra. For Aries ascen-
dant, Saturn’should be in the 10th, in direct mo-
tion, not being retrograde. He must also occupy
a Navamsa of either Jupiter or of Mercury. The
present slokas clearly differentiate first and
second halves of Mangala Nadiamsa.

2216-2219. Father: The Sun having Saturn
in the 10th from him while the 8th lord is in the
6th will denote following effects respecting the
father of the native belonging to the first half of
Mangala Nadiamsa. He will be bereft of physical
strength, be gentle, given to anger, but instantly
pleased, will for some time take to bad ways, will
suffer penury, will regret later (for his misdeeds),
will be afraid of committing sins, will honour gods
and Brahnins and will enjoy the blessings of Lord
Siva. He will be fond of Tantrikas, will have only
one brother, and will have limited number of
sisters.

2229-2235. There will be sometimes
Balarishta effects for a native of Mangala
Nadiamsa, former half, if Venus joins the ascen-
dant lord. This will be during the "dasa about to
retrograde". (This expression is faulty). These
effects will come to pass in the end/beginning of
first dasa, or in the first sub period of second dasa.
Due to the past merits of the father, the child will
survive. Performance of Mrityunjaya Japa and
donation of an image of the zodiac will eliminate
Balarishta effects as a hill remains unaffected by
## Page 218

Deva Keralam

lightning. If the native is in the dasas of the
luminaries or of Rahu, prayers be performed,
clothes be donated and recitation of Mrityunjaya
Japa for a hundred times be done. Benefics in
angle/trines will confer a medium span of life.
One will be short-lived if birth is in the first one-
third part of first half Mangala Nadiamsa; and be
long-lived if birth is in the middle portion of the
same Nadiamsa. The life-span will be full if birth
is in the first one-third part of second half of
Mangala Nadiamsa. Long life is denoted for a
subject of middle part of second half.

Notes: "Dasa about to retrograde" should
actually read as first dasa, as Balarishta always
occurs in the first dasa. If the same is however for
a short duration, then it can go to second dasa,
but before the child is twelve. The text also sup-
ports this view.

2272. Timely Death: Either in the end of
first dasa, or in the first sub periods of second

struck by (due) death.

2275. Jupiter in Varuna Nadiamsa for birth
in Chakra Yoga will endanger the father in his

appears after Sloka 2274.)

to be the right part of the text. Chakra yoga and
father’s death have no connection. Hence
’Chakra Yoga’ may be ignored in this context.

Nadiamsa denotes that the native was a Soodra in

equal measure. He will attain the heavens. Ac-
cording to some, he will go to some good world.
The 12th lord in Deva Shastiamsa will give wis-
dom in the end. The effects from Lagna Nadi
narrated in Deva Keralam will bear truth.

2292-2254. In case of birth in second half, the
above result (vide sloka 2291) will not come to

mortality. But in second half, such a fear may

Nadiamsa will be in a forest region, nearby a town

mythological trace). According to some, such a
birth will be near a temple of Lord Siva. The
native of former half of Uraga Nadiamsa will be
lonely, bereft of coborn.

memory). His face will be broad. He will be
honourable and will respect gods and Brahmins.

2305. Rahu in Aslesha Nakshatra: If Rahu
at birth is placed in Aslesha Nakshatra, he will
give following effects: The native will be en-
dowed with wealth, be valorous, and be grateful.

beautiful (Varna also means renown, property
etc.) and will eat anything. He will be ever given
to passion.

2308-2312. Mother's Side: The Moon in the
former half of Uraga Nadiamsa, while the natal
ascendant is in a navamsa whose lord is friendly
to ascendant lord Sun (or in Leo Navamsa itself
as Mitramsa means so) will give the following
effects to a Leo native. His maternal family will
be quite prosperous. If in latter half, the birth
concerned will not destroy mother (early). The
native will have two maternal uncles, one of whom
will have two wives. One maternal uncle will have
many children while the other will be childless.
Birth in former half will cause destruction of
mother in the 2nd dasa. In case of birth in second
half, the (numerous) coborns of the native will
attain prosperity and greatness the difference
being in the increasing order from elder to
younger. (That is, the 3rd brother will be more
prosperous than the 2nd one; the 4th one will be
more prosperous than the 3rd one, and in that
order, the last brother will be the best placed of
all.) The native’s mother will die early in his
childhood if Ketu is connected with Mars by
aspect/association in case of birth in the first half
of Uraga Nadiamsa.

2321-2323. The Moon in association with or
in aspect to benefics will cause prosperity for
in-laws. The parents-in-law of the native will be
endowed with longevity. This applies to birth in
first half of Uraga Nadiamsa. Whereas his bride
will not have her father alive at the time of her
marriage if he belongs to the 2nd half of Uraga
Nadiamsa. His marriage will take place at 15.
18th year will be the year of marriage for birth in
first half, and the native will have both the
parents-in-law alive, (at the time of marriage).

native’s daughter. (The second line of sloka 2337
and the two lines of sloka 2338 are irrelevant and
a mix-up with natal astrology as they describe
famine etc.)

the sloka means: The lord of the ascendant, an
immovable sign, occupying the Navamsa owned
by the 9th lord, will give blood-red complexion
and charming appearance to the native. (This
however applies to Sumathi Nadiamsa in Scorpio

2359-2363. Mother & Maternal Relatives:
The lord of the 3rd house, Saturn, placed in an
angle counted from the ascendant, will cause the
birth of along-living sister to the native of former
half of Sumathi Nadiamsa. In case of the native
of second half of this Nadiamsa, this yoga will give
two sisters. The 4th lord, Saturn, occupying a
dual sign with Aquarius Navamsa will give a long
lease of life to the mother of the native of former
half of Sumathi Nadiamsa. Mars, the 6th lord,
denoting maternal uncles, if found in the 11th
house (Virgo) with Aries Navamsa, denotes that
the native will have two maternal uncles; accord-
ing to some the native will have only one maternal
## Page 229

2\2

uncle. Birth in Sumathi Nadiamsa, former half,
in Scorpio ascendant, with a friendly Navamsa (or
Leo Navamsa, Mitra also means Sun) - as aresult,
the maternal kinsmen will be destroyed. Further
there will be two maternal uncles, out of whom
one will have two wives.

2364-2365. Second Dasa: For a subject
belonging to the former half of Sumathi Nadiam-
sa, the dasa which is the second from birth will
give following effects. Danger to maternal rela-
tives, loss of the wealth gathered by the subject
and grief in abundance. If the ascendant Scorpio
itself becomes the ninth Aroodha Pada (i.e. the
Moon placed in Pisces, for birth in Scorpio), the
native of former half of Sumathi Nadiamsa in
Scorpio ascendant will enjoy comforts (as against
above evils, vide sloka 2364) in the second dasa.

in the 14th year, while the one belonging to the
other half will have his marriage in the 13th year.

2372-2374. The Moon in the 7th house, ...
[some word is missing before "Tathrikone"] in a

Nadiamsa will have two wives while the one
belonging to the first half will have one wife.

Notes: Who should be in trine to the 7th
containing is not mentioned in the text. It should
be Venus as the latter lines suggest.

2375-2376. Family Deaths: The native’s
father-in-law will be endangered if Saturn in tran-
sit is found in the Rasi represented by the Navam-

house, (or) in second dasa of the native. Danger
to maternal uncle be predicted if Saturn in transit
is seen in the last part of Sagittarius, with Scorpio
Navamsa. His mother will be distressed due to
loss of brother at that time. These apply to
Sumathi Nadiamsa native.

2380-23801/2. Progeny: For a Sumathi
Nadiamsa native, see if Jupiter at birth is in the
10th house with a movable Navamsa. In that case,
his transit in the last part of Pisces, or in Aries,
will cause birth of a son. On the whole, the said
natal position of Jupiter will bless the native with
two sons and one daughter, all of whom will be
long-lived.

2381-2383. Abortions: For a native of
Sumathi Nadiamsa, the 4th lord placed in Gada
Nadiamsa will cause abortions to the native’s
spouse. Or she will give birth to dead children.
To overcome this blemish, suitable remedies be
done.

under sloka 518 supra.

Sun’s adverse transits will cause a great danger
(to the native of Sumathi Nadiamsa).

2386-2389. Birth in an immovable sign with
Cancer Navamsa will cause bilious natured body,
and due to imbalances of wind and phlegm, the
native will be troubled by bilious disorders. Due
to distress caused to his friends by him, he will
incur some planetary blemishes. To overcome
these, donation of an image of the zodiac be given.
Single-footed image of the zodiac be got made,
worship of the same in a prescribed manner be
done, names of Nakshatras including that of Ab-
hyit be written on it and be donated to an

astrologer. Following this, the patient wiil
recover.

2390-23901/2. One born in the first half of
Sumathi Nadiamsa will be troubled in the 3rd
dasa, due to sins committed against Lord Siva. As
a remedy for one hundred thousand times
Mrityunjaya be recited before the image of Lord
Siva. Nava Graha worship be done at home.
After these, the native will recover his health and
will experience auspicious results. In the absence
of these remedies, recitation of Mrityunjaya for a
crore times be done in a pilgrim centre dedicated
to Lord Siva and installation of a Siva Linga be
done. Then the native in the grip of bilious disor-
ders will feel relieved.

2393-2395. The Moon in Kutila Nadiamsa
while the 4th lord is in Gada Nadiamsa will cause
happiness to the native of Sumathi Nadiamsa in
his fourth dasa. The 4th lord placed in an immov-
able sign, while the significator for happiness
(Venus), is ina movable sign, the native in the first
sub period of the dasa of the 4th lord will have his
friends destroyed. During this period, the native
belonging to the former half of Sumathi Nadiam-
sa will be physically ill.

Notes: For Kutila Nadiamsa, see notes
under sloka 130-131.

2399-2401. Saturn - Venus: Should the
planet Venus be related to Saturn by way of aspect
or association, the subject will enjoy pleasures, be
liked by the king, interested in treading the path
of virtues and be endowed with wealth exceeding
ten thousand, or even a myriad (gold coins),
Saturn remaining in aspect to or in association
with Venus will give following effects concerning
birth in former half of Sumathi Nadiamsa. The
native will be a wealthy and wise person (or an
astrologer, as the word Gnaani indicates), and a
philosopher. He will be somewhat diseased,
somewhat miserly and be a pleased soul.

2403-2404. Pilgrimage: Jupiter in the 10th
from the ascendant will enable the native have a
dip in Sethu, and he will visit Sethu for three
weeks each time in childhood, youth and old-age.
He will earn abundant religious merits having
dips in the Ganges. These results (about Jupiter)
have been narrated in detail in Guru Nadi.

2405-24071/2. Pisces Ascendant: One born
in the former half of Vasudha Nadiamsa, in Pisces
ascendant, will be a Brahmin, be ever happy, and
be either the third issue or the fourth issue of his
family. Belonging to the Trimsamsa of Jupiter,
the subject will be born in a town near the region
of a great sea. In case of second half of this
Nadiamsa, birth will be in newly built house, near
a river, in an auspicious time with umbilical cord
around the body.

Notes: From hereon, the text deals with
Pisces ascendant. Vasudha Nadiamsa may be
referred to in the notes under sloka 1-2.

and will possess a sturdy body. Birth in first half
of Vasudha Nadiamsa of Pisces, with Scorpio
Navamsa, will give abundant prosperity in youth,
particularly after the 25th year, and the native will
be blessed with the mercy of goddess Lakshmi.

2411-2412. The Moon - Indra Nadiamsa:
Birth in the former half of Vasudha Nadiamsa, as
the Moon is Indra Nadiamsa, will bless the native
with physical charm, intelligence, eloquence in
speech and a beautiful face. He will be fortunate,
charitable and be endowed with Rajayoga (lead-
ing to wealth, prosperity et cetera). He will pos-
sess a complexion which will be blood-red. He
will have a body of medium-build and be short in
stature.

Notes: Please see notes under sloka 1105
supra for Indra Nadiamsa.

2413-24131/2. Jupiterian Trimsamsa: One
born in the former half of Vasudha Nadiamsa (in
Pisces) with Jupiter’s Trimsamsa, will also get
same effects (ie. blood-red in complexion,
medium-build and short stature) and will show
fondness for leading ascetics. He will be eloquent
in speech and will honour gods and Brahmins.
He will be greatly devoted to Lord Siva, be
sacrificing in nature and will be fond of his
kinsfolk.

2414-2416. Paternal Properties etc.: If the
native belongs to the 2nd half of Vasudha
Nadiamsa, the aspect of Mars on to Saturn will
denote the following in respect of the native of
Pisces ascendant: He will be endowed with pater-
nal properties and be quite prosperous. He will
be a fool before wicked, and will be evil to evil
men. He will help all and be endowed with valour
and fame. Mythological accounts will be of inter-

est to him. He will be wealthy and be fond of the
poor.

in her childhood while later on, she will live ina
respectable abode. Another sister will be (per-

progeny. She will have a great disease in her
womb. She will in addition be troubied by

2434-24371/2. For a native of former halt of
Vasudha Nadiamsa, marriage will occur in the
first dasa, in ascendant lord’s sub period, and in
the sub-sub period of 9th lord. If the Sun is in

first half of this Nadiamsa will have two wives.
When Jupiter reaches Capricorn, the father of the
native of former half will be endangered and later
on, his mother will be endangered. This native’s
nuptials will take place when Jupiter reaches the
11th, in the first dasa.

2438-2441. Parental Evils: The Sun in Sagit-
tarius with Aries Navamsa will endanger the
Vasudha Nadiamsa native’s father in Venus dasa,
Ketu sub period. On the first day of the obse-
quies of his father, the subject will not be present.
Either the 22nd year, or the 20th year will cause
danger to father. Mother’s death will take place
prior to father’s. The native will have (wide)
travels (Yaathayaatha denotes going and coming).
These effects are for former half of the Nadiamsa
under discusion.

2442-2448. See if the 10th lord Jupiter is in
the company of the Sun and Mars. Or see if
Jupiter is in either 10th or in the 4th, in aspect to
Mars. Then the effects to occur are: The native
will be ever a lord. He will ever be a pleasure-
seeker and will be highly adulterous. He will be
fond of drama, poetry and music. Eloquent in
speeech, he will speak truth. He will be fond of
scents, garlands and robes. After 12 years of age,
## Page 236

Deva Keralam

he will prosper. In the 16th year, he will obtain
wealth. During the 25th year of age, he will beget
Rajayoga effects. He will join women of many
castes and will befriend whores. He will be spor-
tive at the time of sexual enjoyment if the Sun is
in Kaala Nadiamsa. In the assemblies of
emperors, the subject will be skilful in speech and
will be resourceful of expedients. Lord Siva’s
blessings will enable him achieve even the most
unachievable thing. He will own two or three
hundred thousand (gold coins). He will have
comforts provided by the State and be endowed
with all kinds of wealth and grains. He will join
others’ wives, as the planet Moon does. Other
effects of this yoga are: Intoxicated, given to
sexual lust, and fame swinging up and down.

Note: For Kaala Nadiamsa, please see notes
under Slokas 2494-95 infra.

2481-2483. If the luminaries join in the same
degree (or Navamsa) in the 7th from natal ascen-
dant, they may bring (early) death. Their being
in the same degree will cause poverty and will
make the native an expert in adultery and thiev-
ing. For an ascendant that is Movable in nature,
the conjunction of the Moon with Rahu will cause
penury. If in the process, Rahu does not obtain
his exaltation Rasi, the native will be highly
prosperous. In Sagittarius, this yoga of Rahu-
Moon will cause poverty to a native of Libra
ascendant.

2487-2493. A malefic in the 7th will cause
worries on account of wife. If the 7th lord is bereft
of strength, and be with a malefic, the subject will
have two wives. But he will be worshipped during
his tenure with the king. He will be skilful in
writing and be learned. For birth in Dhruva
Nadiamsa, Saturn occupying the 3rd house, while
the 3rd lord is conjunct Rahu, predict grief on
account of coborn in Saturn’s dasa, apart from
loss of children born to the native. After the 12th
year of age, the native’s father will be endangered.
His mother will be long- lived, while there will be
destruction of her kinsfolk. After the native is 10,
his king will die(?) In his country, famine etc. will
strike. His king will be destroyed when the native
is in Saturn dasa, Saturn bhukti(?). In the 3rd
bhukti of Saturn’s dasa, the native’s son will be
struck by a serious disease and the native will be
endangered through his kinsfolk. Afterwards he
will quit the world. His son will become great and
will prosper through coborn.

2494-2495. Capricorn Ascendant: One born
in Jupiter’s Trimsamsa, in Capricorn ascendant,
with the Nadiamsa entitled ‘Kaala’ will be a Brah-
min, be ever happy and be the eldest issue. His
birth will be in a big village, near Mahanadi, in a
north-facing house, in an east-west street.

Notes: Kaala Nadiamsa rules thus: From 6
deg. 12’ to 6 deg. 24’ of a movable sign; from 23
deg. 36° to 23 deg. 48° of an immovable sign; and
from 21 deg. 12’ to 21 deg. 24 of a common sign.

2522. No Coborn: If Saturn is in Kamala

2524, Saturn: If Saturn is found in the
(Nadi) amsa called Apaampathi the subject will
not be religious, will do others’ jobs, will be a
knower of everything, be virtuous, given to anger,
indolent and a law-breaker.

Notes: Apaampathi is not enlisted in that
name as a Nadiamsa. Apampathi means Varuna.
In that case, Varuna Nadiamsa has been ex-
plained in the notes under sloka 188-189 supra.

Apampathi is also a Sahshtiamsa. This ex-
tends from 6 deg. to 6 deg. 30’ of an odd sign, and
from 23 deg. 30’ to 24 deg. of sn even Shashtiamsa.
In my view, Saturn’s position should be located in
the Shashtiamsa cited, for a subject of
Capricorn’s Dhruva Nadiamsa.

2606-2608. Should the 7th lord, placed in the
ascendant occupy a Shashtiamsa owned by Mer-
cury, the native’s spouse will have abortions and

23e Chandra Kala Nad

will have obstacles in begetting progeny. To over-
come this blemish, religious vows on Sundays be
performed. To obtain an excellent son, donation
of an image of Bala Krishna (1.c. Lord Krishna’s
image relating to His childhood) and (or) an
image of Lord Krishna got spending two gold
coins, on the native’s birth day be done. Follow-
ing these, a long-living son will take birth.

Notes: In sloka 2606, Saumya Shashtiamsa
does not refer to a benefic Shashtiamsa. It re-
quires the 7th lord Mars to be in Gemini/Virgo
Shashtiamsa ruled by Mercury who is the Sth lord
for Gemini ascendant.

will be a pilgrim centre, in a colony of Brahmins.

subject of former half will be born near a temple
of Lord Siva.

2645-2647 1/2. One born in Kamala Nadiam-

anger to be only pleased instantly. If the 7th lord

2648-2651. The father of the native of former
half of Kamala Nadiamsa is described thus. He
will be skilled in the interpretation of internal
sentiments by external gestures, will have a
charming face, be skilful (in general), timid,
bereft of learning and comforts, be crooked in
childhood and will join others’ women, will later
on regret and be afraid of committing (such a) sin
and will follow the codes prescribed by the Vedas.
Now about the native. He will be dark-bodied,
highly intelligent, be ever interested in helping
others, skilful in three scripts (i.e. languages), be
a God-believer, versed in all religions (or human-
laws), be generous, and be friendly to messengers.

2657-2660 1/2. Obstacle to Progeny: The Sth
lord Venus, if in aspect to or be with Saturn,
should be in Pisces with Sagittarius Navamsa.
Then the subject will face obstacles in begetting
progeny. If per chance, children are born, the
native on account of previous sins will lose them.
To overcome such a blemish, worship of Cobra
made of turmeric be done. Also of the image of
Lord Vishnu obtained spending three gold coins.
Propitiations on birth days etc. should be done.
Only then will the native obtain a good and long-
living son. The native of Kamala Nadiamsa will
celebrate the birth of a son when Jupiter traverses
the sign Scorpio in his third round of the zodiac.

ruled by the lord of the 9th, the native’s prosperity
will increase after his 36th year. He will obtain a
son (or will have auspicious functions relating to
his progeny). He will make friends with people
in royal employ. He will attain wealth and become
great. He will gain conveyances and robes.

2664-2667. Third Dasa: The dasa which is
the third from birth will in its first half cause
worries of a great order. In the second half of the
dasa in question, danger to father and the native’s
taking to ascetic order will come to pass. When
the Sun transits the three signs commencing Can-
cer, (particularly) in Leo, and when Saturn is in
retrogression or in accelerated motion, predict
danger to father. In the third dasa, the sub-
periods ruled by Sun, Mars and Rahu will cause
illness to the native apart from loss of wealth. The
ascendant lord in Sagittarius will enable the
Kamala Nadiamsa native follow virtuous and
religious path according to his caste.

careful, learned and will know the thoughts of
others. He will be skilful (in genenral) and will
excel in many languages.

2697-2698. If the 7th lord Venus is in an even
Navamsa, obtaining Mangala Nadiamsa, the
spouse will be blood-red in complexion and the
native will be happy following marriage. He will
be ever blessed with the mercy of goddess
Lakshmi, and will have abundance of grains and
quadrupeds. After marriage it will be wealth and
auspiciousness for ever.

Notes: For Aries ascendant Venus is lord of
the 7th. He should be in even Navamsa (of any
Rasi). Additionally he should be in Mangaia
Nadiamsa (refer to notes under sloka 226 supra).

PGR WATT AAI! 1 2ERS I |

2699. Life-long Fortunes: If Jupiter is in
Pushkara Navamsa while the 10th lord (Jupiter
himself) is in aspect to Mars, the native of Cham-
paka Nadiamsa will enjoy fortune throughout his
life.

Notes: Pushkara Navamsa may be under-
stood thus. If a planet is placed in the Rasi and
Navamsa mentioned below, at one and the same
time, it is said to be in Pushkara Navamsa:

Navamsa

Rasi

Aries Libra
Taurus Pisces
Gemini Pisces
Cancer Cancer
Leo Libra
Virgo Pisces
Libra Pisces
Scorpio Cancer
Sagittarius Sagittarius
Capricorn Taurus
Aquarius Taurus
Pisces Virgo

From the above, it is clear that planets in
Aries/Gemini/Leo/Scorpio/Capricorn/Aquarius
Navamsa are not entitled to attain Pushkara
Navamsa.

2717-2718. According to Bhargava Nadi:

(Aries) and the 4th being in occupation by, or in

Deva Keralam - Book 1 - The most exhautive text book of Nadi astrology, describing many events
based on Nadiamsa (150th part of a Sign) and enlisting many rules unheard of so far. Has Sanskrit
slokas in original Devanagari script with English translation and easy-to-understand notes.

Essentials of Predictive Hindu Astrology - containes best researched editorials, research rules
and over 100 prctical horoscopes selected from the author’s works. Essence of 20 years of devoted
study and a must for every practsing astrologer.

Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra (Part 1 only)

Gospel Book of Hindu Astrology with masterkey to the art of prediction. First time in English
press. Original slokas in Devanagari and English translation with exhaustive commentary.

Saravali - Original by Kalyana Varma. Success ladder and encyclopaedia of astrology. Original
slokas in Devanagari and English translation with exhaustive commentary - 2 Vol Set.

Hora Sara of Prithu Yasas, son of Varaha Mihira - an adorable masterpiece. Original slokas in
Devanagari and English translation and exhaustive commentary.

Garga Hora of Sage Garga. Helps partically to interpret any possible planetary conjunction
irrespective of Bhava and number of planets. English version with about 1400 conjunctions.

Nashta Jatakam (Lost horoscopy) - with Devanagari slokas and English translation. Helps
reconstruct unrecorded birth data.

Doctrines of Suka Nadi Retold. This book reveals Nadi system’s mysteries. Contains thrilling
information. English Version with notes.
